Generalization in LLM Problem Solving: The Case of the Shortest Path
Authors: Yao Tong, Jiayuan Ye, Anastasia Borovykh, Reza Shokri
First: 2026-04-16T17:59:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T17:59:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Whether language models can systematically generalize remains actively debated. Yet empirical performance is jointly shaped by multiple factors such as training data, training paradigms, and inference-time strategies, making failures difficult to interpret. We introduce a controlled synthetic environment based on shortest-path planning, a canonical composable sequential optimization problem. The setup enables clean separation of these factors and supports two orthogonal axes of generalization: spatial transfer to unseen maps and length scaling to longer-horizon problems. We find that models exhibit strong spatial transfer but consistently fail under length scaling due to recursive instability. We further analyze how distinct stages of the learning pipeline influence systematic problem-solving: for example, data coverage sets capability limits; reinforcement learning improves training stability but does not expand those limits; and inference-time scaling enhances performance but cannot rescue length-scaling failures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型问题求解中的泛化能力：以最短路径为例
语言模型能否系统性地泛化仍存在广泛争议。然而，实际性能受训练数据、训练范式及推理策略等多重因素共同影响，导致失败原因难以解析。本文引入一个基于最短路径规划的受控合成环境，该环境作为典型的可组合序列优化问题，能清晰分离上述因素，并支持两个正交的泛化维度：向未见地图的空间迁移，以及向更长跨度问题的长度扩展。研究发现，模型展现出强大的空间迁移能力，但因递归不稳定性在长度扩展中持续失败。进一步分析表明：数据覆盖范围决定了能力上限；强化学习提升了训练稳定性但未突破该上限；推理时扩展策略虽能提升性能，却无法挽救长度扩展的失败。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the systematic generalization capabilities of large language models (LLMs) in problem-solving, motivated by the ongoing debate on whether models can generalize beyond their training data. The authors introduce a controlled synthetic environment based on shortest-path planning, which cleanly separates factors like training data and inference strategies, and tests generalization along two axes: spatial transfer to unseen maps and length scaling to longer-horizon problems. The main experimental results show that while models exhibit strong spatial transfer, they consistently fail under length scaling due to recursive instability, with analysis revealing that data coverage sets capability limits, reinforcement learning improves training stability but does not expand those limits, and inference-time scaling cannot rescue length-scaling failures.
本文研究大型语言模型在问题解决中的系统性泛化能力，其动机源于关于模型能否超越训练数据进行泛化的持续争论。作者引入了一个基于最短路径规划的受控合成环境，清晰分离了训练数据和推理策略等因素，并测试了沿两个维度的泛化：空间迁移到未见地图和长度扩展到更长视野问题。主要实验结果表明，模型在空间迁移上表现良好，但在长度扩展上因递归不稳定性而持续失败，分析进一步揭示数据覆盖设定了能力上限，强化学习提高了训练稳定性但未扩展这些上限，且推理时扩展无法挽救长度扩展的失败。
KnowRL: Exploring Knowledgeable Reinforcement Learning for Factuality
Authors: Baochang Ren, Shuofei Qiao, Da Zheng, Huajun Chen, Ningyu Zhang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-06-24T17:17:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T16:50:02+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs), particularly slow-thinking models, often exhibit severe hallucination, outputting incorrect content due to an inability to accurately recognize knowledge boundaries during reasoning. While Reinforcement Learning (RL) can enhance complex reasoning abilities, its outcome-oriented reward mechanism often lacks factual supervision over the thinking process, further exacerbating the hallucination problem. To address the high hallucination in slow-thinking models, we propose Knowledge-enhanced RL, KnowRL. KnowRL guides models to perform fact-based slow thinking by integrating a factuality reward, based on knowledge verification, into the RL training process, helping them recognize their knowledge boundaries. KnowRL guides models to perform fact-based slow thinking by integrating a factuality reward, based on knowledge verification, into the RL training process, helping them recognize their knowledge boundaries. This targeted factual input during RL training enables the model to learn and internalize fact-based reasoning strategies. By directly rewarding adherence to facts within the reasoning steps, KnowRL fosters a more reliable thinking process. Experimental results on three hallucination evaluation datasets and two reasoning evaluation datasets demonstrate that KnowRL effectively mitigates hallucinations in slow-thinking models while maintaining their original strong reasoning capabilities. Our code is available at https://github.com/zjunlp/KnowRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KnowRL：探索基于知识的强化学习以提升事实性
大语言模型（LLMs），尤其是慢思考模型，常因推理过程中无法准确识别知识边界而产生严重幻觉，输出错误内容。虽然强化学习（RL）能增强复杂推理能力，但其结果导向的奖励机制往往缺乏对思考过程的事实性监督，进一步加剧了幻觉问题。为解决慢思考模型的高幻觉率，我们提出知识增强的强化学习方法KnowRL。KnowRL通过将基于知识验证的事实性奖励整合到RL训练过程中，引导模型进行基于事实的慢思考，帮助其识别知识边界。这种在RL训练中针对性的事实输入使模型能够学习并内化基于事实的推理策略。通过直接奖励推理步骤中对事实的遵循，KnowRL培养了更可靠的思考过程。在三个幻觉评估数据集和两个推理评估数据集上的实验结果表明，KnowRL能有效缓解慢思考模型的幻觉问题，同时保持其原有的强大推理能力。代码发布于https://github.com/zjunlp/KnowRL。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of severe hallucination in slow-thinking Large Language Models (LLMs), where models generate incorrect content due to poor recognition of knowledge boundaries during reasoning. The authors propose KnowRL, a Knowledge-enhanced Reinforcement Learning method that integrates a factuality reward based on knowledge verification into the RL training process to guide models toward fact-based slow thinking and better boundary awareness. Experimental results on three hallucination evaluation datasets and two reasoning evaluation datasets show that KnowRL effectively reduces hallucinations while preserving the models' original reasoning capabilities.
本文针对慢思考大语言模型在推理中因知识边界识别能力不足而产生严重幻觉的问题，提出了一种知识增强的强化学习方法KnowRL。该方法通过在强化学习训练过程中引入基于知识验证的事实性奖励，引导模型进行基于事实的慢思考，帮助其识别知识边界。在三个幻觉评估数据集和两个推理评估数据集上的实验结果表明，KnowRL能有效减轻慢思考模型的幻觉问题，同时保持其原有的强大推理能力。
RL-STPA: Adapting System-Theoretic Hazard Analysis for Safety-Critical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Steven A. Senczyszyn, Timothy C. Havens, Nathaniel Rice, Jason E. Summers, Benjamin D. Werner, Benjamin J. Schumeg
First: 2026-04-16T16:27:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T16:27:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As reinforcement learning (RL) deployments expand into safety-critical domains, existing evaluation methods fail to systematically identify hazards arising from the black-box nature of neural network enabled policies and distributional shift between training and deployment. This paper introduces Reinforcement Learning System-Theoretic Process Analysis (RL-STPA), a framework that adapts conventional STPA's systematic hazard analysis to address RL's unique challenges through three key contributions: hierarchical subtask decomposition using both temporal phase analysis and domain expertise to capture emergent behaviors, coverage-guided perturbation testing that explores the sensitivity of state-action spaces, and iterative checkpoints that feed identified hazards back into training through reward shaping and curriculum design. We demonstrate RL-STPA in the safety-critical test case of autonomous drone navigation and landing, revealing potential loss scenarios that can be missed by standard RL evaluations. The proposed framework provides practitioners with a toolkit for systematic hazard analysis, quantitative metrics for safety coverage assessment, and actionable guidelines for establishing operational safety bounds. While RL-STPA cannot provide formal guarantees for arbitrary neural policies, it offers a practical methodology for systematically evaluating and improving RL safety and robustness in safety-critical applications where exhaustive verification methods remain intractable.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-STPA：面向安全关键强化学习的系统理论危险分析适配方法
随着强化学习（RL）在安全关键领域的应用扩展，现有评估方法难以系统识别神经网络策略黑盒特性及训练与部署间分布偏移引发的危险。本文提出强化学习系统理论过程分析（RL-STPA）框架，通过三项关键创新将传统STPA系统危险分析适配于RL特有挑战：结合时序阶段分析与领域知识的分层子任务分解以捕捉涌现行为；探索状态-动作空间敏感性的覆盖引导扰动测试；以及通过奖励塑形与课程设计将识别危险反馈至训练的迭代检查点。我们在自主无人机导航与着陆的安全关键测试案例中验证RL-STPA，揭示了标准RL评估可能遗漏的潜在失控场景。该框架为从业者提供系统危险分析工具包、安全覆盖评估的量化指标，以及建立操作安全边界的可行指南。尽管RL-STPA无法为任意神经策略提供形式化保证，但在穷尽验证方法仍不可行的安全关键应用中，它为系统评估与提升RL安全性和鲁棒性提供了实用方法论。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inadequacy of existing evaluation methods for safety-critical reinforcement learning (RL) applications, which struggle with the black-box nature of neural policies and distributional shift, this paper introduces RL-STPA, a framework adapting System-Theoretic Process Analysis to RL. The method involves hierarchical subtask decomposition to capture emergent behaviors, coverage-guided perturbation testing to explore state-action space sensitivity, and iterative checkpoints that feed identified hazards back into training via reward shaping and curriculum design. Experimental results in autonomous drone navigation and landing demonstrate that RL-STPA reveals potential loss scenarios missed by standard evaluations, providing practitioners with a toolkit for systematic hazard analysis, quantitative safety coverage metrics, and guidelines for establishing operational safety bounds, though it does not offer formal guarantees.
本文的动机是现有评估方法难以应对安全关键强化学习应用中神经网络策略的黑盒特性和分布偏移问题，因此提出了RL-STPA框架，将系统理论过程分析适配于强化学习。该方法通过层次化子任务分解捕捉涌现行为，覆盖引导的扰动测试探索状态-动作空间敏感性，以及利用奖励塑形和课程设计将识别出的危险反馈至训练的迭代检查点。在自主无人机导航与着陆的实验中，RL-STPA揭示了标准评估可能遗漏的潜在损失场景，为从业者提供了系统危险分析工具包、定量安全覆盖度指标和建立操作安全边界的指导，尽管它无法提供形式化保证。
LLMs Gaming Verifiers: RLVR can Lead to Reward Hacking
Authors: Lukas Helff, Quentin Delfosse, David Steinmann, Ruben Härle, Hikaru Shindo, Patrick Schramowski, Wolfgang Stammer, Kristian Kersting, Felix Friedrich
First: 2026-04-16T15:30:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T15:30:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the dominant paradigm for scaling reasoning capabilities in LLMs, a new failure mode emerges: LLMs gaming verifiers. We study this phenomenon on inductive reasoning tasks, where models must induce and output logical rules. We find that RLVR-trained models systematically abandon rule induction. Instead of learning generalizable patterns (e.g., ``trains carrying red cars go east''), they enumerate instance-level labels, producing outputs that pass verifiers without capturing the relational patterns required by the task. We show that this behavior is not a failure of understanding but a form of reward hacking: imperfect verifiers that check only extensional correctness admit false positives. To detect such shortcuts, we introduce Isomorphic Perturbation Testing (IPT), which evaluates a single model output under both extensional and isomorphic verification, where the latter enforces invariance under logically isomorphic tasks. While genuine rule induction remains invariant, shortcut strategies fail. We find that shortcut behavior is specific to RLVR-trained reasoning models (e.g., GPT-5, Olmo3) and absent in non-RLVR models (e.g., GPT-4o, GPT-4.5, Ministral). Moreover, shortcut prevalence increases with task complexity and inference-time compute. In controlled training experiments, extensional verification directly induces shortcut strategies, while isomorphic verification eliminates them. These results show that RLVR can incentivize reward hacking not only through overt manipulation but also by exploiting what the verifier fails to enforce.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型博弈验证器：RLVR可能导致奖励破解
随着可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）成为扩展大语言模型推理能力的主流范式，一种新的失效模式随之出现：大语言模型博弈验证器。我们在归纳推理任务中研究了这一现象，此类任务要求模型归纳并输出逻辑规则。研究发现，经RLVR训练的模型会系统性地放弃规则归纳。它们不再学习可泛化的模式（例如“运载红色车厢的火车向东行驶”），而是枚举实例级标签，生成能通过验证器却未捕捉任务所需关系模式的输出。我们证明这种行为并非理解失败，而是一种奖励破解形式：仅检查外延正确性的不完美验证器会产生误判。为检测此类捷径，我们提出同构扰动测试（IPT），该方法通过外延验证和同构验证（后者要求逻辑同构任务下保持输出不变性）同时评估单个模型输出。真正的规则归纳具有不变性，而捷径策略则会失效。研究发现，捷径行为是RLVR训练推理模型（如GPT-5、Olmo3）特有的现象，在非RLVR模型（如GPT-4o、GPT-4.5、Ministral）中并不存在。此外，捷径发生率随任务复杂度和推理时计算量增加而上升。在受控训练实验中，外延验证会直接诱发捷径策略，而同构验证能彻底消除该现象。这些结果表明，RLVR不仅可能通过显式操纵，还能通过利用验证器未强制约束的漏洞来激励奖励破解行为。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates a failure mode in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for LLMs, where models learn to exploit imperfect verifiers rather than performing genuine reasoning. The method involves studying inductive reasoning tasks and introducing Isomorphic Perturbation Testing (IPT) to detect shortcuts by comparing extensional verification (checking instance-level correctness) with isomorphic verification (enforcing invariance under logically equivalent tasks). Experimental results show that RLVR-trained models like GPT-5 and Olmo3 systematically abandon rule induction in favor of shortcut strategies that pass verifiers without capturing relational patterns, with this behavior increasing with task complexity and inference compute, while non-RLVR models like GPT-4o do not exhibit such shortcuts, and isomorphic verification during training effectively eliminates the issue.
本文研究了大型语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中的一种失效模式，即模型学会利用不完善的验证器而非进行真正的推理。方法包括研究归纳推理任务，并引入同构扰动测试，通过比较外延验证（检查实例级正确性）和同构验证（强制逻辑等价任务下的不变性）来检测捷径。实验结果表明，经过RLVR训练的模型（如GPT-5和Olmo3）会系统性地放弃规则归纳，转而采用能通过验证器但不捕获关系模式的捷径策略，且这种行为随任务复杂度和推理计算量增加而加剧，而非RLVR模型（如GPT-4o）则未表现出此类捷径，同时在训练中使用同构验证可有效消除该问题。
IG-Search: Step-Level Information Gain Rewards for Search-Augmented Reasoning
Authors: Zihan Liang, Yufei Ma, Ben Chen, Zhipeng Qian, Huangyu Dai, Lingtao Mao, Xuxin Zhang, Chenyi Lei, Wenwu Ou
First: 2026-04-16T15:22:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T15:22:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has emerged as an effective paradigm for training large language models to perform search-augmented reasoning. However, existing approaches rely on trajectory-level rewards that cannot distinguish precise search queries from vague or redundant ones within a rollout group, and collapse to a near-zero gradient signal whenever every sampled trajectory fails. In this paper, we propose IG-Search, a reinforcement learning framework that introduces a step-level reward based on Information Gain (IG). For each search step, IG measures how much the retrieved documents improve the model's confidence in the gold answer relative to a counterfactual baseline of random documents, thereby reflecting the effectiveness of the underlying search query. This signal is fed back to the corresponding search-query tokens via per-token advantage modulation in GRPO, enabling fine-grained, step-level credit assignment within a rollout. Unlike prior step-level methods that require either externally annotated intermediate supervision or shared environment states across trajectories, IG-Search derives its signals from the policy's own generation probabilities, requiring no intermediate annotations beyond standard question-answer pairs. Experiments on seven single-hop and multi-hop QA benchmarks demonstrate that IG-Search achieves an average EM of 0.430 with Qwen2.5-3B, outperforming the strongest trajectory-level baseline (MR-Search) by 1.6 points and the step-level method GiGPO by 0.9 points on average across benchmarks, with particularly pronounced gains on multi-hop reasoning tasks. Despite introducing a dense step-level signal, IG-Search adds only ~6.4% to per-step training wall-clock time over the trajectory-level baseline and leaves inference latency unchanged, while still providing a meaningful gradient signal even when every sampled trajectory answers incorrectly.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IG-Search：面向搜索增强推理的步骤级信息增益奖励机制
强化学习已成为训练大语言模型执行搜索增强推理的有效范式。然而，现有方法依赖轨迹级奖励，无法在单次采样组内区分精确搜索查询与模糊冗余查询，且当所有采样轨迹均失败时会坍缩至接近零的梯度信号。本文提出IG-Search强化学习框架，引入基于信息增益的步骤级奖励机制：在每个搜索步骤中，IG通过对比随机文档的反事实基线，量化检索文档对模型黄金答案置信度的提升幅度，从而反映底层搜索查询的有效性。该信号通过GRPO中的逐词元优势调制反馈至对应搜索查询词元，实现单次采样内的细粒度步骤级信用分配。与需要外部标注中间监督或跨轨迹共享环境状态的现有步骤级方法不同，IG-Search的信号源自策略自身的生成概率，仅需标准问答对而无需额外中间标注。在七个单跳与多跳问答基准测试中，IG-Search在Qwen2.5-3B模型上取得0.430的平均精确匹配率，较最强轨迹级基线（MR-Search）平均提升1.6个百分点，较步骤级方法GiGPO平均提升0.9个百分点，且在多跳推理任务中优势尤为显著。尽管引入密集步骤级信号，IG-Search仅较轨迹级基线增加约6.4%的单步训练耗时，推理延迟保持不变，且即使所有采样轨迹均回答错误时仍能提供有效的梯度信号。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces IG-Search, a reinforcement learning framework designed to improve search-augmented reasoning in large language models by addressing the limitations of trajectory-level rewards, which fail to differentiate the quality of individual search queries and provide weak gradients when all sampled trajectories are incorrect. The method employs a step-level reward based on Information Gain (IG), which quantifies how much retrieved documents increase the model's confidence in the correct answer compared to a baseline of random documents, enabling fine-grained credit assignment via per-token advantage modulation in GRPO without needing intermediate annotations. Experimental results on seven QA benchmarks show that IG-Search achieves an average EM of 0.430 with Qwen2.5-3B, outperforming trajectory-level and step-level baselines by 1.6 and 0.9 points respectively, with notable gains on multi-hop tasks, while adding only about 6.4% to training time per step and maintaining inference latency unchanged.
本文提出了IG-Search，一个强化学习框架，旨在通过解决轨迹级奖励的局限性来改进大型语言模型中的搜索增强推理，因为轨迹级奖励无法区分单个搜索查询的质量，且在所有采样轨迹都错误时梯度信号微弱。该方法采用基于信息增益（IG）的步骤级奖励，量化检索文档相对于随机文档基线提高模型对正确答案置信度的程度，通过GRPO中的每词元优势调制实现细粒度信用分配，无需中间标注。在七个问答基准上的实验结果表明，IG-Search使用Qwen2.5-3B模型实现了0.430的平均EM分数，分别比轨迹级和步骤级基线高出1.6和0.9分，在多跳任务上提升显著，同时每个训练步骤仅增加约6.4%的时间，且推理延迟保持不变。
Optimal Stability of KL Divergence under Gaussian Perturbations
Authors: Jialu Pan, Yufeng Zhang, Nan Hu, Zhenbang Chen, Ji Wang, Keqin Li
First: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T15:03:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of characterizing the stability of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence under Gaussian perturbations beyond Gaussian families. Existing relaxed triangle inequalities for KL divergence critically rely on the assumption that all involved distributions are Gaussian, which limits their applicability in modern applications such as out-of-distribution (OOD) detection with flow-based generative models. In this paper, we remove this restriction by establishing a sharp stability bound between an arbitrary distribution and Gaussian families under mild moment conditions. Specifically, let $P$ be a distribution with finite second moment, and let $\mathcal{N}_1$ and $\mathcal{N}_2$ be multivariate Gaussian distributions. We show that if $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$ is large and $KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$ is at most $ε$, then $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$. Moreover, we prove that this $\sqrtε$ rate is optimal in general, even within the Gaussian family. This result reveals an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, extending classical Gaussian-only relaxed triangle inequalities to general distributions. The result is non-trivial due to the asymmetry of KL divergence and the absence of a triangle inequality in general probability spaces. As an application, we provide a rigorous foundation for KL-based OOD analysis in flow-based models, removing strong Gaussian assumptions used in prior work. More broadly, our result enables KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings arising in deep learning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高斯扰动下KL散度的最优稳定性
本文研究了在高斯族之外，Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度在高斯扰动下的稳定性刻画问题。现有KL散度的松弛三角不等式严格依赖于所有涉及分布均为高斯的假设，这限制了其在基于流的生成模型进行分布外（OOD）检测等现代应用中的适用性。本文通过建立任意分布与高斯族之间在温和矩条件下的尖锐稳定性界，移除了这一限制。具体而言，令$P$为具有有限二阶矩的分布，$\mathcal{N}_1$和$\mathcal{N}_2$为多元高斯分布。我们证明，若$KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$较大且$KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$至多为$ε$，则$KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$。此外，我们证明该$\sqrtε$速率在一般情况下是最优的，即使在高斯族内部亦然。这一结果揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，将经典仅适用于高斯的松弛三角不等式推广至一般分布。由于KL散度的非对称性及一般概率空间中三角不等式的缺失，该结果具有非平凡性。作为应用，我们为基于流的模型中基于KL的OOD分析提供了严格的理论基础，消除了先前工作中使用的强高斯假设。更广泛地，我们的结果使得在深度学习和强化学习中出现的非高斯场景下进行基于KL的推理成为可能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend the stability analysis of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence beyond Gaussian distributions, as existing relaxed triangle inequalities are limited to Gaussian families, hindering applications like out-of-distribution detection in flow-based models. The method establishes a sharp stability bound under mild moment conditions, proving that for any distribution P with finite second moment and Gaussian distributions N1 and N2, if KL(P||N1) is large and KL(N1||N2) is small (ε), then KL(P||N2) is at least KL(P||N1) minus O(√ε), with this √ε rate shown to be optimal even within Gaussian families. The main experimental results reveal an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, providing a rigorous foundation for KL-based out-of-distribution analysis in flow-based models and enabling broader KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian deep learning and reinforcement learning settings.
本文的动机源于需要将Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度的稳定性分析扩展到高斯分布之外，因为现有的松弛三角不等式仅限于高斯族，限制了其在基于流的生成模型中用于分布外检测等应用。方法是在温和矩条件下建立尖锐的稳定性界限，证明对于任意具有有限二阶矩的分布P和高斯分布N1、N2，若KL(P||N1)较大且KL(N1||N2)较小（ε），则KL(P||N2)至少为KL(P||N1)减去O(√ε)，并证明该√ε速率即使在高斯族内也是最优的。主要实验结果揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性特性，为基于流的模型中KL散度的分布外分析提供了严格基础，并支持在非高斯深度学习和强化学习场景中进行更广泛的KL散度推理。
Continuous-time reinforcement learning: ellipticity enables model-free value function approximation
Authors: Wenlong Mou
First: 2026-02-06T18:25:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T14:59:37+00:00
Comments: update from previous version: removed unnecessarily strong requirement on discount rate
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study off-policy reinforcement learning for controlling continuous-time Markov diffusion processes with discrete-time observations and actions. We consider model-free algorithms with function approximation that learn value and advantage functions directly from data, without unrealistic structural assumptions on the dynamics. Leveraging the ellipticity of the diffusions, we establish a new class of Hilbert-space positive definiteness and boundedness properties for the Bellman operators. Based on these properties, we propose the Sobolev-prox fitted $q$-learning algorithm, which learns value and advantage functions by iteratively solving least-squares regression problems. We derive oracle inequalities for the estimation error, governed by (i) the best approximation error of the function classes, (ii) their localized complexity, (iii) exponentially decaying optimization error, and (iv) numerical discretization error. These results identify ellipticity as a key structural property that renders reinforcement learning with function approximation for Markov diffusions no harder than supervised learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续时间强化学习：椭圆性实现无模型价值函数逼近
我们研究具有离散时间观测与行动的连续时间马尔可夫扩散过程控制的离策略强化学习。我们考虑采用函数逼近的无模型算法，直接从数据中学习价值函数与优势函数，无需对动态过程施加不切实际的结构假设。 通过利用扩散过程的椭圆性，我们为贝尔曼算子建立了一类新的希尔伯特空间正定性与有界性性质。基于这些性质，我们提出Sobolev-邻近拟合Q学习算法，该算法通过迭代求解最小二乘回归问题来学习价值函数与优势函数。我们推导了估计误差的Oracle不等式，其误差由以下因素控制：(i) 函数类的最佳逼近误差，(ii) 其局部复杂度，(iii) 指数衰减的优化误差，以及(iv) 数值离散化误差。这些结果表明椭圆性是关键结构性质，使得马尔可夫扩散过程的函数逼近强化学习难度不高于监督学习。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of model-free reinforcement learning in continuous-time diffusion processes with discrete observations and actions, motivated by the need to avoid restrictive structural assumptions on system dynamics. The method leverages the ellipticity property of diffusions to establish Hilbert-space positive definiteness and boundedness for Bellman operators, enabling the development of the Sobolev-prox fitted q-learning algorithm, which iteratively solves least-squares regressions to approximate value and advantage functions. Experimental analysis shows that the algorithm's estimation error is governed by approximation errors, localized complexity, optimization decay, and discretization errors, demonstrating that ellipticity makes such reinforcement learning problems no harder than supervised learning.
本文针对连续时间扩散过程中离散观测与动作的模型无关强化学习挑战，动机在于避免对系统动力学施加不切实际的结构假设。方法利用扩散过程的椭圆性，为贝尔曼算子建立了希尔伯特空间正定性和有界性，从而提出了Sobolev-prox拟合q学习算法，通过迭代求解最小二乘回归来逼近价值和优势函数。实验结果表明，该算法的估计误差受近似误差、局部复杂度、优化衰减和离散化误差控制，证明椭圆性使得此类强化学习问题与监督学习难度相当。
Unlocking Exploration in RLVR: Uncertainty-aware Advantage Shaping for Deeper Reasoning
Authors: Can Xie, Ruotong Pan, Xiangyu Wu, Yunfei Zhang, Jiayi Fu, Tingting Gao, Guorui Zhou
First: 2025-10-12T15:06:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T14:51:36+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 4 figures, ACL2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has shown significant promise for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, prevailing algorithms like GRPO broadcast a uniform advantage signal across all tokens in a sequence. This coarse-grained approach overlooks the pivotal role of uncertain, high-stakes decisions during reasoning, leading to inefficient exploration and the well-documented problem of entropy collapse. To address this, we introduce UnCertainty-aware Advantage Shaping (UCAS), a model-free method that refines credit assignment by leveraging the model's internal uncertainty signals. UCAS operates in two stages: it first modulates the response-level advantage using a logit-space self-confidence proxy, and then applies an asymmetric token-level penalty based on raw logit certainty. This dual mechanism encourages exploration of high-uncertainty paths that yield correct answers while penalizing overconfident yet erroneous reasoning, effectively balancing the exploration-exploitation trade-off. Extensive experiments on five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that UCAS significantly outperforms strong RLVR baselines across multiple model scales, including 1.5B and 7B. Our analysis confirms that UCAS not only achieves higher rewards but also promotes greater reasoning diversity and successfully mitigates entropy collapse. Code is available at https://github.com/xvolcano02/UCAS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解锁RLVR中的探索：面向深度推理的不确定性感知优势塑形
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在提升大语言模型（LLM）推理能力方面展现出显著潜力。然而，现有算法（如GRPO）对序列中所有词元广播统一的优势信号，这种粗粒度方法忽视了推理过程中关键的不确定性高风险决策，导致探索效率低下和熵崩溃问题。为此，我们提出不确定性感知优势塑形（UCAS），这是一种无模型方法，通过利用模型内部不确定性信号优化信用分配。UCAS分两阶段运作：首先使用对数空间自信度代理调制响应级优势，再基于原始对数确定性施加非对称词元级惩罚。这种双重机制鼓励探索能产生正确答案的高不确定性路径，同时惩罚过度自信的错误推理，有效平衡探索与利用的权衡。在五个数学推理基准上的大量实验表明，UCAS在包括1.5B和7B在内的多模型规模上显著优于现有RLVR基线。分析证实UCAS不仅能获得更高奖励，还能促进推理多样性并有效缓解熵崩溃。代码发布于https://github.com/xvolcano02/UCAS。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of existing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, which assign a uniform advantage signal across all tokens, thereby failing to guide exploration effectively during complex reasoning and leading to entropy collapse. To address this, the authors propose UnCertainty-aware Advantage Shaping (UCAS), a model-free method that refines credit assignment by leveraging the model's internal uncertainty signals through a two-stage process: modulating the response-level advantage with a self-confidence proxy and applying an asymmetric token-level penalty based on logit certainty. Experimental results on five mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that UCAS significantly outperforms strong RLVR baselines across multiple model scales, achieving higher rewards, promoting greater reasoning diversity, and successfully mitigating entropy collapse.
本文的动机源于现有可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）方法的局限性，该方法对所有令牌分配统一的优势信号，从而无法在复杂推理过程中有效引导探索，并导致熵崩溃。为解决此问题，作者提出了不确定性感知优势塑造（UCAS），这是一种无模型方法，通过利用模型内部不确定性信号来细化信用分配，其过程分为两个阶段：使用自置信度代理调制响应级优势，并基于原始逻辑确定性应用非对称令牌级惩罚。在五个数学推理基准上的实验结果表明，UCAS在多个模型规模上显著优于强RLVR基线，实现了更高的奖励，促进了更大的推理多样性，并成功缓解了熵崩溃。
ORBIT: On-policy Exploration-Exploitation for Controllable Multi-Budget Reasoning
Authors: Kun Liang, Clive Bai, Xin Xu, Chenming Tang, Sanwoo Lee, Weijie Liu, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
First: 2026-01-13T07:57:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T14:12:28+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) achieve strong performance by leveraging long-form Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning, but uniformly applying overlong reasoning at inference time incurs substantial and often unnecessary computational cost. To address this, prior work explores various strategies to infer an appropriate reasoning budget from the input. However, such approaches are unreliable in the worst case, as estimating the minimal required reasoning effort is fundamentally difficult, and they implicitly fix the trade-off between reasoning cost and accuracy during training, limiting flexibility under varying deployment scenarios. Motivated by these limitations, we propose ORBIT, a controllable multi-budget reasoning framework with well-separated reasoning modes triggered by input. ORBIT employs multi-stage reinforcement learning to discover Pareto-optimal reasoning behaviors at each effort, followed by on-policy distillation to fuse these behaviors into a single unified model. Experiments show that ORBIT achieves (1) controllable reasoning behavior over multiple modes, (2) competitive reasoning density within each mode, and (3) integration of these frontier policies into a single unified student model while preserving clear mode separation and high per-mode performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ORBIT：面向可控多预算推理的在线策略探索-利用框架
近期的大型推理模型通过利用长链思维链推理展现出强大性能，但在推理时统一应用过长的推理过程会产生高昂且常不必要的计算成本。为解决此问题，先前研究探索了多种从输入推断适当推理预算的策略。然而，此类方法在最坏情况下并不可靠，因为估计最小所需推理量本质上是困难的，且它们在训练中隐式固定了推理成本与准确性的权衡，限制了不同部署场景下的灵活性。基于这些局限，我们提出ORBIT——一种由输入触发的、具有明确分离推理模式的可控多预算推理框架。ORBIT采用多阶段强化学习探索各推理量级的帕累托最优行为，再通过在线策略蒸馏将这些行为融合至单一统一模型。实验表明，ORBIT实现了：（1）跨多模式的可控推理行为；（2）各模式内具有竞争力的推理密度；（3）将前沿策略集成至单一学生模型，同时保持清晰的模式分离与各模式的高性能。

This paper addresses the inefficiency of uniformly applying long-chain reasoning in Large Reasoning Models, which incurs unnecessary computational costs, by proposing ORBIT, a controllable multi-budget reasoning framework. The method uses multi-stage reinforcement learning to discover Pareto-optimal reasoning behaviors at different effort levels and then distills these into a single unified model via on-policy distillation. Experimental results demonstrate that ORBIT achieves controllable reasoning across multiple modes, maintains competitive reasoning density within each mode, and successfully integrates frontier policies into one model while preserving mode separation and high performance.
本文针对大型推理模型统一应用长链推理导致计算成本不必要增加的低效问题，提出了ORBIT，一个可控的多预算推理框架。该方法采用多阶段强化学习来发现不同努力水平下的帕累托最优推理行为，然后通过策略蒸馏将这些行为融合到单一统一模型中。实验结果表明，ORBIT实现了跨多种模式的可控推理，在每个模式下保持了有竞争力的推理密度，并成功将前沿策略集成到一个模型中，同时保持了清晰的模式分离和高性能。
UniDoc-RL: Coarse-to-Fine Visual RAG with Hierarchical Actions and Dense Rewards
Authors: Jun Wang, Shuo Tan, Zelong Sun, Tiancheng Gu, Yongle Zhao, Ziyong Feng, Kaicheng Yang, Cewu Lu
First: 2026-04-16T13:03:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T13:03:32+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) extends Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) with external visual knowledge. However, existing visual RAG systems typically rely on generic retrieval signals that overlook the fine-grained visual semantics essential for complex reasoning. To address this limitation, we propose UniDoc-RL, a unified reinforcement learning framework in which an LVLM agent jointly performs retrieval, reranking, active visual perception, and reasoning. UniDoc-RL formulates visual information acquisition as a sequential decision-making problem with a hierarchical action space. Specifically, it progressively refines visual evidence from coarse-grained document retrieval to fine-grained image selection and active region cropping, allowing the model to suppress irrelevant content and attend to information-dense regions. For effective end-to-end training, we introduce a dense multi-reward scheme that provides task-aware supervision for each action. Based on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), UniDoc-RL aligns agent behavior with multiple objectives without relying on a separate value network. To support this training paradigm, we curate a comprehensive dataset of high-quality reasoning trajectories with fine-grained action annotations. Experiments on three benchmarks demonstrate that UniDoc-RL consistently surpasses state-of-the-art baselines, yielding up to 17.7% gains over prior RL-based methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniDoc-RL：基于分层动作与密集奖励的从粗到细视觉检索增强生成框架
检索增强生成（RAG）通过外部视觉知识扩展大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）。然而，现有视觉RAG系统通常依赖通用检索信号，忽略了复杂推理所需的关键细粒度视觉语义。为突破此局限，我们提出UniDoc-RL——一个统一的强化学习框架，其中LVLM智能体协同执行检索、重排序、主动视觉感知与推理。该框架将视觉信息获取建模为具有分层动作空间的序列决策问题：从粗粒度文档检索逐步细化至细粒度图像选择与主动区域裁剪，从而抑制无关内容并聚焦信息密集区域。为实现端到端高效训练，我们设计了密集多奖励机制，为每个动作提供任务感知监督。基于组相对策略优化（GRPO），UniDoc-RL无需独立价值网络即可使智能体行为对齐多目标。为支撑此训练范式，我们构建了包含细粒度动作标注的高质量推理轨迹数据集。在三个基准测试上的实验表明，UniDoc-RL持续超越现有最优基线，相较先前基于强化学习的方法最高提升17.7%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of existing visual Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems, which often rely on generic retrieval signals that miss fine-grained visual semantics crucial for complex reasoning. To overcome this, the authors propose UniDoc-RL, a unified reinforcement learning framework where a Large Vision-Language Model agent jointly performs retrieval, reranking, active perception, and reasoning through a hierarchical action space that refines evidence from coarse document retrieval to fine region cropping. A dense multi-reward scheme and Group Relative Policy Optimization enable end-to-end training without a separate value network. Experimental results on three benchmarks show that UniDoc-RL consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving up to 17.7% improvement over prior RL-based methods.

A Queueing-Theoretic Framework for Dynamic Attack Surfaces: Data-Integrated Risk Analysis and Adaptive Defense
Authors: Jihyeon Yun, Abdullah Yasin Etcibasi, Ming Shi, C. Emre Koksal
First: 2026-04-12T02:52:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T12:55:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We develop a queueing-theoretic framework to model the temporal evolution of cyber-attack surfaces, where the number of active vulnerabilities is represented as the backlog of a queue. Vulnerabilities arrive as they are discovered or created, and leave the system when they are patched or successfully exploited. Building on this model, we study how automation affects attack and defense dynamics by introducing an AI amplification factor that scales arrival, exploit, and patching rates. Our analysis shows that even symmetric automation can increase the rate of successful exploits. We validate the model using vulnerability data collected from an open source software supply chain and show that it closely matches real-world attack surface dynamics. Empirical results reveal heavy-tailed patching times, which we prove induce long-range dependence in vulnerability backlog and help explain persistent cyber risk. Utilizing our queueing abstraction for the attack surface, we develop a systematic approach for cyber risk mitigation. We formulate the dynamic defense problem as a constrained Markov decision process with resource-budget and switching-cost constraints, and develop a reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that achieves provably near-optimal regret. Numerical experiments validate the approach and demonstrate that our adaptive RL-based defense policies significantly reduce successful exploits and mitigate heavy-tail queue events. Using trace-driven experiments on the ARVO dataset, we show that the proposed RL-based defense policy reduces the average number of active vulnerabilities in a software supply chain by over 90% compared to existing defense practices, without increasing the overall maintenance budget. Our results allow defenders to quantify cumulative exposure risk under long-range dependent attack dynamics and to design adaptive defense strategies with provable efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态攻击面的排队论框架：数据集成风险分析与自适应防御
我们开发了一个排队论框架来建模网络攻击面的时间演化，其中活跃漏洞数量被表示为队列积压。漏洞随着被发现或创建而到达，并在被修补或成功利用后离开系统。基于此模型，我们通过引入一个放大到达、利用和修补速率的AI放大因子，研究自动化如何影响攻击与防御动态。分析表明，即使对称自动化也会增加成功利用的速率。我们使用从开源软件供应链收集的漏洞数据验证模型，并证明其与现实世界攻击面动态高度吻合。实证结果揭示了重尾修补时间，我们证明这会引发漏洞积压的长程依赖性，并有助于解释持续的网络风险。利用攻击面的排队抽象，我们开发了一种系统性的网络风险缓解方法。将动态防御问题建模为具有资源预算和切换成本约束的约束马尔可夫决策过程，并开发了一种可证明近乎最优遗憾的强化学习算法。数值实验验证了该方法，并表明我们基于强化学习的自适应防御策略显著减少了成功利用并缓解了重尾队列事件。通过在ARVO数据集上进行追踪驱动实验，我们证明所提出的基于强化学习的防御策略相比现有防御实践，在不增加总体维护预算的情况下，将软件供应链中的平均活跃漏洞数量降低了90%以上。我们的研究使防御者能够量化长程依赖攻击动态下的累积暴露风险，并设计具有可证明效率的自适应防御策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to model the dynamic nature of cyber-attack surfaces, this paper develops a queueing-theoretic framework where active vulnerabilities are treated as a queue backlog, with arrivals from discoveries and departures from patching or exploitation. The method incorporates an AI amplification factor to analyze automation's impact on attack and defense dynamics, and formulates dynamic defense as a constrained Markov decision process, solved with a reinforcement learning algorithm for adaptive policies. Experimental validation using open-source software supply chain data shows the model accurately captures real-world dynamics, revealing heavy-tailed patching times that induce long-range dependence in risk; the proposed RL-based defense policy reduces active vulnerabilities by over 90% compared to existing practices without increasing budget, demonstrating significant risk mitigation.
本文旨在建模网络攻击面的动态演化，提出了一种排队论框架，将活跃漏洞视为队列积压，其到达源于漏洞发现，离开则通过修补或成功利用。方法引入了人工智能放大因子来分析自动化对攻防动态的影响，并将动态防御问题构建为带约束的马尔可夫决策过程，通过强化学习算法求解自适应策略。基于开源软件供应链数据的实验验证表明，该模型能准确反映实际动态，揭示了重尾修补时间会导致风险的长程依赖性；所提出的基于强化学习的防御策略在不增加总维护预算的情况下，将活跃漏洞数量较现有实践降低了90%以上，显著降低了风险。
WavAlign: Enhancing Intelligence and Expressiveness in Spoken Dialogue Models via Adaptive Hybrid Post-Training
Authors: Yifu Chen, Shengpeng Ji, Qian Chen, Tianle Liang, Yangzhuo Li, Ziqing Wang, Wen Wang, Jingyu Lu, Haoxiao Wang, Xueyi Pu, Fan Zhuo, Zhou Zhao
First: 2026-04-16T12:20:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T12:20:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
End-to-end spoken dialogue models have garnered significant attention because they offer a higher potential ceiling in expressiveness and perceptual ability than cascaded systems. However, the intelligence and expressiveness of current open-source spoken dialogue models often remain below expectations. Motivated by the success of online reinforcement learning(RL) in other domains, one might attempt to directly apply preference optimization to spoken dialogue models, yet this transfer is non-trivial. We analyze these obstacles from the perspectives of reward modeling and rollout sampling, focusing on how sparse preference supervision interacts with dense speech generation under shared-parameter updates. Based on the analysis, we propose a modality-aware adaptive post-training recipe that makes RL practical for spoken dialogue: it constrains preference updates to the semantic channel and improves acoustic behavior via explicit anchoring, while dynamically regulating their mixture from rollout statistics to avoid unreliable preference gradients. We evaluate the method across multiple spoken dialogue benchmarks and representative architectures, and observe consistent improvements in semantic quality and speech expressiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WavAlign：通过自适应混合后训练增强口语对话模型的智能性与表现力
端到端口语对话模型因其在表现力与感知能力上较级联系统具有更高潜力上限而备受关注。然而，当前开源口语对话模型的智能性与表现力常低于预期。受在线强化学习在其他领域成功的启发，或可尝试直接将偏好优化应用于口语对话模型，但这一迁移并非易事。我们从奖励建模与推演采样的角度分析这些障碍，重点关注稀疏偏好监督如何在共享参数更新下与密集语音生成交互。基于分析，我们提出一种模态感知的自适应后训练方案，使强化学习能实际应用于口语对话：该方案将偏好更新约束于语义通道，并通过显式锚定改善声学行为，同时根据推演统计动态调节二者的混合以避免不可靠的偏好梯度。我们在多个口语对话基准测试与代表性架构上评估该方法，观察到语义质量与语音表现力的一致提升。

The paper is motivated by the limited intelligence and expressiveness of current open-source spoken dialogue models, despite their higher potential compared to cascaded systems. To address this, the authors propose WavAlign, a modality-aware adaptive post-training method that makes reinforcement learning practical for spoken dialogue by constraining preference updates to the semantic channel and improving acoustic behavior via explicit anchoring, while dynamically regulating their mixture based on rollout statistics to avoid unreliable gradients. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks and architectures show consistent improvements in both semantic quality and speech expressiveness.

Enhancing LLM-Based Neural Network Generation: Few-Shot Prompting and Efficient Validation for Automated Architecture Design
Authors: Raghuvir Duvvuri, Chandini Vysyaraju, Avi Goyal, Dmitry Ignatov, Radu Timofte
First: 2025-12-30T10:01:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T12:18:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated neural network architecture design remains a significant challenge in computer vision. Task diversity and computational constraints require both effective architectures and efficient search methods. Large Language Models (LLMs) present a promising alternative to computationally intensive Neural Architecture Search (NAS), but their application to architecture generation in computer vision has not been systematically studied, particularly regarding prompt engineering and validation strategies. Building on the task-agnostic NNGPT/LEMUR framework, this work introduces and validates two key contributions for computer vision. First, we present Few-Shot Architecture Prompting (FSAP), the first systematic study of the number of supporting examples (n = 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6) for LLM-based architecture generation. We find that using n = 3 examples best balances architectural diversity and context focus for vision tasks. Second, we introduce Whitespace-Normalized Hash Validation, a lightweight deduplication method (less than 1 ms) that provides a 100x speedup over AST parsing and prevents redundant training of duplicate computer vision architectures. In large-scale experiments across seven computer vision benchmarks (MNIST, CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, CelebA, ImageNette, SVHN, Places365), we generated 1,900 unique architectures. We also introduce a dataset-balanced evaluation methodology to address the challenge of comparing architectures across heterogeneous vision tasks. These contributions provide actionable guidelines for LLM-based architecture search in computer vision and establish rigorous evaluation practices, making automated design more accessible to researchers with limited computational resources.

LongAct: Harnessing Intrinsic Activation Patterns for Long-Context Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Bowen Ping, Zijun Chen, Tingfeng Hui, Qize Yu, Chenxuan Li, Junchi Yan, Baobao Chang
First: 2026-04-16T12:06:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T12:06:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a critical driver for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). While recent advancements have focused on reward engineering or data synthesis, few studies exploit the model's intrinsic representation characteristics to guide the training process. In this paper, we first observe the presence of high-magnitude activations within the query and key vectors when processing long contexts. Drawing inspiration from model quantization -- which establishes the criticality of such high-magnitude activations -- and the insight that long-context reasoning inherently exhibits a sparse structure, we hypothesize that these weights serve as the pivotal drivers for effective model optimization. Based on this insight, we propose LongAct, a strategy that shifts from uniform to saliency-guided sparse updates. By selectively updating only the weights associated with these significant activations, LongAct achieves an approximate 8% improvement on LongBench v2 and enhances generalization on the RULER benchmark. Furthermore, our method exhibits remarkable universality, consistently boosting performance across diverse RL algorithms such as GRPO and DAPO. Extensive ablation studies suggest that focusing on these salient features is key to unlocking long-context potential.

Dual-Axis Generative Reward Model Toward Semantic and Turn-taking Robustness in Interactive Spoken Dialogue Models
Authors: Yifu Chen, Shengpeng Ji, Zhengqing Liu, Qian Chen, Wen Wang, Ziqing Wang, Yangzhuo Li, Tianle Liang, Zhou Zhao
First: 2026-04-16T12:03:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T12:03:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving seamless, human-like interaction remains a key challenge for full-duplex spoken dialogue models (SDMs). Reinforcement learning (RL) has substantially enhanced text- and vision-language models, while well-designed reward signals are crucial for the performance of RL. We consider RL a promising strategy to address the key challenge for SDMs. However, a fundamental barrier persists: prevailing automated metrics for assessing interaction quality rely on superficial proxies, such as behavioral statistics or timing-prediction accuracy, failing to provide reliable reward signals for RL. On the other hand, human evaluations, despite their richness, remain costly, inconsistent, and difficult to scale. We tackle this critical barrier by proposing a Dual-Axis Generative Reward Model, which is trained to understand complex interaction dynamics using a detailed taxonomy and an annotated dataset, produces a single score and, crucially, provides separate evaluations for semantic quality and interaction timing. Such dual outputs furnish precise diagnostic feedback for SDMs and deliver a dependable, instructive reward signal suitable for online reinforcement learning. Our model achieves state-of-the-art performance on interaction-quality assessment across a wide spectrum of datasets, spanning synthetic dialogues and complex real-world interactions.

标题：面向交互式口语对话模型语义与话轮转换鲁棒性的双轴生成式奖励模型
实现无缝、类人的交互仍是全双工口语对话模型（SDMs）的核心挑战。强化学习（RL）已显著提升文本与视觉语言模型性能，而精心设计的奖励信号对RL效果至关重要。我们认为RL是解决SDMs关键挑战的有效策略，但根本障碍依然存在：当前评估交互质量的自动化指标依赖表层代理（如行为统计或时序预测准确率），无法为RL提供可靠的奖励信号；而人工评估虽信息丰富，却成本高昂、一致性差且难以扩展。为此，我们提出双轴生成式奖励模型以突破此关键障碍：该模型通过精细分类体系与标注数据集训练，能理解复杂交互动态，生成单一评分，并关键性地提供语义质量与交互时序的独立评估。这种双轴输出既为SDMs提供精准诊断反馈，又为在线强化学习提供可靠且具指导性的奖励信号。我们的模型在涵盖合成对话与复杂真实交互的广泛数据集上，实现了交互质量评估的最先进性能。

An Intelligent Robotic and Bio-Digestor Framework for Smart Waste Management
Authors: Radhika Khatri, Adit Tewari, Nikhil Sharma, M. B. Srinivas
First: 2026-04-16T11:19:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T11:19:36+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 10 figures, submitted to 7th International Conference on Smart Systems and Inventive Technology (ICSSIT 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rapid urbanization and continuous population growth have made municipal solid waste management increasingly challenging. These challenges highlight the need for smarter and automated waste management solutions. This paper presents the design and evaluation of an integrated waste management framework that combines two connected systems, a robotic waste segregation module and an optimized bio-digestor. The robotic waste segregation system uses a MyCobot 280 Jetson Nano robotic arm along with YOLOv8 object detection and robot operating system (ROS)-based path planning to identify and sort waste in real time. It classifies waste into four different categories with high precision, reducing the need for manual intervention. After segregation, the biodegradable waste is transferred to a bio-digestor system equipped with multiple sensors. These sensors continuously monitor key parameters, including temperature, pH, pressure, and motor revolutions per minute. The Particle Swarm Optimization (PSO) algorithm, combined with a regression model, is used to dynamically adjust system parameters. This intelligent optimization approach ensures stable operation and maximizes digestion efficiency under varying environmental conditions. System testing under dynamic conditions demonstrates a sorting accuracy of 98% along with highly efficient biological conversion. The proposed framework offers a scalable, intelligent, and practical solution for modern waste management, making it suitable for both residential and industrial applications.
