GenRec: A Preference-Oriented Generative Framework for Large-Scale Recommendation
Authors: Yanyan Zou, Junbo Qi, Lunsong Huang, Yu Li, Kewei Xu, Jiabao Gao, Binglei Zhao, Xuanhua Yang, Sulong Xu, Shengjie Li
Venue: SIGIR 2026
First: 2026-04-16T11:07:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T11:07:05+00:00
Comments: SIGIR 2026 Camera-Ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative Retrieval (GR) offers a promising paradigm for recommendation through next-token prediction (NTP). However, scaling it to large-scale industrial systems introduces three challenges: (i) within a single request, the identical model inputs may produce inconsistent outputs due to the pagination request mechanism; (ii) the prohibitive cost of encoding long user behavior sequences with multi-token item representations based on semantic IDs, and (iii) aligning the generative policy with nuanced user preference signals. We present GenRec, a preference-oriented generative framework deployed on the JD App that addresses above challenges within a single decoder-only architecture. For training objective, we propose Page-wise NTP task, which supervises over an entire interaction page rather than each interacted item individually, providing denser gradient signal and resolving the one-to-many ambiguity of point-wise training. On the prefilling side, an asymmetric linear Token Merger compresses multi-token Semantic IDs in the prompt while preserving full-resolution decoding, reducing input length by ~2X with negligible accuracy loss. To further align outputs with user satisfaction, we introduce GRPO-SR, a reinforcement learning method that pairs Group Relative Policy Optimization with NLL regularization for training stability, and employs Hybrid Rewards combining a dense reward model with a relevance gate to mitigate reward hacking. In month-long online A/B tests serving production traffic, GenRec achieves 9.5% improvement in click count and 8.7% in transaction count over the existing pipeline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GenRec：面向偏好的生成式大规模推荐框架
生成式检索（GR）通过下一词预测（NTP）为推荐系统提供了有前景的范式。然而，将其扩展至大规模工业系统面临三大挑战：（i）在单次请求中，由于分页请求机制，相同的模型输入可能产生不一致的输出；（ii）基于语义ID的多词项表示对长用户行为序列进行编码的成本过高；（iii）使生成策略与细粒度用户偏好信号对齐。本文提出GenRec——一个部署于京东App的面向偏好生成框架，在单一仅解码器架构内解决上述挑战。在训练目标上，我们提出页面级NTP任务，对整个交互页面而非单个交互项进行监督，提供更密集的梯度信号并解决逐点训练的一对多歧义问题。在预填充侧，非对称线性词元融合器压缩提示中的多词元语义ID，同时保持全分辨率解码能力，将输入长度减少约2倍且精度损失可忽略。为进一步对齐输出与用户满意度，我们提出GRPO-SR强化学习方法，将组相对策略优化与负对数似然正则化结合以稳定训练，并采用融合稠密奖励模型与相关性门控的混合奖励机制以缓解奖励破解。在为期一个月的生产流量在线A/B测试中，GenRec相比现有流水线实现了点击量提升9.5%，交易量提升8.7%。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces GenRec, a generative framework for large-scale recommendation, motivated by challenges in scaling generative retrieval to industrial systems: inconsistent outputs due to pagination, high encoding costs from long user behavior sequences, and misalignment with user preferences. The method employs a decoder-only architecture with a Page-wise Next-Token Prediction task for denser training signals, an asymmetric linear Token Merger to compress multi-token item representations, and GRPO-SR, a reinforcement learning approach using hybrid rewards for policy alignment. Experimental results from month-long online A/B tests on the JD App show that GenRec achieves a 9.5% increase in click count and an 8.7% increase in transaction count compared to the existing pipeline.
本文提出了GenRec，一种面向大规模推荐的生成式框架，其动机在于解决生成式检索在工业系统中扩展时的挑战：分页机制导致的输出不一致、长用户行为序列编码成本过高以及与用户偏好对齐困难。该方法采用仅解码器架构，通过页面级下一词预测任务提供更密集的训练信号，使用非对称线性令牌合并器压缩多令牌项目表示，并引入GRPO-SR强化学习方法，结合混合奖励以优化策略对齐。在京东应用的在线A/B测试中，GenRec相比现有流水线实现了点击量提升9.5%和交易量提升8.7%的主要实验结果。
Does RL Expand the Capability Boundary of LLM Agents? A PASS@(k,T) Analysis
Authors: Zhiyuan Zhai, Wenjing Yan, Xiaodan Shao, Xin Wang
First: 2026-04-16T11:06:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T11:06:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Does reinforcement learning genuinely expand what LLM agents can do, or merely make them more reliable? For static reasoning, recent work answers the second: base and RL pass@k curves converge at large k. We ask whether this holds for agentic tool use, where T rounds of interaction enable compositional strategies that re-sampling cannot recover. We introduce PASS@(k,T), a two-dimensional metric that jointly varies sampling budget k and interaction depth T, separating capability expansion from efficiency improvement. Our main finding is that, contrary to the static-reasoning result, tool-use RL genuinely enlarges the capability boundary: the RL agent's pass-curve pulls above the base model's and the gap widens at large k rather than converging. The expansion is specific to compositional, sequential information gathering; on simpler tasks RL behaves as prior work predicts. Under matched training data, supervised fine-tuning regresses the boundary on the same compositional tasks, isolating self-directed exploration as the causal factor. Mechanism analysis shows RL reweights the base strategy distribution toward the subset whose downstream reasoning more often yields a correct answer, with the improvement concentrated on how the agent integrates retrieved information. These results reconcile optimistic and pessimistic readings of RL for LLMs: both are correct, on different task types.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习是否拓展了LLM智能体的能力边界？基于PASS@(k,T)的分析
强化学习究竟能真正拓展LLM智能体的能力边界，还是仅提升其可靠性？针对静态推理任务，近期研究表明后者成立：基础模型与RL模型的pass@k曲线在大k值处趋于收敛。本文探究这一结论是否适用于智能体工具调用场景——在该场景中，T轮交互能实现组合式策略，而重采样无法复现此类策略。我们提出PASS@(k,T)二维评估指标，通过联合调控采样预算k与交互深度T，区分能力拓展与效率提升。核心发现表明：与静态推理结论相反，工具调用场景中的RL确实能拓展能力边界——RL智能体的通过率曲线持续高于基础模型，且在大k值时差距扩大而非收敛。这种拓展性特指组合式序贯信息获取任务；在简单任务中RL表现符合先前研究预期。在训练数据匹配条件下，监督微调在相同组合任务上会出现能力边界退化，这证实自主探索是根本成因。机制分析显示RL会重构基础策略分布，使其更倾向于下游推理更易得出正确答案的策略子集，且改进主要集中在智能体整合检索信息的方式上。这些发现调和了关于LLM强化学习的乐观与悲观观点：二者在不同任务类型中均成立。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether reinforcement learning (RL) genuinely expands the capabilities of LLM agents in tool-use settings, rather than merely improving their reliability, a distinction previously established for static reasoning tasks. The authors introduce PASS@(k,T), a two-dimensional metric that jointly varies sampling budget (k) and interaction depth (T) to separate capability expansion from efficiency gains. The main experimental finding is that, contrary to results in static reasoning, RL for tool use genuinely enlarges the capability boundary: the RL agent's performance curve pulls above that of the base model, and the gap widens at larger sampling budgets rather than converging. This expansion is specific to compositional, sequential information-gathering tasks; on simpler tasks, RL behaves as prior work predicts. Under matched training data, supervised fine-tuning regresses performance on these compositional tasks, isolating self-directed exploration as the causal factor. Mechanism analysis indicates RL reweights the base strategy distribution toward subsets whose downstream reasoning more often yields correct answers, with improvement concentrated on how the agent integrates retrieved information.
本文研究强化学习（RL）是否真正扩展了大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在工具使用场景中的能力边界，而非仅提升其可靠性，这一区别在静态推理任务中已有定论。作者引入了PASS@(k,T)这一二维指标，联合变化采样预算（k）和交互深度（T），以区分能力扩展与效率提升。主要实验发现是，与静态推理的结果相反，工具使用的RL确实扩大了能力边界：RL智能体的性能曲线超越了基础模型，且差距在更大采样预算下扩大而非收敛。这种扩展特定于组合性、顺序性的信息收集任务；在更简单的任务上，RL的表现与先前研究预测一致。在匹配的训练数据下，监督微调在这些组合任务上会导致性能退化，从而将自我导向的探索确认为因果因素。机制分析表明，RL重新加权了基础策略分布，使其偏向于下游推理更常产生正确答案的子集，且改进集中在智能体如何整合检索到的信息上。
Drowsiness-Aware Adaptive Autonomous Braking System based on Deep Reinforcement Learning for Enhanced Road Safety
Authors: Hossem Eddine Hafidi, Elisabetta De Giovanni, Teodoro Montanaro, Ilaria Sergi, Massimo De Vittorio, Luigi Patrono
First: 2026-04-15T13:39:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T09:51:50+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 12 figures. Under review at IEEE Transactions on Intelligent Vehicles
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Driver drowsiness significantly impairs the ability to accurately judge safe braking distances and is estimated to contribute to 10%-20% of road accidents in Europe. Traditional driver-assistance systems lack adaptability to real-time physiological states such as drowsiness. This paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning-based autonomous braking system that integrates vehicle dynamics with driver physiological data. Drowsiness is detected from ECG signals using a Recurrent Neural Network (RNN), selected through an extensive benchmark analysis of 2-minute windows with varying segmentation and overlap configurations. The inferred drowsiness state is incorporated into the observable state space of a Double-Dueling Deep Q-Network (DQN) agent, where driver impairment is modeled as an action delay. The system is implemented and evaluated in a high-fidelity CARLA simulation environment. Experimental results show that the proposed agent achieves a 99.99% success rate in avoiding collisions under both drowsy and non-drowsy conditions. These findings demonstrate the effectiveness of physiology-aware control strategies for enhancing adaptive and intelligent driving safety systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的睡意感知自适应自主制动系统以提升道路安全
驾驶员睡意显著削弱准确判断安全制动距离的能力，据估计在欧洲导致10%-20%的道路事故。传统驾驶辅助系统缺乏对睡意等实时生理状态的适应性。本文提出一种基于深度强化学习的自主制动系统，将车辆动力学与驾驶员生理数据相结合。通过采用不同分段和重叠配置的2分钟窗口进行广泛基准分析，选用循环神经网络（RNN）从心电信号中检测睡意。推断出的睡意状态被纳入双竞争深度Q网络（DQN）智能体的可观测状态空间，其中驾驶员能力受损被建模为动作延迟。该系统在高保真CARLA仿真环境中实现并评估。实验结果表明，所提智能体在睡意与非睡意条件下均实现99.99%的碰撞避免成功率。这些发现证明了生理感知控制策略对增强自适应智能驾驶安全系统的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the significant role of driver drowsiness in road accidents and the lack of adaptability in traditional assistance systems, this paper proposes a deep reinforcement learning-based autonomous braking system that integrates real-time driver drowsiness detection. The method employs a Recurrent Neural Network to detect drowsiness from ECG signals, with the state integrated into a Double-Dueling DQN agent that models impairment as an action delay. Experimental evaluation in a CARLA simulation environment demonstrates that the proposed system achieves a 99.99% collision avoidance success rate under both drowsy and non-drowsy conditions, highlighting the effectiveness of physiology-aware control for enhanced driving safety.
本研究针对驾驶员疲劳在交通事故中的重要作用以及传统辅助系统缺乏适应性的问题，提出了一种基于深度强化学习的自主制动系统，该系统整合了实时驾驶员疲劳检测。方法采用循环神经网络从心电信号中检测疲劳状态，并将该状态集成到一个将驾驶员损伤建模为动作延迟的双重决斗深度Q网络智能体中。在CARLA仿真环境中的实验评估表明，所提出的系统在疲劳和非疲劳条件下均实现了99.99%的碰撞避免成功率，这凸显了生理感知控制策略对于提升自适应智能驾驶安全系统的有效性。
Learning Ad Hoc Network Dynamics via Graph-Structured World Models
Authors: Can Karacelebi, Yusuf Talha Sahin, Elif Surer, Ertan Onur
First: 2026-04-16T09:32:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T09:32:15+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 4 figures. Submitted to the IEEE Global Communications Conference (GLOBECOM) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ad hoc wireless networks exhibit complex, innate and coupled dynamics: node mobility, energy depletion and topology change that are difficult to model analytically. Model-free deep reinforcement learning requires sustained online interaction whereas existing model based approaches use flat state representations that lose per node structure. Therefore we propose G-RSSM, a graph structured recurrent state space model that maintains per node latent states with cross node multi head attention to learn the dynamics jointly from offline trajectories. We apply the proposed method to the downstream task clustering where a cluster head selection policy trains entirely through imagined rollouts in the learned world model. Across 27 evaluation scenarios spanning MANET, VANET, FANET, WSN and tactical networks with N=30 to 1000 nodes, the learned policy maintains high connectivity with only trained for N=50. Herein, we propose the first multi physics graph structured world model applied to combinatorial per node decision making in size agnostic wireless ad hoc networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过图结构世界模型学习自组织网络动态
自组织无线网络展现出复杂、固有且耦合的动态特性：节点移动性、能量耗竭与拓扑变化难以通过解析方法建模。无模型深度强化学习需要持续在线交互，而现有基于模型的方法使用扁平化状态表征，丢失了节点级结构信息。为此，我们提出G-RSSM——一种图结构循环状态空间模型，通过跨节点多头注意力机制维护各节点潜在状态，从离线轨迹中联合学习网络动态。我们将该方法应用于下游任务聚类，其中簇头选择策略完全通过在已学习世界模型中的想象推演进行训练。在涵盖MANET、VANET、FANET、WSN及战术网络的27个评估场景中（节点数N=30至1000），仅使用N=50节点训练的策略仍能保持高连接性。本研究首次提出将多物理图结构世界模型应用于规模无关无线自组织网络中的组合式节点级决策。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the complex, coupled dynamics of ad hoc wireless networks—such as node mobility and energy depletion—which are difficult to model analytically, and the limitations of existing model-free or flat state representation methods. The proposed method, G-RSSM, is a graph-structured recurrent state space model that maintains per-node latent states and uses cross-node multi-head attention to learn network dynamics jointly from offline trajectories. In experiments, the model was applied to a clustering task where a cluster head selection policy was trained entirely through imagined rollouts in the learned world model; across 27 evaluation scenarios with 30 to 1000 nodes, the policy maintained high connectivity despite being trained on only 50 nodes, demonstrating effectiveness in size-agnostic networks.
本研究的动机在于无线自组织网络具有复杂且耦合的动态特性，如节点移动性和能量消耗，难以用解析方法建模，而现有的无模型或扁平状态表示方法存在局限。提出的方法G-RSSM是一种图结构循环状态空间模型，通过维护每个节点的潜在状态并利用跨节点多头注意力机制，从离线轨迹中联合学习网络动态。在实验中，该模型应用于聚类任务，其中簇头选择策略完全通过在所学世界模型中的想象推演进行训练；在涵盖30至1000个节点的27个评估场景中，该策略尽管仅基于50个节点训练，仍能保持高连接性，证明了其在规模无关网络中的有效性。
Sequence Search: Automated Sequence Design using Neural Architecture Search
Authors: Rokgi Hong, Hongjun An, Sooyeon Ji, Jongho Lee
First: 2026-04-16T08:50:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:50:22+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing an MR sequence is challenging and remains largely constrained by human intuition. Recently, AI-driven approaches have been proposed; however, most require an initial sequence for parameter optimization or extensive training datasets, limiting their general applicability. In this study, we propose "Sequence Search," an automated sequence design framework based on neural architecture search. The method takes tissue properties, imaging parameters, and design objectives as inputs and generates pulse sequences satisfying the design objectives, without requiring prior knowledge of conventional sequence structures. Sequence Search iteratively generates candidate sequences through neural architecture search and optimizes them via a differentiable Bloch simulator and objective-specific loss functions using gradient-based learning. The framework successfully replicated conventional spin-echo, T2-weighted spin-echo, and inversion recovery sequences. Less intuitive solutions were also discovered, such as three-RF spin-echo-like sequences with reduced RF energy and refocusing phases deviating from the conventional Hahn-echo. This work establishes a generalizable framework for automated MR sequence design, highlighting the potential to explore configurations beyond conventional designs based on human intuition.
中文标题/摘要
标题：序列搜索：基于神经架构搜索的自动化序列设计
磁共振序列开发具有挑战性，且主要受限于人类直觉。近期虽提出了AI驱动方法，但大多需要初始序列进行参数优化或大量训练数据集，限制了其普适性。本研究提出“序列搜索”——一种基于神经架构搜索的自动化序列设计框架。该方法以组织特性、成像参数和设计目标为输入，生成满足设计目标的脉冲序列，无需传统序列结构的先验知识。该框架通过神经架构搜索迭代生成候选序列，并借助可微分Bloch模拟器与基于梯度的目标损失函数进行优化。该框架成功复现了传统自旋回波、T2加权自旋回波及反转恢复序列，同时发现了非直觉性解决方案，如降低射频能量的三射频类自旋回波序列及偏离传统Hahn回波的重聚相位设计。本研究构建了可推广的自动化磁共振序列设计框架，展现了探索超越人类直觉传统设计的可能性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of designing MRI sequences, which traditionally relies heavily on human expertise and existing AI methods that require initial sequences or large datasets, this paper introduces Sequence Search, an automated framework using neural architecture search. The method inputs tissue properties, imaging parameters, and design goals, then generates pulse sequences via iterative candidate generation and optimization with a differentiable Bloch simulator and gradient-based learning, without needing prior knowledge of conventional structures. Experimentally, the framework successfully replicated standard sequences like spin-echo and inversion recovery, and also discovered novel designs such as three-RF spin-echo-like sequences with lower RF energy and unconventional refocusing phases, demonstrating its ability to explore configurations beyond human intuition.
本研究针对磁共振序列设计长期依赖人工经验、且现有AI方法需初始序列或大量数据的局限，提出了基于神经架构搜索的自动化框架“Sequence Search”。该方法以组织特性、成像参数和设计目标为输入，通过神经架构搜索迭代生成候选序列，并利用可微分布洛赫模拟器和基于梯度的学习进行优化，无需传统序列结构先验知识。实验结果表明，该框架成功复现了自旋回波、T2加权自旋回波和反转恢复等常规序列，并发现了非直观的新设计，如降低射频能量的三射频自旋回波类序列及偏离传统哈恩回波的复相位方案，展现了超越人类直觉探索序列配置的潜力。
CogEvolution: A Human-like Generative Educational Agent to Simulate Student's Cognitive Evolution
Authors: Wei Zhang, Yihang Cheng, Zhirong Ye, Kezhen Huang
First: 2026-04-16T08:49:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:49:10+00:00
Comments: none
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative Agents, owing to their precise modeling and simulation capabilities of human behavior, have become a pivotal tool in the field of Artificial Intelligence in Education (AIEd) for uncovering complex cognitive processes of learners. However, existing educational agents predominantly rely on static personas to simulate student learning behaviors, neglecting the decisive role of deep cognitive capabilities in learning outcomes during practice interactions. Furthermore, they struggle to characterize the dynamic fluidity of knowledge internalization, transfer, and cognitive state transitions. To overcome this bottleneck, this paper proposes a human-like educational agent capable of simulating student cognitive evolution: CogEvolution. Specifically, we first construct a cognitive depth perceptron based on the Interactive, Constructive, Active, Passive (ICAP) taxonomy from cognitive psychology, achieving precise quantification of learner cognitive engagement. Subsequently, we propose a memory retrieval method based on Item Response Theory (IRT) to simulate the connection and assimilation of new and prior knowledge. Finally, we design a dynamic cognitive update mechanism based on evolutionary algorithms to simulate the real-time integration of student learning behaviors and cognitive evolution processes. Comprehensive evaluations demonstrate that CogEvolution not only significantly outperforms baseline models in behavioral fidelity and learning curve fitting but also uniquely reproduces plausible and robust cognitive evolutionary paths consistent with educational psychology expectations, providing a novel paradigm for constructing highly interpretable educational agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CogEvolution：模拟学生认知演化的人性化生成式教育智能体
生成式智能体凭借对人类行为的精准建模与仿真能力，已成为人工智能教育领域揭示学习者复杂认知过程的关键工具。然而，现有教育智能体主要依赖静态角色模拟学生学习行为，忽视了实践交互中深层认知能力对学习效果的决定性作用，且难以刻画知识内化、迁移及认知状态转换的动态流动性。为突破此瓶颈，本文提出能模拟学生认知演化的人性化教育智能体CogEvolution。具体而言，我们首先基于认知心理学的交互-建构-主动-被动分类框架构建认知深度感知器，实现对学习者认知投入的精准量化；随后提出基于项目反应理论的记忆检索方法，模拟新旧知识的联结与同化；最后设计基于演化算法的动态认知更新机制，模拟学生学习行为与认知演化过程的实时整合。综合评估表明，CogEvolution不仅在行为拟真度与学习曲线拟合上显著优于基线模型，更能独特复现符合教育心理学预期的合理且稳健的认知演化路径，为构建高可解释性教育智能体提供了新范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static personas in existing educational agents, which fail to capture deep cognitive capabilities and the dynamic nature of knowledge internalization, this paper introduces CogEvolution, a human-like generative agent designed to simulate student cognitive evolution. The method constructs a cognitive depth perceptron based on the ICAP taxonomy to quantify cognitive engagement, employs an Item Response Theory-based memory retrieval to model knowledge assimilation, and implements a dynamic cognitive update mechanism using evolutionary algorithms. Experimental results show that CogEvolution significantly outperforms baselines in behavioral fidelity and learning curve fitting, while also generating plausible cognitive evolutionary paths aligned with educational psychology.
针对现有教育智能体依赖静态角色、难以模拟深层认知能力和知识内化动态过程的不足，本文提出了CogEvolution，一种模拟学生认知演化的人性化生成教育智能体。方法基于认知心理学的ICAP分类构建认知深度感知器以量化学习投入，采用基于项目反应理论的记忆检索来模拟新旧知识联结与同化，并设计基于进化算法的动态认知更新机制来整合学习行为与认知演化。综合评估表明，CogEvolution在行为保真度和学习曲线拟合上显著优于基线模型，并能生成符合教育心理学预期的合理认知演化路径，为构建高可解释性教育智能体提供了新范式。
A hierarchical spatial-aware algorithm with efficient reinforcement learning for human-robot task planning and allocation in production
Authors: Jintao Xue, Xiao Li, Nianmin Zhang
Venue: Volume 98, April 2026, 103159
First: 2026-04-14T12:40:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:32:17+00:00
Comments: This is the accepted manuscript of a journal article accepted for publication in Robotics and Computer-Integrated Manufacturing (Elsevier)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In advanced manufacturing systems, humans and robots collaborate to conduct the production process. Effective task planning and allocation (TPA) is crucial for achieving high production efficiency, yet it remains challenging in complex and dynamic manufacturing environments. The dynamic nature of humans and robots, particularly the need to consider spatial information (e.g., humans' real-time position and the distance they need to move to complete a task), substantially complicates TPA. To address the above challenges, we decompose production tasks into manageable subtasks. We then implement a real-time hierarchical human-robot TPA algorithm, including a high-level agent for task planning and a low-level agent for task allocation. For the high-level agent, we propose an efficient buffer-based deep Q-learning method (EBQ), which reduces training time and enhances performance in production problems with long-term and sparse reward challenges. For the low-level agent, a path planning-based spatially aware method (SAP) is designed to allocate tasks to the appropriate human-robot resources, thereby achieving the corresponding sequential subtasks. We conducted experiments on a complex real-time production process in a 3D simulator. The results demonstrate that our proposed EBQ&SAP method effectively addresses human-robot TPA problems in complex and dynamic production processes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种具有高效强化学习的层次化空间感知算法用于生产中的人机任务规划与分配
在先进制造系统中，人与机器人协作完成生产过程。有效的任务规划与分配（TPA）对实现高生产效率至关重要，但在复杂动态的制造环境中仍具挑战性。人与机器人的动态特性，尤其是需要考虑空间信息（如人的实时位置及完成任务需移动的距离），显著增加了TPA的复杂性。为应对上述挑战，我们将生产任务分解为可管理的子任务，并实现了一种实时层次化人机TPA算法，包含用于任务规划的高层智能体和用于任务分配的低层智能体。针对高层智能体，我们提出了一种高效的基于缓冲区的深度Q学习方法（EBQ），该方法减少了训练时间，并在具有长期稀疏奖励挑战的生产问题中提升了性能。对于低层智能体，设计了一种基于路径规划的空间感知方法（SAP），用于将任务分配给合适的人机资源，从而实现相应的顺序子任务。我们在3D模拟器中针对复杂实时生产过程进行了实验，结果表明所提出的EBQ&SAP方法能有效解决复杂动态生产过程中的人机TPA问题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient human-robot collaboration in dynamic manufacturing, where spatial information and real-time task allocation are critical challenges, this paper proposes a hierarchical algorithm. The method decomposes tasks and employs a high-level agent using an efficient buffer-based deep Q-learning (EBQ) for planning and a low-level agent using a spatial-aware path planning (SAP) method for allocation. Experimental results in a 3D simulator show that the combined EBQ&SAP approach effectively handles task planning and allocation in complex, real-time production processes, reducing training time and improving performance.
针对动态制造中人机协作中空间信息和实时任务分配的挑战，本文提出了一种分层算法。该方法将任务分解，采用高层智能体基于高效缓冲深度Q学习进行规划，低层智能体基于空间感知路径规划方法进行分配。在3D模拟器中的实验结果表明，所提出的EBQ&SAP方法能有效处理复杂实时生产过程中的任务规划与分配问题，减少了训练时间并提升了性能。
Safe reinforcement learning with online filtering for fatigue-predictive human-robot task planning and allocation in production
Authors: Jintao Xue, Xiao Li, Nianmin Zhang
Venue: Volume 84, February 2026, Pages 561-583
First: 2026-04-14T12:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:32:15+00:00
Comments: This is the accepted manuscript of an article accepted for publication in \textit{Journal of Manufacturing Systems (Elsevier)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human-robot collaborative manufacturing, a core aspect of Industry 5.0, emphasizes ergonomics to enhance worker well-being. This paper addresses the dynamic human-robot task planning and allocation (HRTPA) problem, which involves determining when to perform tasks and who should execute them to maximize efficiency while ensuring workers' physical fatigue remains within safe limits. The inclusion of fatigue constraints, combined with production dynamics, significantly increases the complexity of the HRTPA problem. Traditional fatigue-recovery models in HRTPA often rely on static, predefined hyperparameters. However, in practice, human fatigue sensitivity varies daily due to factors such as changed work conditions and insufficient sleep. To better capture this uncertainty, we treat fatigue-related parameters as inaccurate and estimate them online based on observed fatigue progression during production. To address these challenges, we propose PF-CD3Q, a safe reinforcement learning (safe RL) approach that integrates the particle filter with constrained dueling double deep Q-learning for real-time fatigue-predictive HRTPA. Specifically, we first develop PF-based estimators to track human fatigue and update fatigue model parameters in real-time. These estimators are then integrated into CD3Q by making task-level fatigue predictions during decision-making and excluding tasks that exceed fatigue limits, thereby constraining the action space and formulating the problem as a constrained Markov decision process (CMDP).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于在线滤波的安全强化学习在生产中用于疲劳预测的人机任务规划与分配
人机协同制造作为工业5.0的核心要素，强调通过人机工程学提升劳动者福祉。本文研究动态人机任务规划与分配问题，旨在确定任务执行时机与执行主体，以在确保劳动者生理疲劳处于安全限值内的同时实现效率最大化。疲劳约束与生产动态性的结合显著增加了该问题的复杂性。传统人机任务规划中的疲劳恢复模型常依赖静态预定义超参数，然而实践中，人类疲劳敏感性会因工作条件变化、睡眠不足等因素产生日间波动。为更好捕捉这种不确定性，我们将疲劳相关参数视为不精确量，并基于生产过程中观测到的疲劳进展进行在线估计。针对这些挑战，我们提出PF-CD3Q——一种融合粒子滤波与约束对决双深度Q学习的安全强化学习方法，用于实时疲劳预测的人机任务规划。具体而言，我们首先开发基于粒子滤波的估计器来追踪人体疲劳状态并实时更新疲劳模型参数；随后将这些估计器集成至CD3Q框架中，通过在决策时进行任务级疲劳预测、排除超限任务来约束动作空间，从而将问题构建为约束马尔可夫决策过程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance worker well-being in Industry 5.0 human-robot collaboration, this paper tackles the dynamic task planning and allocation problem under uncertain human fatigue constraints. The method introduces PF-CD3Q, a safe reinforcement learning approach that integrates particle filters for real-time fatigue parameter estimation with constrained dueling double deep Q-learning to predict fatigue and exclude unsafe tasks, formulating the problem as a constrained Markov decision process. Experimental results demonstrate that the approach effectively manages production efficiency while keeping physical fatigue within safe limits by dynamically adapting to daily variations in human fatigue sensitivity.
本文的动机是在工业5.0人机协作中提升工人福祉，解决动态任务规划与分配问题，同时应对不确定的人体疲劳约束。方法上提出了PF-CD3Q，这是一种安全强化学习方法，结合粒子滤波器实时估计疲劳参数，并利用约束对决双深度Q学习来预测疲劳、排除不安全任务，将问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程。实验结果表明，该方法能通过动态适应人体疲劳敏感性的日常变化，有效维持生产效率，同时确保身体疲劳保持在安全限度内。
Towards Bridging the Reward-Generation Gap in Direct Alignment Algorithms
Authors: Zeguan Xiao, Yun Chen, Guanhua Chen, Ke Tang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-06-11T07:02:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:26:13+00:00
Comments: Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Direct Alignment Algorithms (DAAs), such as Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) and Simple Preference Optimization (SimPO), have emerged as efficient alternatives to Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) algorithms for aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences. However, DAAs suffer from a fundamental limitation we identify as the "reward-generation gap", a discrepancy between training objectives and autoregressive decoding dynamics. In this paper, we consider that one contributor to the reward-generation gap is the mismatch between the inherent importance of prefix tokens during the LLM generation process and how this importance is reflected in the implicit reward functions of DAAs. To bridge the gap, we adopt a token-level MDP perspective of DAAs to analyze its limitations and introduce a simple yet effective approach called Prefix-Oriented Equal-length Training (POET), which truncates both preferred and dispreferred responses to match the shorter one's length. We conduct experiments with DPO and SimPO, two representative DAAs, demonstrating that POET improves over their standard implementations, achieving up to 11.8 points in AlpacaEval 2 and overall improvements across downstream tasks. These results underscore the need to mitigate the reward-generation gap in DAAs by better aligning training objectives with autoregressive decoding dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：弥合直接对齐算法中奖励-生成差距的探索
直接对齐算法（如直接偏好优化和简单偏好优化）已成为替代基于人类反馈的强化学习算法的高效方案，用于使大语言模型与人类偏好对齐。然而，这类算法存在一个根本性局限——我们称之为“奖励-生成差距”，即训练目标与自回归解码动态之间的不一致。本文认为，导致该差距的因素之一在于大语言模型生成过程中前缀词元的内在重要性，与其在直接对齐算法隐式奖励函数中的体现方式存在错配。为弥合此差距，我们采用词元级马尔可夫决策过程视角分析直接对齐算法的局限性，并提出一种简洁有效的方法——前缀导向等长训练。该方法通过截断偏好与非偏好响应至较短者长度实现对齐。我们在两种代表性直接对齐算法上的实验表明，该方法较标准实现获得显著提升，在AlpacaEval 2评测中最高提升11.8分，并在下游任务中取得全面改进。这些结果凸显了通过更好对齐训练目标与自回归解码动态来缓解奖励-生成差距的必要性。
Summary / 总结
This paper identifies a fundamental limitation in Direct Alignment Algorithms (DAAs) like DPO and SimPO, termed the "reward-generation gap," which arises from a mismatch between training objectives and the autoregressive decoding dynamics of large language models, particularly regarding how prefix token importance is reflected in implicit reward functions. To address this, the authors adopt a token-level Markov Decision Process perspective and propose a simple method called Prefix-Oriented Equal-length Training (POET), which truncates both preferred and dispreferred responses to the length of the shorter one during training. Experimental results with DPO and SimPO show that POET improves performance, achieving gains of up to 11.8 points on AlpacaEval 2 and consistent improvements across various downstream tasks, highlighting the importance of aligning training objectives with decoding dynamics to mitigate the reward-generation gap.
本文指出了直接对齐算法（如DPO和SimPO）存在的一个根本性局限，即“奖励-生成差距”，这源于训练目标与大型语言模型自回归解码动态之间的不匹配，特别是在前缀令牌重要性如何反映在隐式奖励函数方面。为解决此问题，作者采用令牌级马尔可夫决策过程视角，并提出了一种简单有效的方法称为前缀导向等长训练（POET），该方法在训练时将偏好和非偏好响应都截断至较短响应的长度。在DPO和SimPO上的实验结果表明，POET提升了性能，在AlpacaEval 2上取得了高达11.8分的增益，并在多个下游任务中实现了一致性改进，强调了通过更好对齐训练目标与解码动态来缓解奖励-生成差距的必要性。
Safe Reinforcement Learning using Action Projection: Safeguard the Policy or the Environment?
Authors: Hannah Markgraf, Shambhuraj Sawant, Hanna Krasowski, Lukas Schäfer, Sebastien Gros, Matthias Althoff
First: 2025-09-16T08:56:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:25:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Projection-based safety filters, which modify unsafe actions by mapping them to the closest safe alternative, are widely used to enforce safety constraints in reinforcement learning (RL). Two integration strategies are commonly considered: Safe environment RL (SE-RL), where the safeguard is treated as part of the environment, and safe policy RL (SP-RL), where it is embedded within the policy through differentiable optimization layers. Despite their practical relevance in safety-critical settings, a formal understanding of their differences is lacking. In this work, we present a theoretical comparison of SE-RL and SP-RL. We identify a key distinction in how each approach is affected by action aliasing, a phenomenon in which multiple unsafe actions are projected to the same safe action, causing information loss in the policy gradients. In SE-RL, this effect is implicitly approximated by the critic, while in SP-RL, it manifests directly as rank-deficient Jacobians during backpropagation through the safeguard. Our contributions are threefold: (i) a unified formalization of SE-RL and SP-RL in the context of actor-critic algorithms, (ii) a theoretical analysis of their respective policy gradient estimates, highlighting the role of action aliasing, and (iii) a comparative study of mitigation strategies, including a novel penalty-based improvement for SP-RL that aligns with established SE-RL practices. Empirical results support our theoretical predictions, showing that action aliasing is more detrimental for SP-RL than for SE-RL. However, with appropriate improvement strategies, SP-RL can match or outperform improved SE-RL across a range of environments. These findings provide actionable insights for choosing and refining projection-based safe RL methods based on task characteristics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动作投影的安全强化学习：保护策略还是环境？
基于投影的安全过滤器通过将不安全动作映射至最近的安全替代动作来修改不安全动作，被广泛用于强化学习中强制执行安全约束。常见有两种集成策略：安全环境强化学习（SE-RL）将安全机制视为环境的一部分，而安全策略强化学习（SP-RL）则通过可微分优化层将其嵌入策略内部。尽管在安全关键场景中具有实际意义，但对其差异缺乏形式化理解。本文对SE-RL和SP-RL进行了理论比较，发现两种方法在动作别名现象影响上存在关键差异——该现象指多个不安全动作被投影至同一安全动作，导致策略梯度信息丢失。在SE-RL中，该效应由评论家隐式近似；而在SP-RL中，则通过安全机制反向传播时直接表现为秩亏缺雅可比矩阵。我们的贡献包括：（1）在行动者-评论家算法框架下对SE-RL和SP-RL进行统一形式化；（2）通过理论分析揭示动作别名在各自策略梯度估计中的作用；（3）比较缓解策略并提出SP-RL的新型基于惩罚的改进方法，使其与成熟SE-RL实践对齐。实证结果支持理论预测：动作别名对SP-RL的损害大于SE-RL，但采用适当改进策略后，SP-RL能在多种环境中达到或超越改进版SE-RL。这些发现为根据任务特性选择和完善基于投影的安全强化学习方法提供了可操作的见解。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates two strategies for integrating projection-based safety filters into reinforcement learning (RL) to enforce safety constraints: safe environment RL (SE-RL), where the safeguard is part of the environment, and safe policy RL (SP-RL), where it is embedded within the policy. The motivation is to formally understand their differences, particularly regarding the impact of action aliasing, where multiple unsafe actions map to the same safe action, causing information loss in policy gradients. The method involves a unified formalization of both approaches in actor-critic algorithms, a theoretical analysis of their policy gradient estimates, and a comparative study of mitigation strategies, including a novel penalty-based improvement for SP-RL. Experimental results confirm that action aliasing is more detrimental to SP-RL, but with appropriate improvements, SP-RL can match or outperform enhanced SE-RL across various environments.
本文研究了将基于投影的安全过滤器集成到强化学习（RL）中以强制执行安全约束的两种策略：安全环境RL（SE-RL），其中安全防护是环境的一部分；以及安全策略RL（SP-RL），其中安全防护通过可优化层嵌入策略内部。研究动机是正式理解两者的差异，特别是关于动作别名（即多个不安全动作映射到同一安全动作，导致策略梯度信息丢失）的影响。方法包括在行动者-评论家算法中对两种方法进行统一形式化、对其策略梯度估计进行理论分析，以及对缓解策略进行比较研究，包括为SP-RL提出一种新颖的基于惩罚的改进方法。实验结果证实，动作别名对SP-RL的损害更大，但通过适当改进，SP-RL可以在多种环境中匹配或超越改进后的SE-RL。
Wasserstein Formulation of Reinforcement Learning. An Optimal Transport Perspective on Policy Optimization
Authors: Mathias Dus
First: 2026-04-16T08:24:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:24:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a geometric framework for Reinforcement Learning (RL) that views policies as maps into the Wasserstein space of action probabilities. First, we define a Riemannian structure induced by stationary distributions, proving its existence in a general context. We then define the tangent space of policies and characterize the geodesics, specifically addressing the measurability of vector fields mapped from the state space to the tangent space of probability measures over the action space. Next, we formulate a general RL optimization problem and construct a gradient flow using Otto's calculus. We compute the gradient and the Hessian of the energy, providing a formal second-order analysis. Finally, we illustrate the method with numerical examples for low-dimensional problems, computing the gradient directly from our theoretical formalism. For high-dimensional problems, we parameterize the policy using a neural network and optimize it based on an ergodic approximation of the cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习的Wasserstein表述：策略优化的最优传输视角
本文提出一种强化学习的几何框架，将策略视为映射到动作概率Wasserstein空间的函数。首先，我们定义了由稳态分布诱导的黎曼结构，并在一般性背景下证明其存在性。随后定义了策略的切空间并刻画了测地线，特别解决了从状态空间映射到动作空间概率测度切空间的向量场可测性问题。接着，我们构建了通用的强化学习优化问题，并利用Otto微积分构造梯度流。通过计算能量的梯度和Hessian矩阵，提供了形式化的二阶分析。最后，我们以低维问题的数值算例演示该方法，直接从理论形式体系计算梯度。针对高维问题，我们采用神经网络参数化策略，并基于代价函数的遍历近似进行优化。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a geometric framework for reinforcement learning by viewing policies as maps into the Wasserstein space of action probabilities, motivated by the need for a structured, optimal transport perspective on policy optimization. The method establishes a Riemannian structure via stationary distributions, defines policy tangent spaces and geodesics, and formulates a gradient flow using Otto's calculus, including gradient and Hessian computations for second-order analysis. Experimental results demonstrate the approach through numerical examples on low-dimensional problems, where gradients are computed directly from the theory, and on high-dimensional problems, where a neural network parameterization is optimized using an ergodic cost approximation.
本文提出了一种强化学习的几何框架，将策略视为映射到动作概率的Wasserstein空间，其动机是从最优传输视角为策略优化提供结构化方法。该方法通过平稳分布建立黎曼结构，定义策略的切空间和测地线，并利用奥托微积分构建梯度流，包括能量的梯度和海森矩阵计算以进行二阶分析。实验结果表明，该方法在低维问题上通过理论形式直接计算梯度进行了数值示例验证，并在高维问题上使用神经网络参数化策略，并基于成本的遍历近似进行优化。
One Step is Enough: Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning based on One-Step Policy Optimization for Order Dispatch on Ride-Sharing Platforms
Authors: Zijian Zhao, Sen Li
First: 2025-07-21T08:04:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T08:13:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Order dispatch is a critical task in ride-sharing systems with Autonomous Vehicles (AVs), directly influencing efficiency and profits. Recently, Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) has emerged as a promising solution to this problem by decomposing the large state and action spaces among individual agents, effectively addressing the Curse of Dimensionality (CoD) in transportation market, which is caused by the substantial number of vehicles, passengers, and orders. However, conventional MARL-based approaches heavily rely on accurate estimation of the value function, which becomes problematic in large-scale, highly uncertain environments. To address this issue, we propose two novel methods that bypass value function estimation, leveraging the homogeneous property of AV fleets. First, we draw an analogy between AV fleets and groups in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), adapting it to the order dispatch task. By replacing the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) baseline with the group average reward-to-go, GRPO eliminates critic estimation errors and reduces training bias. Inspired by this baseline replacement, we further propose One-Step Policy Optimization (OSPO), demonstrating that the optimal policy can be trained using only one-step group rewards under a homogeneous fleet. Experiments on a real-world ride-hailing dataset show that both GRPO and OSPO achieve promising performance across all scenarios, efficiently optimizing pickup times and the number of served orders using simple Multilayer Perceptron (MLP) networks. Furthermore, OSPO outperforms GRPO in all scenarios, attributed to its elimination of bias caused by the bounded time horizon of GRPO. Our code, trained models, and processed data are provided at https://github.com/RS2002/OSPO .
中文标题/摘要
标题：一步足矣：基于一步策略优化的多智能体强化学习在网约车平台订单调度中的应用
订单调度是自动驾驶车辆（AV）网约车系统中的关键任务，直接影响效率和利润。近年来，多智能体强化学习（MARL）通过将庞大的状态和动作空间分解至个体智能体，有效应对了由大量车辆、乘客和订单引发的交通市场维度灾难（CoD），成为该问题的潜力解决方案。然而，传统基于MARL的方法严重依赖价值函数的精确估计，这在规模庞大、高度不确定的环境中存在问题。为解决此问题，我们提出两种绕过价值函数估计的新方法，利用自动驾驶车队的同质特性。首先，我们将自动驾驶车队类比为组相对策略优化（GRPO）中的群组，并将其适配至订单调度任务。通过用群组平均未来收益替代近端策略优化（PPO）基线，GRPO消除了评论者估计误差并减少了训练偏差。受此基线替换启发，我们进一步提出一步策略优化（OSPO），证明在同质车队条件下仅需单步群组收益即可训练最优策略。基于真实网约车数据集的实验表明，GRPO和OSPO在所有场景中均取得优异性能，仅使用简单多层感知机（MLP）网络即可高效优化接载时间和完成订单数。此外，OSPO因消除了GRPO有限时间范围导致的偏差，在所有场景中均优于GRPO。代码、训练模型及处理数据已发布于https://github.com/RS2002/OSPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of order dispatch in ride-sharing systems with autonomous vehicles, where traditional multi-agent reinforcement learning methods suffer from value function estimation errors in large-scale uncertain environments. The authors propose two novel methods that bypass value function estimation by leveraging fleet homogeneity: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), which adapts group-based policy optimization to replace the PPO baseline with group average reward-to-go, and One-Step Policy Optimization (OSPO), which demonstrates that optimal policies can be trained using only one-step group rewards. Experiments on real-world ride-hailing data show that both methods achieve promising performance in optimizing pickup times and served orders using simple MLP networks, with OSPO outperforming GRPO by eliminating bias from bounded time horizons.
本文针对共享出行系统中自动驾驶车辆的订单调度问题，传统多智能体强化学习方法在大规模不确定环境中存在价值函数估计误差的挑战。作者提出了两种绕过价值函数估计的新方法，利用车队同质性：群体相对策略优化（GRPO）将基于群体的策略优化应用于订单调度，用群体平均未来奖励替代PPO基线；以及一步策略优化（OSPO），证明在同质车队下仅需一步群体奖励即可训练最优策略。在真实网约车数据集上的实验表明，两种方法均使用简单的多层感知机网络，在优化接载时间和完成订单数方面表现良好，其中OSPO通过消除GRPO有限时间范围引起的偏差，在所有场景中表现更优。
RELOAD: A Robust and Efficient Learned Query Optimizer for Database Systems
Authors: Seokwon Lee, Jaeyoung Sim, Sihyun Kim, Yuhsing Li, Yiwen Zhu, Kwanghyun Park
First: 2026-04-16T07:35:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T07:35:05+00:00
Comments: This work is currently under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in query optimization have shifted from traditional rule-based and cost-based techniques towards machine learning-driven approaches. Among these, reinforcement learning (RL) has attracted significant attention due to its ability to optimize long-term performance by learning policies over query planning. However, existing RL-based query optimizers often exhibit unstable performance at the level of individual queries, including severe performance regressions, and require prolonged training to reach the plan quality of expert, cost-based optimizers. These shortcomings make learned query optimizers difficult to deploy in practice and remain a major barrier to their adoption in production database systems. To address these challenges, we present RELOAD, a robust and efficient learned query optimizer for database systems. RELOAD focuses on (i) robustness, by minimizing query-level performance regressions and ensuring consistent optimization behavior across executions, and (ii) efficiency, by accelerating convergence to expert-level plan quality. Through extensive experiments on standard benchmarks, including Join Order Benchmark, TPC-DS, and Star Schema Benchmark, RELOAD demonstrates up to 2.4x higher robustness and 3.1x greater efficiency compared to state-of-the-art RL-based query optimization techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RELOAD：一种面向数据库系统的鲁棒高效学习型查询优化器
查询优化领域的最新进展正从传统的基于规则和基于成本的技术转向机器学习驱动的方法。其中，强化学习因其能通过学习查询规划策略来优化长期性能而备受关注。然而，现有的基于强化学习的查询优化器在单查询层面常表现出性能不稳定，包括严重的性能退化，且需要长时间训练才能达到专家级基于成本优化器的计划质量。这些缺陷使得学习型查询优化器难以实际部署，成为其在生产数据库系统中应用的主要障碍。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了RELOAD——一种面向数据库系统的鲁棒高效学习型查询优化器。RELOAD聚焦于：（一）鲁棒性，通过最小化查询级性能退化并确保跨执行过程优化行为的一致性；（二）高效性，通过加速收敛至专家级计划质量。通过在Join Order Benchmark、TPC-DS和Star Schema Benchmark等标准基准上的大量实验，RELOAD相较于最先进的基于强化学习的查询优化技术，展现出高达2.4倍的鲁棒性提升和3.1倍的效率提升。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the instability and slow convergence of existing reinforcement learning-based query optimizers, which suffer from severe performance regressions and prolonged training times, hindering their practical deployment. The proposed method, RELOAD, introduces a robust and efficient learned query optimizer that specifically targets minimizing query-level performance regressions and accelerating convergence to expert-level plan quality. Experimental results on benchmarks such as Join Order Benchmark, TPC-DS, and Star Schema Benchmark show that RELOAD achieves up to 2.4 times higher robustness and 3.1 times greater efficiency compared to state-of-the-art RL-based techniques.
本研究的动机源于现有基于强化学习的查询优化器存在性能不稳定和收敛缓慢的问题，包括严重的性能回归和训练时间长，阻碍了其实际部署。提出的方法RELOAD是一种鲁棒且高效的查询优化器，专注于最小化查询级性能回归并加速收敛至专家级计划质量。在Join Order Benchmark、TPC-DS和Star Schema Benchmark等标准基准测试中的实验结果表明，与最先进的基于强化学习的技术相比，RELOAD实现了高达2.4倍的鲁棒性提升和3.1倍的效率提升。
Mean Flow Policy Optimization
Authors: Xiaoyi Dong, Xi Sheryl Zhang, Jian Cheng
First: 2026-04-16T06:59:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T06:59:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Diffusion models have recently emerged as expressive policy representations for online reinforcement learning (RL). However, their iterative generative processes introduce substantial training and inference overhead. To overcome this limitation, we propose to represent policies using MeanFlow models, a class of few-step flow-based generative models, to improve training and inference efficiency over diffusion-based RL approaches. To promote exploration, we optimize MeanFlow policies under the maximum entropy RL framework via soft policy iteration, and address two key challenges specific to MeanFlow policies: action likelihood evaluation and soft policy improvement. Experiments on MuJoCo and DeepMind Control Suite benchmarks demonstrate that our method, Mean Flow Policy Optimization (MFPO), achieves performance comparable to or exceeding current diffusion-based baselines while considerably reducing training and inference time. Our code is available at https://github.com/MFPolicy/MFPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：均值流策略优化
扩散模型近期作为在线强化学习的表达性策略表示方法崭露头角，但其迭代生成过程带来了显著的训练与推理开销。为克服此限制，我们提出采用均值流模型——一类基于流的少步生成模型——来表示策略，以提升基于扩散的强化学习方法的训练与推理效率。为促进探索，我们在最大熵强化学习框架下通过软策略迭代优化均值流策略，并解决了均值流策略特有的两个关键挑战：动作似然评估与软策略改进。在MuJoCo和DeepMind Control Suite基准测试上的实验表明，我们的方法——均值流策略优化（MFPO）——在显著减少训练与推理时间的同时，取得了与当前基于扩散的基线方法相当或更优的性能。代码发布于https://github.com/MFPolicy/MFPO。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of diffusion-based policies in reinforcement learning, this paper introduces Mean Flow Policy Optimization (MFPO) to improve efficiency. The method employs MeanFlow models, a few-step flow-based generative model, as the policy representation and optimizes them under a maximum entropy framework using a tailored soft policy iteration that addresses action likelihood evaluation and policy improvement challenges. Experimental results on MuJoCo and DeepMind Control Suite benchmarks show that MFPO achieves performance comparable to or better than diffusion-based baselines while significantly reducing both training and inference time.
本文针对基于扩散模型的强化学习策略计算成本高的问题，提出了均值流策略优化（MFPO）以提高效率。该方法采用均值流模型（一种少步长的基于流的生成模型）作为策略表示，并在最大熵框架下通过专门设计的软策略迭代进行优化，解决了动作似然评估和策略改进的挑战。在MuJoCo和DeepMind Control Suite基准测试中的实验结果表明，MFPO实现了与基于扩散的基线方法相当或更优的性能，同时显著减少了训练和推理时间。
SPaCe: Unlocking Sample-Efficient Large Language Models Training With Self-Pace Curriculum Learning
Authors: Dai Do, Manh Nguyen, Svetha Venkatesh, Hung Le
First: 2025-08-07T03:50:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T06:15:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong reasoning capabilities when fine-tuned with reinforcement learning (RL). However, such methods require extensive data and compute, making them impractical under many realistic training budgets. Many existing pipelines sample training examples uniformly across steps or epochs, ignoring differences in difficulty, redundancy, and learning value, which slows learning and wastes computation. We propose \textbf{SPaCe}, a self-paced learning framework that enables efficient learning based on the capability of the model being trained through optimizing which data to use and when. First, we apply \emph{cluster-based data reduction} to partition training data by semantics and difficulty, extracting a compact yet diverse subset that reduces redundancy. Then, a \textit{multi-armed bandit} treats data clusters as arms, allocating training samples based on the model's solve rates and learning progress. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks show that SPaCe achieves comparable or better accuracy than state-of-the-art baselines while using up to \(100\times\) fewer samples. Ablation studies and analyses further highlight the importance of both data clustering and adaptive selection. Our results demonstrate that carefully curated, performance-driven training curricula can unlock strong reasoning abilities in LLMs with minimal resources.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPaCe：通过自步课程学习解锁样本高效的大型语言模型训练
大型语言模型（LLM）在使用强化学习（RL）进行微调时展现出强大的推理能力，但此类方法需要大量数据和计算资源，在许多实际训练预算下难以实现。现有流程通常均匀采样训练样本，忽略了难度、冗余度和学习价值的差异，导致学习效率低下和计算浪费。本文提出SPaCe，一种自步学习框架，通过优化数据使用时机和选择策略，实现基于模型当前能力的高效训练。该框架首先采用基于聚类的数据缩减技术，依据语义和难度划分训练数据，提取紧凑而多样的子集以降低冗余；随后通过多臂老虎机机制将数据簇视为臂，根据模型解题率和学习进度动态分配训练样本。在多个推理基准测试中，SPaCe仅使用最多百分之一的样本量即可达到或超越现有最优基线的准确率。消融实验进一步验证了数据聚类与自适应选择机制的关键作用。研究表明，精心设计的性能驱动型训练课程能以最小资源激发LLM的强推理能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational and data demands of fine-tuning large language models (LLMs) with reinforcement learning, which often involves uniform and inefficient data sampling, this paper introduces SPaCe, a self-paced curriculum learning framework designed to enhance sample efficiency. The method first applies cluster-based data reduction to partition training data by semantics and difficulty, creating a compact and diverse subset, and then uses a multi-armed bandit algorithm to adaptively allocate training samples based on the model's real-time solve rates and learning progress. Experimental results on multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that SPaCe achieves accuracy comparable to or better than state-of-the-art baselines while using up to 100 times fewer training samples, with ablations confirming the importance of both clustering and adaptive selection for unlocking strong reasoning abilities with minimal resources.
针对使用强化学习微调大语言模型时计算和数据需求高、且通常采用均匀低效数据采样的问题，本文提出了SPaCe这一自步课程学习框架，旨在提升样本效率。该方法首先通过基于聚类的数据缩减，依据语义和难度对训练数据进行分区，构建一个紧凑而多样的子集；随后采用多臂老虎机算法，根据模型实时解题率和学习进度自适应地分配训练样本。在多个推理基准上的实验结果表明，SPaCe在使用多达100倍更少训练样本的情况下，达到了与最先进基线相当或更好的准确率，消融研究进一步验证了数据聚类和自适应选择对于以最小资源激发强大推理能力的重要性。
Targeted Exploration via Unified Entropy Control for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chen Wang, Lai Wei, Yanzhi Zhang, Chenyang Shao, Zedong Dan, Weiran Huang, Ge Lan, Yue Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-16T05:52:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T05:52:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication in Findings of the 64th Annual Meeting of the Association for Computational Linguistics (ACL 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advances in reinforcement learning (RL) have improved the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs). However, the widely used Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) consistently suffers from entropy collapse, causing the policy to converge prematurely and lose diversity. Existing exploration methods introduce additional bias or variance during exploration, making it difficult to maintain optimization stability. We propose Unified Entropy Control for Reinforcement Learning (UEC-RL), a framework that provides targeted mechanisms for exploration and stabilization. UEC-RL activates more exploration on difficult prompts to search for potential and valuable reasoning trajectories. In parallel, a stabilizer prevents entropy from growing uncontrollably, thereby keeping training stable as the model consolidates reliable behaviors. Together, these components expand the search space when needed while maintaining robust optimization throughout training. Experiments on both LLM and VLM reasoning tasks show consistent gains over RL baselines on both Pass@1 and Pass@$k$. On Geometry3K, UEC-RL achieves a 37.9\% relative improvement over GRPO, indicating that it sustains effective exploration without compromising convergence and underscoring UEC-RL as a key for scaling RL-based reasoning in large models. Our code is available at https://github.com/597358816/UEC-RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习的统一熵调控定向探索方法
强化学习（RL）的最新进展提升了大型语言模型（LLM）和视觉语言模型（VLM）的推理能力。然而，广泛使用的组相对策略优化（GRPO）持续面临熵崩溃问题，导致策略过早收敛并丧失多样性。现有探索方法在探索过程中会引入额外偏差或方差，难以维持优化稳定性。我们提出强化学习的统一熵控制框架（UEC-RL），该框架为探索与稳定化提供了定向机制。UEC-RL在困难提示上激活更多探索，以搜寻潜在且有价值的推理轨迹；同时，稳定器防止熵无限增长，从而在模型巩固可靠行为时保持训练稳定性。这些组件协同工作，在必要时扩展搜索空间，并在整个训练过程中保持稳健优化。在LLM和VLM推理任务上的实验表明，UEC-RL在Pass@1和Pass@$k$指标上均持续优于RL基线方法。在Geometry3K数据集上，UEC-RL相较GRPO实现了37.9%的相对提升，这表明其能在不损害收敛性的前提下维持有效探索，凸显了UEC-RL作为大规模模型基于RL的推理扩展关键技术的重要性。代码已开源：https://github.com/597358816/UEC-RL。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the entropy collapse issue in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for reinforcement learning, which leads to premature convergence and loss of policy diversity, while existing exploration methods often introduce instability. The proposed method, Unified Entropy Control for Reinforcement Learning (UEC-RL), introduces a targeted framework that activates enhanced exploration on difficult prompts to discover valuable reasoning trajectories and employs a stabilizer to prevent uncontrolled entropy growth, thereby maintaining training stability. Main experimental results on LLM and VLM reasoning tasks demonstrate consistent improvements over RL baselines in Pass@1 and Pass@k metrics, with a notable 37.9% relative gain over GRPO on Geometry3K, showing that UEC-RL sustains effective exploration without compromising convergence.

Asking What Matters: Reward-Driven Clarification for Software Engineering Tasks
Authors: Sanidhya Vijayvargiya, Vijay Viswanathan, Graham Neubig
First: 2026-04-16T05:11:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T05:11:02+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humans often specify tasks incompletely, so assistants must know when and how to ask clarifying questions. However, effective clarification remains challenging in software engineering tasks as not all missing information is equally valuable, and questions must target information users can realistically provide. We study clarification in real software engineering tasks by quantifying which types of information most affect task success and which questions elicit useful responses from simulated users. Using Shapley attribution and distributional comparisons, we identify two key properties of effective clarification: task relevance (which information predicts success) and user answerability (what users can realistically provide). We operationalize these properties as multi-stage reinforcement learning rewards to train CLARITI, an 8B-parameter clarification module, that matches GPT-5's resolution rate on underspecified issues while generating 41% fewer questions. Our results suggest that grounding reward design in empirical analysis of information impact and user answerability improves clarification efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：询问关键问题：面向软件工程任务的奖励驱动式澄清机制
人类常以不完整的方式描述任务，因此助手需掌握何时及如何提出澄清问题。然而在软件工程任务中，有效澄清仍具挑战性：并非所有缺失信息都具有同等价值，且问题必须针对用户实际能提供的信息。本研究通过量化分析，探究哪些信息类型对任务成功影响最大，以及哪些问题能从模拟用户处获得有效回应。运用沙普利归因与分布比较方法，我们识别出有效澄清的两大关键属性：任务相关性（可预测成功的信息）与用户可答性（用户实际能提供的信息）。我们将这些属性转化为多阶段强化学习奖励机制，训练出包含80亿参数的CLARITI澄清模块。该模块在未充分说明问题的解决率上与GPT-5持平，同时将提问数量减少41%。研究表明，基于信息影响与用户可答性的实证分析来设计奖励机制，能有效提升澄清效率。

The paper addresses the challenge of effectively asking clarifying questions in software engineering tasks, where human specifications are often incomplete. The motivation stems from the need to identify which missing information is most valuable for task success and what users can realistically provide. The method involves using Shapley attribution and distributional comparisons to quantify task relevance and user answerability, then operationalizing these as multi-stage reinforcement learning rewards to train CLARITI, an 8B-parameter clarification module. Experimental results show that CLARITI matches GPT-5's resolution rate on underspecified issues while generating 41% fewer questions, demonstrating improved clarification efficiency through empirically grounded reward design.
本文针对软件工程任务中如何有效提出澄清性问题展开研究，因为人类给出的任务描述往往不完整。研究动机在于需要识别哪些缺失信息对任务成功最关键，以及用户实际能提供什么。方法上，通过Shapley归因和分布比较来量化任务相关性和用户可答性，并将其作为多阶段强化学习奖励来训练CLARITI（一个80亿参数的澄清模块）。实验结果表明，CLARITI在处理不明确问题时与GPT-5的解决率相当，但生成的问题数量减少了41%，这表明基于信息影响和用户可答性的实证分析来设计奖励能提高澄清效率。
Do Not Step Into the Same River Twice: Learning to Reason from Trial and Error
Authors: Chenming Tang, Hsiu-Yuan Huang, Weijie Liu, Clive Bai, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-10-30T03:36:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T04:58:10+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (main conference)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly boosted the reasoning capability of language models (LMs). However, existing RLVR approaches train LMs based on their own on-policy responses and are constrained by the initial capability of LMs, thus prone to exploration stagnation, in which LMs fail to solve more training problems and cannot further learn from the training data. Some approaches try to address this by leveraging off-policy solutions to training problems, but rely on external expert guidance that is limited in availability and scalability. In this work, we propose LTE (Learning to reason from Trial and Error), an approach that hints LMs with their previously self-made mistakes, not requiring any external expert guidance. Experiments validate the effectiveness of LTE, which outperforms the normal group relative policy optimization (GRPO) by 5.02 in Pass@1 and 9.96 in Pass@k on average across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks for Qwen3-8B-Base and even performs better than methods that require external guidance. Further analysis confirms that LTE successfully mitigates exploration stagnation and enhances both exploitation and exploration during training. Our code is available at https://github.com/JamyDon/LTE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：勿重蹈覆辙：从试错中学习推理
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了语言模型（LMs）的推理能力。然而，现有RLVR方法基于语言模型自身的同策略响应进行训练，受限于语言模型的初始能力，容易陷入探索停滞，即语言模型无法解决更多训练问题，也无法从训练数据中进一步学习。部分方法尝试通过利用训练问题的异策略解来解决此问题，但依赖于外部专家指导，其可用性和可扩展性有限。本研究提出LTE（从试错中学习推理），该方法通过提示语言模型其先前自身所犯错误来引导学习，无需任何外部专家指导。实验验证了LTE的有效性：在六个数学推理基准测试中，Qwen3-8B-Base模型使用LTE在Pass@1和Pass@k上平均分别比常规组相对策略优化（GRPO）高出5.02和9.96，甚至优于需要外部指导的方法。进一步分析证实，LTE成功缓解了探索停滞，并增强了训练过程中的利用与探索。代码已开源：https://github.com/JamyDon/LTE。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the issue of exploration stagnation in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for language models, where models are limited by their own on-policy responses and initial capabilities, hindering further learning. The authors propose LTE (Learning to reason from Trial and Error), a method that enables language models to learn from their own past mistakes without relying on external expert guidance. Experimental results across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that LTE outperforms standard group relative policy optimization (GRPO) by 5.02 in Pass@1 and 9.96 in Pass@k on average for Qwen3-8B-Base, even surpassing methods that require external guidance, while analysis confirms it mitigates exploration stagnation and enhances both exploitation and exploration during training.
本文针对语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中的探索停滞问题展开研究，该问题源于模型受限于自身策略响应和初始能力，阻碍了进一步学习。作者提出了LTE（从试错中学习推理）方法，使语言模型能够从自身过往错误中学习，无需依赖外部专家指导。在六个数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，LTE在Qwen3-8B-Base模型上平均比标准组相对策略优化方法在Pass@1和Pass@k指标上分别提升5.02和9.96，甚至优于需要外部指导的方法，分析进一步证实LTE有效缓解了探索停滞，并增强了训练过程中的利用与探索能力。
Large Language Model Post-Training: A Unified View of Off-Policy and On-Policy Learning
Authors: Shiwan Zhao, Zhihu Wang, Xuyang Zhao, Jiaming Zhou, Caiyue Xu, Chenfei Liu, Liting Zhang, Yuhang Jia, Yanzhe Zhang, Hualong Yu, Zichen Xu, Qicheng Li, Yong Qin
First: 2026-04-09T08:00:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T04:43:04+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 1 figure, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training has become central to turning pretrained large language models (LLMs) into aligned, capable, and deployable systems. Recent progress spans supervised fine-tuning (SFT), preference optimization, reinforcement learning (RL), process supervision, verifier-guided methods, distillation, and multi-stage pipelines. Yet these methods are often discussed in fragmented ways, organized by labels or objectives rather than by the behavioral bottlenecks they address. This survey argues that LLM post-training is best understood as structured intervention on model behavior. We organize the field first by trajectory provenance, which defines two primary regimes: off-policy learning on externally supplied trajectories and on-policy learning on learner-generated rollouts. We then interpret methods through two recurring roles -- effective support expansion, which makes useful behaviors more reachable, and policy reshaping, which improves behavior within already reachable regions -- together with a complementary systems-level role, behavioral consolidation, which preserves, transfers, and amortizes useful behavior across stages and model transitions. Under this view, SFT may serve either support expansion or policy reshaping; preference optimization is usually off-policy reshaping, though online variants move closer to learner-generated states. On-policy RL often improves behavior on learner-generated states, but stronger guidance can also make hard-to-reach reasoning paths reachable. Distillation is often better understood as consolidation rather than only compression, and hybrid pipelines emerge as coordinated multi-stage compositions. Overall, the framework helps diagnose post-training bottlenecks and reason about stage composition, suggesting that progress increasingly depends on coordinated systems design rather than any single dominant objective.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型后训练：离策略与在策略学习的统一视角
后训练已成为将预训练大语言模型转化为对齐、可用且可部署系统的核心环节。近期进展涵盖监督微调、偏好优化、强化学习、过程监督、验证器引导方法、蒸馏及多阶段流程。然而这些方法常被零散讨论，按标签或目标而非其解决的行为瓶颈进行组织。本综述主张将LLM后训练理解为对模型行为的结构化干预。我们首先按轨迹来源组织该领域，界定两大主要范式：基于外部提供轨迹的离策略学习，以及基于学习者生成轨迹的在策略学习。进而通过两个反复出现的角色解读方法——有效支持扩展（使有益行为更易达成）与策略重塑（改进已可达区域内的行为），辅以一个互补的系统级角色：行为整合（跨阶段与模型迁移时保留、转移并分摊有益行为）。在此视角下，监督微调可服务于支持扩展或策略重塑；偏好优化通常属于离策略重塑，尽管在线变体更接近学习者生成状态。在策略强化学习常改进学习者生成状态上的行为，但更强引导亦可使难以达成的推理路径变得可达。蒸馏更宜理解为整合而非单纯压缩，混合流程则呈现为协调的多阶段组合。总体而言，该框架有助于诊断后训练瓶颈并推演阶段组合，表明进展日益依赖于协调的系统设计而非单一主导目标。
Summary / 总结
This survey paper aims to unify the fragmented landscape of large language model (LLM) post-training methods by proposing a structured framework based on behavioral intervention. The authors organize existing techniques—such as supervised fine-tuning, preference optimization, and reinforcement learning—into two primary regimes defined by trajectory provenance: off-policy learning on external data and on-policy learning on model-generated rollouts. They further interpret methods through the roles of effective support expansion (making useful behaviors reachable) and policy reshaping (improving existing behaviors), complemented by behavioral consolidation for preserving gains across stages. The main experimental insight, drawn from synthesizing numerous studies, is that this framework helps diagnose performance bottlenecks and reveals that advanced post-training increasingly relies on coordinated multi-stage system design rather than isolated algorithmic objectives.
本综述论文旨在通过提出一个基于行为干预的结构化框架，来统一大型语言模型（LLM）后训练领域中碎片化的方法。作者将现有技术——如监督微调、偏好优化和强化学习——组织成由轨迹来源定义的两个主要体系：基于外部数据的离策略学习和基于模型生成轨迹的在策略学习。他们进一步通过有效支持扩展（使有用行为可达）和策略重塑（改进现有行为）这两个核心角色来阐释各种方法，并辅以行为整合来保持各阶段间的收益。通过对大量研究的综合，主要实验结论表明，该框架有助于诊断性能瓶颈，并揭示先进的后训练日益依赖于协调的多阶段系统设计，而非孤立的算法目标。
MARS$^2$: Scaling Multi-Agent Tree Search via Reinforcement Learning for Code Generation
Authors: Pengfei Li, Shijie Wang, Fangyuan Li, Yikun Fu, Kaifeng Liu, Kaiyan Zhang, Dazhi Zhang, Yuqiang Li, Biqing Qi, Bowen Zhou
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-16T02:52:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T02:52:24+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) paradigms have demonstrated strong performance on reasoning-intensive tasks such as code generation. However, limited trajectory diversity often leads to diminishing returns, which constrains the achievable performance ceiling. Search-enhanced RL alleviates this issue by introducing structured exploration, which remains constrained by the single-agent policy priors. Meanwhile, leveraging multiple interacting policies can acquire more diverse exploratory signals, but existing approaches are typically decoupled from structured search. We propose \textbf{MARS$^2$} (Multi-Agent Reinforced Tree-Search Scaling), a unified RL framework in which multiple independently-optimized agents collaborate within a shared tree-structured search environment. MARS$^2$ models the search tree as a learnable multi-agent interaction environment, enabling heterogeneous agents to collaboratively generate and refine candidate solutions within a shared search topology. To support effective learning, we introduce a path-level group advantage formulation based on tree-consistent reward shaping, which facilitates effective credit assignment across complex search trajectories. Experiments on code generation benchmarks show that MARS$^2$ consistently improves performance across diverse model combinations and training settings, demonstrating the effectiveness of coupling multi-agent collaboration with tree search for enhancing reinforcement learning. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/TsinghuaC3I/MARTI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MARS²：基于强化学习的多智能体树搜索扩展框架用于代码生成
强化学习范式在代码生成等推理密集型任务中展现出优异性能，但轨迹多样性受限常导致收益递减，制约了性能上限。搜索增强型强化学习通过引入结构化探索缓解此问题，但仍受限于单智能体策略先验。多智能体交互策略能获取更丰富的探索信号，但现有方法通常与结构化搜索脱钩。本文提出MARS²（多智能体强化树搜索扩展框架），该统一强化学习框架使多个独立优化的智能体在共享树状搜索环境中协作。MARS²将搜索树建模为可学习的多智能体交互环境，支持异构智能体在共享搜索拓扑中协同生成与优化候选解。为保障有效学习，我们提出基于树一致奖励重塑的路径级群体优势计算机制，促进复杂搜索轨迹间的信用分配。代码生成基准实验表明，MARS²在不同模型组合与训练设置下均能持续提升性能，验证了多智能体协作与树搜索耦合对强化学习的增强效果。代码已开源：https://github.com/TsinghuaC3I/MARTI。

Experimental results on code generation benchmarks show that MARS² consistently improves performance across diverse model combinations and training settings, demonstrating the effectiveness of integrating multi-agent collaboration with tree search.

Learning to Plan, Planning to Learn: Adaptive Hierarchical RL-MPC for Sample-Efficient Decision Making
Authors: Toshiaki Hori, Jonathan DeCastro, Deepak Gopinath, Avinash Balachandran, Guy Rosman
First: 2025-12-18T21:44:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T02:13:06+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 10 figures, 8th Annual Learning for Dynamics & Control Conference (L4DC)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a new approach for solving planning problems with a hierarchical structure, fusing reinforcement learning and MPC planning. Our formulation tightly and elegantly couples the two planning paradigms. It leverages reinforcement learning actions to inform the MPPI sampler, and adaptively aggregates MPPI samples to inform the value estimation. The resulting adaptive process leverages further MPPI exploration where value estimates are uncertain, and improves training robustness and the overall resulting policies. This results in a robust planning approach that can handle complex planning problems and easily adapts to different applications, as demonstrated over several domains, including race driving, modified Acrobot, and Lunar Lander with added obstacles. Our results in these domains show better data efficiency and overall performance in terms of both rewards and task success, with up to a 72% increase in success rate compared to existing approaches, as well as accelerated convergence (x2.1) compared to non-adaptive sampling.

Bayesian Optimization with Gaussian Processes to Accelerate Stationary Point Searches
Authors: Rohit Goswami
First: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-16T00:18:55+00:00
Comments: 65 pages, 24 figures (main). Invited article for ACS Physical Chemistry Au
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Building local surrogates to accelerate stationary point searches on potential energy surfaces spans decades of effort. Done correctly, surrogates can reduce the number of expensive electronic structure evaluations by roughly an order of magnitude while preserving the accuracy of the underlying theory, with the gain depending on oracle cost, search distance, and the availability of analytical forces. We present a unified Bayesian optimization view of minimization, single-point saddle searches, and double-ended path searches: all three share one six-step surrogate loop and differ only in the inner optimization target and the acquisition criterion. The framework uses Gaussian process regression with derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, and we develop optional extensions for production use, including farthest-point sampling with the Earth Mover's Distance, MAP regularization, an adaptive trust radius, and random Fourier features for scaling. Accompanying pedagogical Rust code demonstrates that all three applications use the same Bayesian optimization loop, bridging the gap between theoretical formulation and practical execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的贝叶斯优化加速势能面驻点搜索
构建局部代理模型以加速势能面上的驻点搜索已历经数十年研究。正确实施的代理模型能在保持基础理论精度的同时，将昂贵的电子结构计算量减少约一个数量级，其增益取决于计算成本、搜索距离及解析梯度的可用性。本文提出适用于极小值搜索、单点鞍点搜索和双端点路径搜索的统一贝叶斯优化框架：三者共享六步代理循环，仅在内层优化目标和采集准则上存在差异。该框架采用含导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核函数和主动学习机制，并开发了适用于实际计算的扩展功能，包括基于推土机距离的最远点采样、最大后验正则化、自适应信任域及用于规模扩展的随机傅里叶特征。配套的Rust教学代码证明三类应用共享相同的贝叶斯优化循环，弥合了理论构建与实际执行间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing challenge of efficiently locating stationary points on potential energy surfaces with costly electronic structure calculations, this paper presents a unified Bayesian optimization framework using Gaussian processes to accelerate such searches. The method employs a six-step surrogate loop applicable to minimization, saddle point searches, and path finding, incorporating derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, with extensions like farthest-point sampling and adaptive trust radii for robustness. Experimental results demonstrate that the approach can reduce the number of expensive evaluations by roughly an order of magnitude while maintaining theoretical accuracy, as validated through pedagogical code implementations.
本文针对在势能面上高效搜索驻点需进行昂贵电子结构计算这一长期挑战，提出了一种基于高斯过程的统一贝叶斯优化框架以加速此类搜索。该方法采用适用于极小化、鞍点搜索和路径查找的六步代理循环，结合了导数观测、逆距离核和主动学习，并通过最远点采样和自适应信任半径等扩展提升实用性。实验结果表明，该方法能在保持理论精度的同时，将昂贵计算评估次数减少约一个数量级，相关教学代码也验证了其有效性。
The Specification Trap: Why Static Value Alignment Alone Is Insufficient for Robust Alignment
Authors: Austin Spizzirri
First: 2025-11-19T23:31:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T23:15:00+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, no figures. Version 4. First posted as arXiv:2512.03048 in November 2025. First in a six-paper research program on AI alignment
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Static content-based AI value alignment is insufficient for robust alignment under capability scaling, distributional shift, and increasing autonomy. This holds for any approach that treats alignment as optimizing toward a fixed formal value-object, whether reward function, utility function, constitutional principles, or learned preference representation. Three philosophical results create compounding difficulties: Hume's is-ought gap (behavioral data underdetermines normative content), Berlin's value pluralism (human values resist consistent formalization), and the extended frame problem (any value encoding will misfit future contexts that advanced AI creates). RLHF, Constitutional AI, inverse reinforcement learning, and cooperative assistance games each instantiate this specification trap, and their failure modes reflect structural vulnerabilities, not merely engineering limitations that better data or algorithms will straightforwardly resolve. Known workarounds for individual components face mutually reinforcing difficulties when the specification is closed: the moment it ceases to update from the process it governs. Drawing on compatibilist philosophy, the paper argues that behavioral compliance under training conditions does not guarantee robust alignment under novel conditions, and that this gap grows with system capability. For value-laden autonomous systems, known closed approaches face structural vulnerabilities that worsen with capability. The constructive burden shifts to open, developmentally responsive approaches, though whether such approaches can be achieved remains an empirical question.
中文标题/摘要
标题：规范陷阱：为何仅靠静态价值对齐不足以实现稳健对齐
基于静态内容的AI价值对齐在能力扩展、分布偏移和自主性增强的背景下，不足以实现稳健对齐。这一结论适用于所有将对齐视为向固定形式价值目标（无论是奖励函数、效用函数、宪法原则还是习得偏好表征）优化的方法。三项哲学原理共同构成叠加困境：休谟的实然-应然鸿沟（行为数据无法充分决定规范内容）、伯林的价值多元论（人类价值难以被一致形式化）以及扩展框架问题（任何价值编码都将无法适应先进AI创造的未来情境）。RLHF、宪法AI、逆强化学习和协作辅助博弈均体现了这一规范陷阱，其失效模式反映了结构性脆弱，而非仅靠改进数据或算法即可解决的工程局限。针对单个组件的已知变通方案在规范封闭时面临相互强化的困难——即当规范停止从其所治理的过程中更新时。借鉴相容论哲学，本文论证训练条件下的行为合规无法保证新情境下的稳健对齐，且这一鸿沟随系统能力扩大而加剧。对于承载价值的自主系统，已知的封闭式方法面临随能力增强而恶化的结构性脆弱。建设性责任转向开放、发展响应式方法，但此类方法能否实现仍是实证问题。
Summary / 总结
The paper argues that static, content-based AI value alignment methods are fundamentally insufficient for ensuring robust alignment as AI systems scale in capability, face distributional shifts, and gain autonomy, a problem termed the 'specification trap'. It contends that any approach treating alignment as optimization toward a fixed formal objective—such as a reward function or constitutional principles—is structurally vulnerable due to three compounding philosophical difficulties: the is-ought gap, value pluralism, and the extended frame problem. The analysis shows that failure modes in methods like RLHF and Constitutional AI reflect these deep vulnerabilities, not mere engineering flaws, and that the alignment gap widens with increasing system capability. Consequently, the paper shifts the constructive burden toward open, developmentally responsive approaches that can update from the processes they govern, though their feasibility remains an empirical question.
本文论证了静态的、基于内容的AI价值对齐方法在AI系统能力扩展、分布变化和自主性增强时，从根本上不足以确保稳健的对齐，这一问题被称为“规范陷阱”。它认为，任何将对齐视为对固定形式目标（如奖励函数或宪法原则）进行优化的方法，由于三个相互强化的哲学难题——实然与应然鸿沟、价值多元论和扩展框架问题——而在结构上存在脆弱性。分析表明，像RLHF和宪法AI等方法中的故障模式反映了这些深层脆弱性，而非单纯的工程缺陷，且对齐差距随着系统能力的增强而扩大。因此，本文将建设性责任转向开放的、发展响应式的方法，这些方法能够从其治理的过程中更新，尽管其可行性仍是一个实证问题。
Evo-MedAgent: Beyond One-Shot Diagnosis with Agents That Remember, Reflect, and Improve
Authors: Weixiang Shen, Bailiang Jian, Jun Li, Che Liu, Johannes Moll, Xiaobin Hu, Daniel Rueckert, Hongwei Bran Li, Jiazhen Pan
First: 2026-04-15T23:12:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T23:12:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-augmented large language model (LLM) agents can orchestrate specialist classifiers, segmentation models, and visual question-answering modules to interpret chest X-rays. However, these agents still solve each case in isolation: they fail to accumulate experience across cases, correct recurrent reasoning mistakes, or adapt their tool-use behavior without expensive reinforcement learning. While a radiologist naturally improves with every case, current agents remain static. In this work, we propose Evo-MedAgent, a self-evolving memory module that equips a medical agent with the capacity for inter-case learning at test time. Our memory comprises three complementary stores: (1)~\emph{Retrospective Clinical Episodes} that retrieve problem-solving experiences from similar past cases, (2)~an \emph{Adaptive Procedural Heuristics} bank curating priority-tagged diagnostic rules that evolves via reflection, much like a physician refining their internal criteria, and (3)~a \emph{Tool Reliability Controller} that tracks per-tool trustworthiness. On ChestAgentBench, Evo-MedAgent raises multiple-choice question (MCQ) accuracy from 0.68 to 0.79 on GPT-5-mini, and from 0.76 to 0.87 on Gemini-3 Flash. With a strong base model, evolving memory improves performance more effectively than orchestrating external tools on qualitative diagnostic tasks. Because Evo-MedAgent requires no training, its per-case overhead is bounded by one additional retrieval pass and a single reflection call, making it deployable on top of any frozen model.
中文标题/摘要

工具增强型大语言模型（LLM）智能体能够协调专业分类器、分割模型和视觉问答模块来解读胸部X光片。然而，现有智能体仍孤立处理每个病例：无法跨病例积累经验、纠正重复推理错误，或在不依赖昂贵强化学习的情况下调整工具使用策略。放射科医生会随病例积累自然提升，而当前智能体却停滞不前。本研究提出Evo-MedAgent——一种自进化的记忆模块，使医疗智能体在测试阶段具备跨病例学习能力。该记忆模块包含三个互补存储单元：（1）《回顾性临床案例库》检索相似历史病例的解题经验；（2）《自适应流程启发库》通过反思机制演化带优先级标签的诊断规则，类似医生精炼内部诊断标准；（3）《工具可靠性控制器》追踪各工具可信度。在ChestAgentBench基准测试中，Evo-MedAgent将GPT-5-mini的多选题准确率从0.68提升至0.79，Gemini-3 Flash从0.76提升至0.87。对于强基础模型，进化记忆在定性诊断任务中比协调外部工具更能有效提升性能。由于无需训练，Evo-MedAgent的单病例开销仅增加一次检索和单次反思调用，可部署于任何冻结模型之上。

Scouting By Reward: VLM-TO-IRL-Driven Player Selection For Esports
Authors: Qing Yan, Wenyu Yang, Yufei Wang, Wenhao Ma, Linchong Hu, Yifei Jin, Anton Dahbura
First: 2026-04-15T23:10:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T23:10:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional esports scouting workflows rely heavily on manual video review and aggregate performance metrics, which often fail to capture the nuanced decision-making patterns necessary to determine if a prospect fits a specific tactical archetype. To address this, we reframe style-based player evaluation in esports as an Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) problem. In this paper, we introduce a novel player selection framework that learns professional-specific reward functions from logged gameplay demonstrations, allowing organizations to rank candidates by their stylistic alignment with a target star player. Our proposed architecture utilizes a multimodal, two-branch intake: one branch encodes structured state-action trajectories derived from high-resolution in-game telemetry, while the second encodes temporally aligned tactical pseudo-commentary generated by Vision-Language Models (VLMs) from broadcast footage. These representations are fused and evaluated via a Generative Adversarial Imitation Learning (GAIL) objective, where a discriminator learns to capture the unique mechanical and tactical signatures of elite professionals. By transitioning from generic skill estimation to scouting "by reward," this framework provides a scalable, workflow-aware digital twin system that enables data-driven roster construction and targeted talent discovery across massive candidate pools.
