Improving Human Performance with Value-Aware Interventions: A Case Study in Chess
Authors: Saumik Narayanan, Raja Panjwani, Siddhartha Sen, Chien-Ju Ho
First: 2026-04-15T22:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T22:55:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI systems are increasingly used to assist humans in sequential decision-making tasks, yet determining when and how an AI assistant should intervene remains a fundamental challenge. A potential baseline is to recommend the optimal action according to a strong model. However, such actions assume optimal follow-up actions, which human decision makers may fail to execute, potentially reducing overall performance. In this work, we propose and study value-aware interventions, motivated by a basic principle in reinforcement learning: under the Bellman equation, the optimal policy selects actions that maximize the immediate reward plus the value function. When a decision maker follows a suboptimal policy, this policy-value consistency no longer holds, creating discrepancies between the actions taken by the policy and those that maximize the immediate reward plus the value of the next state. We show that these policy-value inconsistencies naturally identify opportunities for intervention. We formalize this problem in a Markov decision process where an AI assistant may override human actions under an intervention budget. In the single-intervention regime, we show that the optimal strategy is to recommend the action that maximizes the human value function. For settings with multiple interventions, we propose a tractable approximation that prioritizes interventions based on the magnitude of the policy-value discrepancy. We evaluate these ideas in the domain of chess by learning models of humans from large-scale gameplay data. In simulation, our approach consistently outperforms interventions based on the strongest chess engine (Stockfish) in a wide range of settings. A within-subject human study with 20 players and 600 games further shows that our interventions significantly improve performance for low- and mid-skill players while matching expert-engine interventions for high-skill players.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过价值感知干预提升人类表现：国际象棋案例研究
人工智能系统日益用于辅助人类进行序列决策任务，但确定AI助手应在何时以何种方式干预仍是根本性挑战。一种潜在基准是依据强模型推荐最优行动，然而此类行动假设后续行动均为最优，而人类决策者可能无法执行，反而降低整体表现。本研究基于强化学习的基本原理提出并研究价值感知干预：在贝尔曼方程下，最优策略选择最大化即时奖励与价值函数之和的行动。当决策者遵循次优策略时，这种策略-价值一致性被打破，导致策略采取的行动与最大化即时奖励加下一状态价值的行动产生差异。我们证明这些策略-价值不一致性天然标识出干预时机。我们将该问题形式化为马尔可夫决策过程，其中AI助手可在干预预算内覆盖人类行动。在单次干预机制中，最优策略是推荐最大化人类价值函数的行动；对于多次干预场景，我们提出可处理的近似方法，依据策略-价值差异幅度确定干预优先级。通过从大规模棋局数据学习人类模型，我们在国际象棋领域评估这些方法。模拟实验表明，在广泛场景中我们的干预策略持续优于基于最强象棋引擎（Stockfish）的干预。针对20名玩家600局棋的受试者内实验进一步证明：我们的干预显著提升中低水平玩家的表现，而对高水平玩家的效果与专家引擎干预相当。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of when and how an AI assistant should intervene to improve human sequential decision-making, motivated by the observation that simply recommending optimal actions can fail if humans cannot execute the required follow-ups. The method introduces value-aware interventions, which identify opportunities for AI override by detecting discrepancies between a human's suboptimal policy and the actions that maximize immediate reward plus the value of the next state, formalizing this in a Markov decision process with an intervention budget. Experimental results in chess, using human models learned from gameplay data, show that in simulation the approach consistently outperforms interventions based on a strong chess engine (Stockfish), and a human study with 20 players across 600 games confirms it significantly improves performance for low- and mid-skill players while matching expert-level interventions for high-skill players.
本文针对AI助手应在何时以及如何干预以提升人类序贯决策性能的挑战，其动机在于观察到若人类无法执行后续动作，单纯推荐最优动作可能失效。方法上提出了价值感知干预，通过检测人类次优策略与最大化即时奖励加下一状态价值的动作之间的差异，来识别AI覆盖的机会，并在带有干预预算的马尔可夫决策过程中形式化该问题。在国际象棋领域的实验结果中，基于游戏数据学习的人类模型在模拟中一致优于基于强大象棋引擎（Stockfish）的干预方法，一项涉及20名玩家和600局游戏的人体研究进一步证实，该方法显著提升了低技能和中技能玩家的表现，同时对于高技能玩家则达到了专家级干预的效果。
AgentOpt v0.1 Technical Report: Client-Side Optimization for LLM-Based Agent
Authors: Wenyue Hua, Sripad Karne, Qian Xie, Armaan Agrawal, Nikos Pagonas, Kostis Kaffes, Tianyi Peng
First: 2026-04-07T17:13:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T22:45:43+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 1 figure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
AI agents are increasingly deployed in real-world applications, including systems such as Manus, OpenClaw, and coding agents. Existing research has primarily focused on server-side efficiency, proposing methods such as caching, speculative execution, traffic scheduling, and load balancing to reduce the cost of serving agentic workloads. However, as users increasingly construct agents by composing local tools, remote APIs, and diverse models, an equally important optimization problem arises on the client side. Client-side optimization asks how developers should allocate the resources available to them, including model choice, local tools, and API budget across pipeline stages, subject to application-specific quality, cost, and latency constraints. Because these objectives depend on the task and deployment setting, they cannot be determined by server-side systems alone. We introduce AgentOpt, the first framework-agnostic Python package for client-side agent optimization. We first study model selection, a high-impact optimization lever in multi-step agent pipelines. Given a pipeline and a small evaluation set, the goal is to find the most cost-effective assignment of models to pipeline roles. This problem is consequential in practice: at matched accuracy, the cost gap between the best and worst model combinations can reach 13-32x in our experiments. To efficiently explore the exponentially growing combination space, AgentOpt implements ten search algorithms, including UCB-E, UCB-E with Low-Rank Factorization, Arm Elimination, Epsilon-LUCB, Threshold Successive Elimination, and Bayesian Optimization. Across four benchmarks, UCB-E recovers near-optimal accuracy while reducing evaluation budget by 62-76\% relative to brute-force search. Code and benchmark results available at https://agentoptimizer.github.io/agentopt/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentOpt v0.1技术报告：基于大语言模型智能体的客户端优化方案
AI智能体在现实应用中的部署日益广泛，涵盖Manus、OpenClaw及代码生成智能体等系统。现有研究主要聚焦服务器端效率，通过缓存、推测执行、流量调度与负载均衡等方法降低智能体工作负载的服务成本。然而，随着用户越来越多地通过组合本地工具、远程API和多样化模型来构建智能体，客户端优化问题变得同等重要。客户端优化旨在探讨开发者如何在满足特定应用场景的质量、成本与延迟约束条件下，合理分配可用资源（包括模型选择、本地工具及跨流水线阶段的API预算）。由于这些目标取决于具体任务与部署环境，无法仅通过服务器端系统确定。本文提出首个框架无关的客户端智能体优化Python工具包AgentOpt。我们首先研究多步骤智能体流水线中的关键优化杠杆——模型选择问题：给定流水线结构和少量评估数据集，目标是寻找流水线各角色最具成本效益的模型分配方案。该问题具有重要实践意义：在我们的实验中，在准确率相当的情况下，最优与最差模型组合的成本差距可达13-32倍。为高效探索指数级增长的组合空间，AgentOpt实现了十种搜索算法，包括UCB-E、低秩分解UCB-E、臂消除、Epsilon-LUCB、阈值逐次消除及贝叶斯优化。在四个基准测试中，UCB-E算法在保持接近最优准确率的同时，相较于暴力搜索将评估成本降低了62-76%。代码与基准测试结果详见https://agentoptimizer.github.io/agentopt/。

The paper addresses the need for client-side optimization in LLM-based agents, motivated by the growing deployment of agents that combine local tools, remote APIs, and diverse models, where server-side efficiency methods alone are insufficient for managing application-specific quality, cost, and latency constraints. It introduces AgentOpt, a framework-agnostic Python package that focuses on model selection within multi-step agent pipelines, aiming to find the most cost-effective model assignments to pipeline roles. Experimental results demonstrate that the cost gap between optimal and suboptimal model combinations can reach 13-32x at matched accuracy, and the proposed UCB-E search algorithm recovers near-optimal accuracy while reducing evaluation budget by 62-76% compared to brute-force search across four benchmarks.
本文针对基于大语言模型的智能体在客户端优化的需求，其动机在于智能体日益结合本地工具、远程API和多样化模型进行部署，仅靠服务器端效率方法无法满足应用特定的质量、成本和延迟约束。研究提出了AgentOpt，一个框架无关的Python包，专注于多步骤智能体流程中的模型选择问题，旨在为流程角色寻找最具成本效益的模型分配方案。实验结果表明，在相同准确度下，最优与最差模型组合的成本差距可达13-32倍，且所提出的UCB-E搜索算法在四个基准测试中恢复了接近最优的准确度，同时相比暴力搜索将评估预算减少了62-76%。
You Only Judge Once: Multi-response Reward Modeling in a Single Forward Pass
Authors: Yinuo Yang, Zixian Ma, Manasi Ganti, Jieyu Zhang, Ranjay Krishna
First: 2026-04-13T04:02:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T22:13:12+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a discriminative multimodal reward model that scores all candidate responses in a single forward pass. Conventional discriminative reward models evaluate each response independently, requiring multiple forward passes, one for each potential response. Our approach concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient $N$-way preference learning. The multi-response design also yields up to $N\times$ wall-clock speedup and FLOPs reduction over conventional single-response scoring. To enable $N$-way reward evaluation beyond existing pairwise benchmarks, we construct two new benchmarks: (1) MR$^2$Bench-Image contains human-annotated rankings over responses from 8 diverse models; (2) MR$^2$Bench-Video is a large-scale video-based reward benchmark derived from 94K crowdsourced pairwise human judgments over video question-answering spanning 19 models, denoised via preference graph ensemble. Both benchmarks provide 4-response evaluation variants sampled from the full rankings. Built on a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning and a lightweight MLP value head, our model achieves state-of-the-art results on six multimodal reward benchmarks, including MR$^2$Bench-Image, MR$^2$Bench-Video, and four other existing benchmarks. Our model outperforms existing larger generative and discriminative reward models. We further demonstrate that our reward model, when used in reinforcement learning with GRPO, produces improved policy models that maintain performance across standard multimodal benchmarks while substantially improving open-ended generation quality, outperforming a single-response discriminative reward model (RM) baseline by a large margin in both training stability and open-ended generation quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：单次判定：单次前向传播中的多响应奖励建模
我们提出了一种判别式多模态奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中为所有候选响应评分。传统的判别式奖励模型需独立评估每个响应，需多次前向传播（每个潜在响应一次）。我们的方法通过分隔符将多个响应拼接，并在其标量分数上应用交叉熵，实现了直接比较推理和高效的N路偏好学习。多响应设计相比传统单响应评分，可获得高达N倍的实时加速和FLOPs降低。为超越现有成对基准实现N路奖励评估，我们构建了两个新基准：（1）MR²Bench-Image包含对8个不同模型响应的人工标注排序；（2）MR²Bench-Video是基于视频的大规模奖励基准，源自94K个众包视频问答人类成对判断（涵盖19个模型），通过偏好图集成去噪。两个基准均提供从完整排序中采样的4响应评估变体。基于4B视觉语言骨干网络（采用LoRA微调和轻量级MLP值头），我们的模型在六个多模态奖励基准（包括MR²Bench-Image、MR²Bench-Video和四个现有基准）上取得最先进成果，性能优于现有更大的生成式和判别式奖励模型。我们进一步证明，当该奖励模型与GRPO结合用于强化学习时，可生成改进的策略模型：在保持标准多模态基准性能的同时，显著提升开放式生成质量，在训练稳定性和开放式生成质量上均大幅超越单响应判别式奖励模型基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of conventional discriminative reward models that require multiple forward passes to score candidate responses independently, this paper introduces a multi-response reward model that scores all responses in a single forward pass. The method concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient N-way preference learning, which yields up to N× speedup and FLOPs reduction. Experimental results show that the model, built on a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning, achieves state-of-the-art performance on six multimodal reward benchmarks, including two newly constructed benchmarks (MR²Bench-Image and MR²Bench-Video), and when used in reinforcement learning, it improves policy models in training stability and open-ended generation quality, outperforming larger generative and discriminative baselines.
本文的动机是解决传统判别式奖励模型需多次前向传播独立评分候选响应的低效问题，提出了一种多响应奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中为所有响应评分。方法通过分隔符连接多个响应，并对其标量分数应用交叉熵，实现直接比较推理和高效的N路偏好学习，从而获得高达N倍的加速和计算量减少。实验结果表明，该模型基于40亿参数视觉语言骨干网络并结合LoRA微调，在六个多模态奖励基准（包括新构建的MR²Bench-Image和MR²Bench-Video基准）上取得了最先进的性能；当用于强化学习时，能提升策略模型的训练稳定性和开放式生成质量，显著优于更大的生成式和判别式基线模型。
Timescale Separation Enables Deep Reinforcement Learning Control of Rotating Detonation Engine Mode Transitions
Authors: Kristian Holme, Jean Rabault, Ricardo Vinuesa, Mikael Mortensen
First: 2026-04-15T20:27:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T20:27:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rotating detonation engines (RDEs) are a promising propulsion concept that may offer higher thermodynamic efficiency and specific impulse than conventional systems, but nonlinear phenomena, including transitions to oscillatory or chaotic propagation modes, can hinder practical operation. Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) has emerged as a promising method for controlling complex nonlinear dynamics such as those observed in RDEs. However, the multi-timescale nature of the RDE system makes direct application of DRL challenging. We address this challenge by reformulating the DRL problem in a moving reference frame that follows the detonation-wave pattern, making the wave structure appear quasi-steady to the agent. This reformulation enables scale separation between fast detonation propagation and slower operating-mode dynamics. We train DRL controllers to modulate spatially segmented injection pressure in a one-dimensional reduced-order RDE model and induce rapid transitions between different mode-locked states. Across a range of actuation periods, initial states, and target modes, controllers trained in the moving frame learn more reliably than those trained in a stationary frame and remain effective over a broader range of actuation periods. These results suggest that symmetry-aware moving reference frame formulations may be useful for related multiscale flow-control problems and that scale separation should be exploited whenever possible to enable DRL control of multi-timescale systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时间尺度分离实现旋转爆震发动机模态转换的深度强化学习控制
旋转爆震发动机是一种具有前景的推进概念，其热力学效率和比冲可能优于传统系统，但非线性现象（包括向振荡或混沌传播模态的转换）会阻碍实际运行。深度强化学习已成为控制复杂非线性动力学（如RDE中观察到的现象）的有力方法。然而，RDE系统的多时间尺度特性使得直接应用DRL具有挑战性。我们通过将DRL问题重构在跟随爆震波模式的移动参考系中来解决这一挑战，使波结构在智能体视角下呈现准稳态。这种重构实现了快速爆震传播与较慢运行模态动力学之间的尺度分离。我们在简化的一维RDE模型中训练DRL控制器来调制空间分段喷射压力，并诱导不同锁模态之间的快速转换。在多种作动周期、初始状态和目标模态下，移动参考系中训练的控制器比固定参考系中训练的控制器学习更可靠，且在更广的作动周期范围内保持有效。这些结果表明，对称感知的移动参考系构建方法可能适用于相关的多尺度流动控制问题，且应尽可能利用尺度分离来实现多时间尺度系统的DRL控制。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of controlling rotating detonation engines (RDEs), which offer high efficiency but suffer from unstable mode transitions, by applying deep reinforcement learning (DRL). The key innovation is reformulating the DRL problem in a moving reference frame that follows the detonation wave, separating fast wave propagation from slower operational dynamics to simplify learning. Experimental results on a reduced-order model show that controllers trained in this moving frame achieve more reliable and rapid mode transitions across various conditions compared to those in a stationary frame, demonstrating the effectiveness of exploiting timescale separation for multi-timescale system control.
本文针对旋转爆震发动机（RDE）控制中因不稳定模态转换带来的挑战，采用深度强化学习（DRL）方法进行解决。其核心方法是将DRL问题重构在跟随爆震波移动的参考系中，从而分离快速波传播与慢速运行动力学，简化学习过程。在简化模型上的实验结果表明，相较于固定参考系训练的控制器，移动参考系训练的控制器能在多种条件下实现更可靠、快速的模态转换，验证了利用时间尺度分离控制多尺度系统的有效性。
Towards AI-assisted Neutrino Flavor Theory Design
Authors: Jason Benjamin Baretz, Max Fieg, Vijay Ganesh, Aishik Ghosh, V. Knapp-Perez, Jake Rudolph, Daniel Whiteson
First: 2025-06-09T18:00:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T20:21:57+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 12 Figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Particle physics theories, such as those which explain neutrino flavor mixing, arise from a vast landscape of model-building possibilities. A model's construction typically relies on the intuition of theorists. It also requires considerable effort to identify appropriate symmetry groups, assign field representations, and extract predictions for comparison with experimental data. We develop an Autonomous Model Builder (AMBer), a framework in which a reinforcement learning agent interacts with a streamlined physics software pipeline to search these spaces efficiently. AMBer selects symmetry groups, particle content, and group representation assignments to construct viable models while minimizing the number of free parameters introduced. We validate our approach in well-studied regions of theory space and extend the exploration to a novel, previously unexamined symmetry group. While demonstrated in the context of neutrino flavor theories, this approach of reinforcement learning with physics software feedback may be extended to other theoretical model-building problems in the future.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向人工智能辅助的中微子味理论设计
粒子物理理论，如解释中微子味混合的理论，源于广阔的理论模型构建可能性空间。模型的构建通常依赖于理论物理学家的直觉，且需要大量工作来识别合适的对称群、分配场表示，并提取预测以与实验数据比较。我们开发了自主模型构建器（AMBer），这是一个强化学习智能体与简化物理软件流程交互的框架，用于高效搜索这些理论空间。AMBer通过选择对称群、粒子内容及群表示分配来构建可行模型，同时最小化引入的自由参数数量。我们在理论空间中已深入研究的区域验证了该方法，并将探索扩展至一个新颖、此前未经检验的对称群。尽管以中微子味理论为背景进行演示，这种结合物理软件反馈的强化学习方法未来可扩展至其他理论模型构建问题。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the vast and complex landscape of particle physics model-building, particularly for neutrino flavor theories, which traditionally relies heavily on theorist intuition and manual effort to select symmetries, assign representations, and compare predictions with data. The method introduces an Autonomous Model Builder (AMBer), a framework that employs a reinforcement learning agent to interact with a streamlined physics software pipeline, enabling an efficient search of theory spaces by automatically selecting symmetry groups, particle content, and representation assignments while minimizing free parameters. The main experimental results demonstrate the validation of AMBer in well-studied theory regions and its successful extension to explore a novel, previously unexamined symmetry group, showcasing its potential for broader application in theoretical model-building beyond neutrino physics.

Step-level Denoising-time Diffusion Alignment with Multiple Objectives
Authors: Qi Zhang, Dawei Wang, Shaofeng Zou
First: 2026-04-15T19:52:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T19:52:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful tool for aligning diffusion models with human preferences, typically by optimizing a single reward function under a KL regularization constraint. In practice, however, human preferences are inherently pluralistic, and aligned models must balance multiple downstream objectives, such as aesthetic quality and text-image consistency. Existing multi-objective approaches either rely on costly multi-objective RL fine-tuning or on fusing separately aligned models at denoising time, but they generally require access to reward values (or their gradients) and/or introduce approximation error in the resulting denoising objectives. In this paper, we revisit the problem of RL fine-tuning for diffusion models and address the intractability of identifying the optimal policy by introducing a step-level RL formulation. Building on this, we further propose Multi-objective Step-level Denoising-time Diffusion Alignment (MSDDA), a retraining-free framework for aligning diffusion models with multiple objectives, obtaining the optimal reverse denoising distribution in closed form, with mean and variance expressed directly in terms of single-objective base models. We prove that this denoising-time objective is exactly equivalent to the step-level RL fine-tuning, introducing no approximation error. Moreover, we provide numerical results, which indicate our method outperforms existing denoising-time approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多目标的步级去噪时间扩散对齐
强化学习已成为将扩散模型与人类偏好对齐的强大工具，通常通过在KL正则化约束下优化单一奖励函数实现。然而，人类偏好本质上是多元的，对齐模型必须平衡多个下游目标，如美学质量和图文一致性。现有的多目标方法要么依赖成本高昂的多目标强化学习微调，要么在去噪时融合分别对齐的模型，但通常需要获取奖励值（或其梯度）和/或在去噪目标中引入近似误差。本文重新审视扩散模型的强化学习微调问题，通过引入步级强化学习框架解决最优策略难以求解的难题。在此基础上，我们进一步提出多目标步级去噪时间扩散对齐（MSDDA），这是一种无需重新训练即可将扩散模型与多目标对齐的框架，能以闭式解形式获得最优反向去噪分布，其均值与方差可直接通过单目标基础模型表达。我们证明该去噪时间目标与步级强化学习微调完全等价，不引入任何近似误差。数值实验结果表明，本方法优于现有去噪时间对齐方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of aligning diffusion models with multiple human preference objectives, such as aesthetic quality and text-image consistency, moving beyond single-reward reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning. The authors propose Multi-objective Step-level Denoising-time Diffusion Alignment (MSDDA), a retraining-free framework that formulates alignment as a step-level RL problem and derives the optimal reverse denoising distribution in closed form using single-objective base models. Experimental results demonstrate that this method outperforms existing denoising-time approaches without introducing approximation error, as it is proven equivalent to step-level RL fine-tuning.
本文针对扩散模型与多种人类偏好目标（如美学质量和图文一致性）对齐的挑战，超越了单一奖励的强化学习微调。作者提出了多目标步级去噪时扩散对齐（MSDDA），这是一个无需重新训练的框架，将对齐问题构建为步级强化学习任务，并利用单目标基础模型以闭式解推导出最优反向去噪分布。实验结果表明，该方法优于现有的去噪时对齐方法，且不引入近似误差，因为其被证明与步级强化学习微调完全等价。
Model-Based Reinforcement Learning under Random Observation Delays
Authors: Armin Karamzade, Kyungmin Kim, JB Lanier, Davide Corsi, Roy Fox
First: 2025-09-25T08:01:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T19:40:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Delays frequently occur in real-world environments, yet standard reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms often assume instantaneous perception of the environment. We study random sensor delays in POMDPs, where observations may arrive out-of-sequence, a setting that has not been previously addressed in RL. We analyze the structure of such delays and demonstrate that naive approaches, such as stacking past observations, are insufficient for reliable performance. To address this, we propose a model-based filtering process that sequentially updates the belief state based on an incoming stream of observations. We then introduce a simple delay-aware framework that incorporates this idea into model-based RL, enabling agents to effectively handle random delays. Applying this framework to the Dreamer world-modeling scheme, our method consistently outperforms delay-aware baselines developed for MDPs and demonstrates robustness to delay distribution shifts during deployment. Additionally, we present experiments on simulated robotic tasks, comparing our method to common practical heuristics and emphasizing the importance of explicitly modeling observation delays.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机观测延迟下的基于模型的强化学习
现实环境中常出现延迟，但标准强化学习算法通常假设环境感知是即时的。我们研究了部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的随机传感器延迟问题，其中观测可能乱序到达，这一设定在强化学习中尚未被充分探讨。我们分析了此类延迟的结构，并证明简单方法（如堆叠历史观测）无法保证稳定性能。为此，我们提出一种基于模型的滤波过程，能依据输入的观测流序贯更新信念状态。进而设计了一个简洁的延迟感知框架，将该思想融入基于模型的强化学习，使智能体能有效处理随机延迟。将此框架应用于Dreamer世界建模方案后，我们的方法在延迟分布变化时仍保持稳健，其性能持续优于为马尔可夫决策过程设计的延迟感知基线。此外，我们在模拟机器人任务中进行了实验，通过与常用启发式方法对比，凸显了显式建模观测延迟的重要性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the frequent occurrence of observation delays in real-world systems, which standard reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms typically ignore, this paper addresses random sensor delays in partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) where observations may arrive out of sequence. The method introduces a model-based filtering process that sequentially updates the belief state from delayed observation streams, integrated into a simple delay-aware framework for model-based RL, specifically applied within the Dreamer world-modeling scheme. Experimental results show that this approach consistently outperforms existing delay-aware baselines designed for Markov decision processes, demonstrates robustness to shifts in delay distributions during deployment, and proves more effective than common practical heuristics in simulated robotic tasks, highlighting the necessity of explicitly modeling delays.

When Missing Becomes Structure: Intent-Preserving Policy Completion from Financial KOL Discourse
Authors: Yuncong Liu, Yuan Wan, Zhou Jiang, Yao Lu
First: 2026-04-15T18:39:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T18:39:40+00:00
Comments: Main paper with supplementary material included
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Key Opinion Leader (KOL) discourse on social media is widely consumed as investment guidance, yet turning it into executable trading strategies without injecting assumptions about unspecified execution decisions remains an open problem. We observe that the gaps in KOL statements are not random deficiencies but a structured separation: KOLs express directional intent (what to buy or sell and why) while leaving execution decisions (when, how much, how long) systematically unspecified. Building on this observation, we propose an intent-preserving policy completion framework that treats KOL discourse as a partial trading policy and uses offline reinforcement learning to complete the missing execution decisions around the KOL-expressed intent. Experiments on multimodal KOL discourse from YouTube and X (2022-2025) show that KICL achieves the best return and Sharpe ratio on both platforms while maintaining zero unsupported entries and zero directional reversals, and ablations confirm that the full framework yields an 18.9% return improvement over the KOL-aligned baseline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当缺失成为结构：基于金融KOL言论的意图保持策略补全
社交媒体上关键意见领袖（KOL）的言论常被用作投资参考，但如何在不引入未明确执行决策假设的情况下，将其转化为可执行的交易策略仍是一个开放性问题。我们发现KOL言论中的缺失并非随机缺陷，而是一种结构化分离：KOL表达方向性意图（买卖标的及原因），却系统性地未指定执行决策（时机、数量、时长）。基于此观察，我们提出一种意图保持策略补全框架，将KOL言论视为部分交易策略，并利用离线强化学习围绕KOL表达的意图补全缺失的执行决策。基于YouTube与X平台（2022-2025年）多模态KOL言论的实验表明，KICL在两大平台均实现最佳收益与夏普比率，同时保持零无依据交易与零方向反转，消融实验证实完整框架较KOL对齐基线提升18.9%收益。

Direct Preference Optimization for Primitive-Enabled Hierarchical RL: A Bilevel Approach
Authors: Utsav Singh, Souradip Chakraborty, Wesley A. Suttle, Brian M. Sadler, Derrik E. Asher, Anit Kumar Sahu, Mubarak Shah, Vinay P. Namboodiri, Amrit Singh Bedi
First: 2024-11-01T04:58:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T18:16:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) enables agents to solve complex, long-horizon tasks by decomposing them into manageable sub-tasks. However, HRL methods face two fundamental challenges: (i) non-stationarity caused by the evolving lower-level policy during training, which destabilizes higher-level learning, and (ii) the generation of infeasible subgoals that lower-level policies cannot achieve. To address these challenges, we introduce DIPPER, a novel HRL framework that formulates goal-conditioned HRL as a bi-level optimization problem and leverages direct preference optimization (DPO) to train the higher-level policy. By learning from stationary preference comparisons over subgoal sequences rather than rewards that depend on the evolving lower-level policy, DIPPER mitigates the impact of non-stationarity on hierarchical learning. To address infeasible subgoals, DIPPER incorporates lower-level value function regularization that encourages the higher-level policy to propose achievable subgoals. We also introduce two novel metrics to quantitatively verify that DIPPER mitigates non-stationarity and infeasible subgoal generation issues in HRL. We perform empirical evaluations on challenging robotic navigation and manipulation benchmarks and show that DIPPER achieves upto 40% improvements over state-of-the-art baselines, demonstrating that preference-based methods can effectively alleviate persistent challenges in hierarchical
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向基元启发的分层强化学习的直接偏好优化：一种双层优化方法
分层强化学习（HRL）通过将复杂长程任务分解为可管理的子任务来帮助智能体解决问题。然而，HRL方法面临两个根本性挑战：（一）训练过程中底层策略演化导致的非平稳性会破坏高层学习的稳定性；（二）可能生成底层策略无法实现的不可行子目标。为应对这些挑战，我们提出DIPPER——一种将目标条件化HRL建模为双层优化问题，并利用直接偏好优化（DPO）训练高层策略的新型HRL框架。通过基于子目标序列的稳态偏好比较（而非依赖演化中底层策略的奖励）进行学习，DIPPER有效缓解了非平稳性对分层学习的影响。针对不可行子目标问题，DIPPER引入底层价值函数正则化机制，促使高层策略提出可达成的子目标。我们还提出两个新量化指标，验证DIPPER在缓解HRL中非平稳性与不可行子目标生成问题的有效性。在具有挑战性的机器人导航与操作基准测试中，DIPPER相较最先进基线方法实现最高40%的性能提升，证明基于偏好的方法能有效缓解分层学习中的长期难题。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces DIPPER, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) framework designed to address two core challenges: non-stationarity from evolving lower-level policies and the generation of infeasible subgoals. The method formulates HRL as a bi-level optimization problem, applying direct preference optimization (DPO) to train the higher-level policy using stationary preference comparisons over subgoal sequences, alongside lower-level value function regularization to promote achievable subgoals. Experimental results on robotic navigation and manipulation tasks show that DIPPER reduces non-stationarity and infeasible subgoals, achieving up to 40% performance improvements over state-of-the-art baselines.
本文提出了DIPPER，一种分层强化学习框架，旨在解决两个核心挑战：由底层策略演化引起的非平稳性以及不可行子目标的生成。该方法将分层强化学习构建为一个双层优化问题，利用直接偏好优化通过稳定的子目标序列偏好比较来训练高层策略，并结合底层价值函数正则化以鼓励生成可实现的子目标。在机器人导航和操作任务上的实验结果表明，DIPPER有效缓解了非平稳性和不可行子目标问题，相比现有先进基线方法性能提升高达40%。
Aerial Multi-Functional RIS in Fluid Antennas-Aided Full-Duplex Networks: A Self-Optimized Hybrid Deep Reinforcement Learning Approach
Authors: Li-Hsiang Shen, Yu-Quan Zheng
First: 2026-04-15T18:06:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T18:06:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To address high data traffic demands of sixth-generation (6G) networks, this paper proposes a novel architecture that integrates autonomous aerial vehicles (AAVs) and multi-functional reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (MF-RISs) as AM-RIS in fluid antenna (FA)-assisted full-duplex (FD) networks. The AM-RIS provides hybrid functionalities, including signal reflection, amplification, and energy harvesting (EH), potentially improving both signal coverage and sustainability. Meanwhile, FA facilitates fine-grained spatial adaptability at FD-enabled base station (BS), which complements residual self-interference (SI) suppression. We aim at maximizing the overall energy efficiency (EE) by jointly optimizing transmit DL beamforming at BS, UL user power, configuration of AM-RIS, and positions of the FA and AM-RIS. Owing to the hybrid continuous-discrete parameters and high dimensionality of the intractable problem, we have conceived a self-optimized multi-agent hybrid deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework (SOHRL), which integrates multi-agent deep Q-networks (DQN) and multi-agent proximal policy optimization (PPO), respectively handling discrete and continuous actions. To enhance self-adaptability, an attention-driven state representation and meta-level hyperparameter optimization are incorporated, enabling multi-agents to autonomously adjust learning hyperparameters. Simulation results validate the effectiveness of the proposed AM-RIS-enabled FA-aided FD networks empowered by SOHRL algorithm. The results reveal that SOHRL outperforms benchmarks of the case without attention mechanism and conventional hybrid/multi-agent/standalone DRL. Moreover, AM-RIS in FD achieves the highest EE compared to half-duplex, conventional rigid antenna arrays, partial EH, and conventional RIS without amplification, highlighting its potential as a compelling solution for EE-aware wireless networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流体天线辅助全双工网络中空中多功能可重构智能表面的自优化混合深度强化学习方法
为应对第六代（6G）网络的高数据流量需求，本文提出一种创新架构，将自主飞行器与多功能可重构智能表面集成为AM-RIS，应用于流体天线辅助的全双工网络。AM-RIS具备信号反射、放大和能量收集的混合功能，可同步提升信号覆盖与系统可持续性。流体天线则在全双工基站端实现细粒度空间自适应，辅助残余自干扰抑制。通过联合优化基站下行波束赋形、上行用户功率、AM-RIS配置及FA与AM-RIS的部署位置，实现整体能效最大化。针对该混合连续-离散参数的高维难题，我们设计了自优化多智能体混合深度强化学习框架，融合多智能体深度Q网络与近端策略优化算法，分别处理离散与连续动作空间。该框架引入注意力驱动的状态表征与元级超参数优化机制，赋予多智能体自主调节学习超参数的自适应能力。仿真结果表明：基于SOHRL算法的AM-RIS增强型FA辅助FD网络能效显著优于无注意力机制基准方案及传统混合/多智能体/独立DRL方法；相较于半双工、传统刚性天线阵列、部分能量收集方案及无放大功能的常规RIS，AM-RIS在全双工模式下实现了最高能效，彰显其作为能效敏感型无线网络解决方案的巨大潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to support high data traffic in 6G networks, this paper proposes a novel architecture combining aerial multi-functional reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (AM-RIS) with fluid antennas in full-duplex networks to enhance energy efficiency, coverage, and sustainability. The method employs a self-optimized multi-agent hybrid deep reinforcement learning framework (SOHRL) that integrates deep Q-networks and proximal policy optimization to jointly optimize beamforming, user power, RIS configuration, and positions, handling both discrete and continuous actions with attention mechanisms and hyperparameter self-tuning. Experimental simulations demonstrate that the proposed SOHRL algorithm outperforms benchmarks without attention and conventional DRL approaches, and the AM-RIS in full-duplex achieves the highest energy efficiency compared to half-duplex, rigid antenna arrays, and conventional RIS without amplification, validating its effectiveness for energy-aware wireless networks.

From $P(y|x)$ to $P(y)$: Investigating Reinforcement Learning in Pre-train Space
Authors: Yuqiao Tan, Minzheng Wang, Bo Liu, Zichen Liu, Tian Liang, Shizhu He, Jun Zhao, Kang Liu
First: 2026-04-15T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:59:01+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Our code is available at https://github.com/Trae1ounG/Pretrain_Space_RLVR
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) significantly enhances LLM reasoning by optimizing the conditional distribution P(y|x), its potential is fundamentally bounded by the base model's existing output distribution. Optimizing the marginal distribution P(y) in the Pre-train Space addresses this bottleneck by encoding reasoning ability and preserving broad exploration capacity. Yet, conventional pre-training relies on static corpora for passive learning, leading to a distribution shift that hinders targeted reasoning enhancement. In this paper, we introduce PreRL (Pre-train Space RL), which applies reward-driven online updates directly to P(y). We theoretically and empirically validate the strong gradient alignment between log P(y) and log P(y|x), establishing PreRL as a viable surrogate for standard RL. Furthermore, we uncover a critical mechanism: Negative Sample Reinforcement (NSR) within PreRL serves as an exceptionally effective driver for reasoning. NSR-PreRL rapidly prunes incorrect reasoning spaces while stimulating endogenous reflective behaviors, increasing transition and reflection thoughts by 14.89x and 6.54x, respectively. Leveraging these insights, we propose Dual Space RL (DSRL), a Policy Reincarnation strategy that initializes models with NSR-PreRL to expand the reasoning horizon before transitioning to standard RL for fine-grained optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DSRL consistently outperforms strong baselines, proving that pre-train space pruning effectively steers the policy toward a refined correct reasoning subspace.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从$P(y|x)$到$P(y)$：探索预训练空间中的强化学习
尽管带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通过优化条件分布P(y|x)显著提升了大型语言模型的推理能力，但其潜力从根本上受限于基础模型现有的输出分布。在预训练空间中优化边缘分布P(y)通过编码推理能力并保持广泛的探索能力，解决了这一瓶颈。然而，传统的预训练依赖静态语料库进行被动学习，导致分布偏移，阻碍了针对性推理增强。本文提出预训练空间强化学习（PreRL），将奖励驱动的在线更新直接应用于P(y)。我们从理论和实证上验证了log P(y)与log P(y|x)之间的强梯度对齐，确立了PreRL作为标准RL可行替代方案的可行性。此外，我们发现了一个关键机制：PreRL中的负样本强化（NSR）是推理能力的极有效驱动力。NSR-PreRL能快速剪除错误推理空间，同时激发内源性反思行为，使转换思维和反思思维分别提升14.89倍和6.54倍。基于这些发现，我们提出双空间强化学习（DSRL）——一种策略重生策略：先用NSR-PreRL初始化模型以扩展推理边界，再过渡到标准RL进行细粒度优化。大量实验表明，DSRL始终优于强基线方法，证明预训练空间剪枝能有效引导策略进入精炼的正确推理子空间。

They theoretically and empirically show gradient alignment between optimizing P(y) and P(y|x), and identify a key mechanism called Negative Sample Reinforcement (NSR) within PreRL, which aggressively prunes incorrect reasoning paths and increases reflective thoughts by factors of 14.89x and 6.54x. Building on this, they introduce Dual Space RL (DSRL), which first uses NSR-PreRL to broaden the reasoning horizon and then applies standard RL for fine-tuning, with experiments showing DSRL consistently outperforms strong baselines.

Enhancing LLM-based Search Agents via Contribution Weighted Group Relative Policy Optimization
Authors: Junzhe Wang, Zhiheng Xi, yajie yang, Hao Luo, Shihan Dou, Tao Gui, Qi Zhang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-15T17:37:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:37:59+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the 64th Annual Meeting of the Association for Computational Linguistics (ACL 2026), Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Search agents extend Large Language Models (LLMs) beyond static parametric knowledge by enabling access to up-to-date and long-tail information unavailable during pretraining. While reinforcement learning has been widely adopted for training such agents, existing approaches face key limitations: process supervision often suffers from unstable value estimation, whereas outcome supervision struggles with credit assignment due to sparse, trajectory-level rewards. To bridge this gap, we propose Contribution-Weighted GRPO (CW-GRPO), a framework that integrates process supervision into group relative policy optimization. Instead of directly optimizing process rewards, CW-GRPO employs an LLM judge to assess the retrieval utility and reasoning correctness at each search round, producing per-round contribution scores. These scores are used to rescale outcome-based advantages along the trajectory, enabling fine-grained credit assignment without sacrificing optimization stability. Experiments on multiple knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that CW-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO by 5.0\% on Qwen3-8B and 6.3\% on Qwen3-1.7B, leading to more effective search behaviors. Additional analysis reveals that successful trajectories exhibit concentrated contributions across rounds, providing empirical insight into search agent tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于贡献加权组相对策略优化增强大语言模型搜索智能体
搜索智能体通过访问预训练时无法获取的最新信息和长尾信息，扩展了大语言模型（LLMs）的静态参数知识边界。尽管强化学习已被广泛用于训练此类智能体，但现有方法面临关键局限：过程监督常受价值估计不稳定困扰，而结果监督则因稀疏的轨迹级奖励而难以进行信用分配。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了贡献加权GRPO（CW-GRPO），该框架将过程监督整合到组相对策略优化中。CW-GRPO不直接优化过程奖励，而是采用LLM评判器评估每轮搜索的检索效用和推理正确性，生成每轮贡献分数。这些分数用于重新调整沿轨迹的结果优势度，实现细粒度信用分配且不牺牲优化稳定性。在多个知识密集型基准测试上的实验表明，CW-GRPO在Qwen3-8B上比标准GRPO提升5.0%，在Qwen3-1.7B上提升6.3%，产生了更有效的搜索行为。进一步分析揭示，成功轨迹在各轮次中表现出集中的贡献分布，为搜索智能体任务提供了实证见解。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address limitations in training LLM-based search agents, where existing reinforcement learning methods using process supervision suffer from unstable value estimation, while outcome supervision struggles with sparse rewards and credit assignment. The proposed method, Contribution-Weighted GRPO (CW-GRPO), integrates process supervision into group relative policy optimization by employing an LLM judge to assess retrieval utility and reasoning correctness per search round, generating contribution scores that rescale outcome-based advantages for fine-grained credit assignment. Experimental results on knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that CW-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO by 5.0% on Qwen3-8B and 6.3% on Qwen3-1.7B, leading to more effective search behaviors, with analysis indicating that successful trajectories exhibit concentrated contributions across rounds.

Hierarchical DLO Routing with Reinforcement Learning and In-Context Vision-language Models
Authors: Mingen Li, Houjian Yu, Yixuan Huang, Youngjin Hong, Hantao Ye, Changhyun Choi
First: 2025-10-22T05:57:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:36:28+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Long-horizon routing tasks of deformable linear objects (DLOs), such as cables and ropes, are common in industrial assembly lines and everyday life. These tasks are particularly challenging because they require robots to manipulate DLO with long-horizon planning and reliable skill execution. Successfully completing such tasks demands adapting to their nonlinear dynamics, decomposing abstract routing goals, and generating multi-step plans composed of multiple skills, all of which require accurate high-level reasoning during execution. In this paper, we propose a fully autonomous hierarchical framework for solving challenging DLO routing tasks. Given an implicit or explicit routing goal expressed in language, our framework leverages vision-language models~(VLMs) for in-context high-level reasoning to synthesize feasible plans, which are then executed by low-level skills trained via reinforcement learning. To improve robustness over long horizons, we further introduce a failure recovery mechanism that reorients the DLO into insertion-feasible states. Our approach generalizes to diverse scenes involving object attributes, spatial descriptions, implicit language commands, and \myred{extended 5-clip settings}. It achieves an overall success rate of 92\% across long-horizon routing scenarios. Please refer to our project page: https://icra2026-dloroute.github.io/DLORoute/

Reinforcement Learning via Value Gradient Flow
Authors: Haoran Xu, Kaiwen Hu, Somayeh Sojoudi, Amy Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-15T17:12:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T17:12:56+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We study behavior-regularized reinforcement learning (RL), where regularization toward a reference distribution (the dataset in offline RL or the base model in LLM RL finetuning) is essential to prevent value over-optimization caused by erroneous out-of-distribution extrapolation. Existing methods either rely on reparameterized policy gradient, which are difficult to scale to large generative models, or on reject sampling, which can be overly conservative when attempting to move beyond the behavior support. In this paper, we propose Value Gradient Flow (VGF), a scalable new paradigm for behavior-regularized RL. VGF casts behavior-regularized RL as an optimal transport problem that maps the reference distribution to the value-induced optimal policy distribution. We solve this transport problem via discrete gradient flow, where value gradients guide particles initialized from the reference distribution. Our analysis shows that VGF imposes regularization implicitly by controlling the transport budget. VGF eliminates explicit policy parameterization while remaining expressive and flexible, this enables adaptive test-time scaling by adjusting the transport budget. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VGF significantly outperforms prior methods, achieving state-of-the-art results on offline RL benchmarks (D4RL, OGBench) and LLM RL tasks. Code and runs can be found at https://ryanxhr.github.io/vgf.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于价值梯度流的强化学习
本文研究行为正则化强化学习（RL），其中朝向参考分布的正则化（离线RL中的数据集或LLM RL微调中的基础模型）对于防止因分布外错误外推导致的价值过度优化至关重要。现有方法要么依赖重参数化的策略梯度（难以扩展至大型生成模型），要么依赖拒绝采样（在尝试超越行为支持集时可能过于保守）。本文提出价值梯度流（VGF），一种可扩展的行为正则化RL新范式。VGF将行为正则化RL构建为将参考分布映射至价值诱导最优策略分布的最优传输问题。我们通过离散梯度流求解该传输问题，其中价值梯度引导从参考分布初始化的粒子。分析表明，VGF通过控制传输预算实现隐式正则化。VGF在保持表达力和灵活性的同时消除了显式策略参数化，这允许通过调整传输预算实现自适应测试时缩放。大量实验表明，VGF显著优于现有方法，在离线RL基准（D4RL、OGBench）和LLM RL任务中取得最先进成果。代码与实验记录见 https://ryanxhr.github.io/vgf。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of value over-optimization in behavior-regularized reinforcement learning, where standard methods like reparameterized policy gradients are hard to scale or reject sampling is too conservative. It introduces Value Gradient Flow (VGF), a scalable paradigm that frames the problem as optimal transport, mapping a reference distribution to an optimal policy distribution via discrete gradient flow guided by value gradients, implicitly regularizing by controlling the transport budget. Experiments show VGF outperforms prior methods, achieving state-of-the-art results on offline RL benchmarks such as D4RL and OGBench, as well as on LLM RL tasks, with adaptive test-time scaling enabled by adjusting the transport budget.
本文针对行为正则化强化学习中的价值过优化问题，现有方法如重参数化策略梯度难以扩展或拒绝采样过于保守。作者提出了价值梯度流（VGF），一种可扩展的新范式，将问题构建为最优传输，通过离散梯度流将参考分布映射到价值诱导的最优策略分布，利用价值梯度引导粒子，通过控制传输预算实现隐式正则化。实验表明，VGF在离线RL基准（如D4RL和OGBench）和LLM RL任务上显著优于先前方法，取得了最先进的结果，并通过调整传输预算实现了自适应测试时缩放。
Deep Neural Network-guided PSO for Tracking a Global Optimal Position in Complex Dynamic Environment
Authors: Stephen Raharja, Toshiharu Sugawara
First: 2026-04-15T16:38:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:38:03+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures, 5 tables. Accepted at ISMSI 2026 (10th International Conference on Intelligent Systems, Metaheuristics & Swarm Intelligence ), Cebu, Philippines, April 24-26, 2026. To appear in the ACM International Conference Proceedings Series
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose novel particle swarm optimization (PSO) variants incorporated with deep neural networks (DNNs) for particles to pursue globally optimal positions in dynamic environments. PSO is a heuristic approach for solving complex optimization problems. However, canonical PSO and its variants struggle to adapt efficiently to dynamic environments, in which the global optimum moves over time, and to track them accurately. Many PSO algorithms improve convergence by increasing the swarm size beyond potential optima, which are global/local optima but are not identified until they are discovered. Additionally, in dynamic environments, several methods use multiple sub-population and re-diversification mechanisms to address outdated memory and local optima entrapment. To track the global optimum in dynamic environments with smaller swarm sizes, the DNNs in our methods determine particle movement by learning environmental characteristics and adapting dynamics to pursue moving optimal positions. This enables particles to adapt to environmental changes and predict the moving optima. We propose two variants: a swarm with a centralized network and distributed networks for all particles. Our experimental results show that both variants can track moving potential optima with lower cumulative tracking error than those of several recent PSO-based algorithms, with fewer particles than potential optima.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度神经网络引导的粒子群优化算法在复杂动态环境中追踪全局最优位置
本文提出融合深度神经网络的新型粒子群优化算法变体，使粒子能在动态环境中追踪全局最优位置。粒子群优化是一种解决复杂优化问题的启发式方法，但经典算法及其变体难以高效适应动态环境（全局最优值随时间移动）并实现精准追踪。现有方法常通过扩大种群规模超越潜在最优值（即未被发现前的全局/局部最优）来提升收敛性，或在动态环境中采用多子群与再多样化机制应对记忆过时和局部最优陷阱。为以较小种群规模追踪动态环境中的全局最优，本方法通过深度神经网络学习环境特征、调整动态策略以追踪移动最优值，使粒子能适应环境变化并预测移动最优值。我们提出两种变体：集中式网络架构与分布式粒子网络架构。实验表明，两种变体均能以少于潜在最优值数量的粒子实现移动最优值追踪，其累积追踪误差低于近年多种粒子群优化算法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of particle swarm optimization (PSO) algorithms struggling to efficiently track moving global optima in dynamic environments with small swarm sizes, this paper introduces novel PSO variants that integrate deep neural networks (DNNs) to guide particle movement. The method employs DNNs, implemented in either a centralized or distributed architecture, to learn environmental characteristics and predict the trajectory of optimal positions, enabling particles to adapt dynamically. Experimental results demonstrate that both proposed variants achieve lower cumulative tracking error compared to several recent PSO-based algorithms, even when using fewer particles than the number of potential optima.
针对粒子群优化算法在动态环境中难以用小规模种群有效追踪移动全局最优解的问题，本文提出了融合深度神经网络的新型粒子群优化变体。该方法通过集中式或分布式的深度神经网络学习环境特征并预测最优位置的移动轨迹，从而动态引导粒子运动。实验结果表明，与多种近期基于粒子群优化的算法相比，所提出的两种变体均能以少于潜在最优解数量的粒子数，实现更低的累积跟踪误差。
A Comparative Study of Dynamic Programming and Reinforcement Learning in Finite Horizon Dynamic Pricing
Authors: Lev Razumovskiy, Nikolay Karenin
First: 2026-04-15T16:36:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:36:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper provides a systematic comparison between Fitted Dynamic Programming (DP), where demand is estimated from data, and Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods in finite-horizon dynamic pricing problems. We analyze their performance across environments of increasing structural complexity, ranging from a single typology benchmark to multi-typology settings with heterogeneous demand and inter-temporal revenue constraints. Unlike simplified comparisons that restrict DP to low-dimensional settings, we apply dynamic programming in richer, multi-dimensional environments with multiple product types and constraints. We evaluate revenue performance, stability, constraint satisfaction behavior, and computational scaling, highlighting the trade-offs between explicit expectation-based optimization and trajectory-based learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有限时域动态定价中动态规划与强化学习的比较研究
本文系统比较了基于数据估计需求的拟合动态规划与强化学习方法在有限时域动态定价问题中的应用。我们分析了它们在结构复杂度递增环境中的性能，从单一类型基准到具有异质需求和跨期收益约束的多类型场景。与将动态规划局限于低维环境的简化比较不同，我们在包含多产品类型和约束的更丰富多维环境中应用动态规划。我们评估了收益表现、稳定性、约束满足行为及计算扩展性，揭示了基于显式期望的优化与基于轨迹的学习之间的权衡关系。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to systematically compare model-based and model-free approaches in complex pricing environments, this paper conducts a comparative study of Fitted Dynamic Programming (DP) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) for finite-horizon dynamic pricing. The method involves applying both approaches across environments of increasing structural complexity, from single to multi-typology settings with heterogeneous demand and inter-temporal constraints, without restricting DP to low-dimensional cases. The main experimental results reveal trade-offs in revenue performance, stability, constraint satisfaction, and computational scaling, highlighting the differences between expectation-based DP optimization and trajectory-based RL learning.
本文旨在系统比较基于模型和无模型方法在复杂定价环境中的表现，对有限时域动态定价中的拟合动态规划（DP）和强化学习（RL）进行了对比研究。研究方法是在结构复杂性递增的环境中应用这两种方法，从单一类型基准到具有异质性需求和跨期收入约束的多类型设置，且未将DP局限于低维情况。主要实验结果表明了两种方法在收入性能、稳定性、约束满足行为和计算扩展性上的权衡，凸显了基于期望的DP优化与基于轨迹的RL学习之间的差异。
Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Runtime Safety Shielding for Power Grid Operation
Authors: Gitesh Malik
First: 2026-04-15T16:11:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T16:11:10+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has shown promise for automating power-grid operation tasks such as topology control and congestion management. However, its deployment in real-world power systems remains limited by strict safety requirements, brittleness under rare disturbances, and poor generalization to unseen grid topologies. In safety-critical infrastructure, catastrophic failures cannot be tolerated, and learning-based controllers must operate within hard physical constraints. This paper proposes a safety-constrained hierarchical control framework for power-grid operation that explicitly decouples long-horizon decision-making from real-time feasibility enforcement. A high-level reinforcement learning policy proposes abstract control actions, while a deterministic runtime safety shield filters unsafe actions using fast forward simulation. Safety is enforced as a runtime invariant, independent of policy quality or training distribution. The proposed framework is evaluated on the Grid2Op benchmark suite under nominal conditions, forced line-outage stress tests, and zero-shot deployment on the ICAPS 2021 large-scale transmission grid without retraining. Results show that flat reinforcement learning policies are brittle under stress, while safety-only methods are overly conservative. In contrast, the proposed hierarchical and safety-aware approach achieves longer episode survival, lower peak line loading, and robust zero-shot generalization to unseen grids. These results indicate that safety and generalization in power-grid control are best achieved through architectural design rather than increasingly complex reward engineering, providing a practical path toward deployable learning-based controllers for real-world energy systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于运行时安全防护的层次化强化学习在电网运行中的应用
强化学习在电网拓扑控制与阻塞管理等自动化任务中展现出潜力，但其在实际电力系统的部署仍受限于严格的安全要求、罕见扰动下的脆弱性以及对未知电网拓扑的泛化能力不足。在安全关键基础设施中，灾难性故障不可容忍，基于学习的控制器必须在硬性物理约束下运行。 本文提出一种面向电网运行的安全约束分层控制框架，明确将长时域决策与实时可行性执行解耦。高层强化学习策略提出抽象控制动作，而确定性运行时安全防护层通过快速前向模拟过滤不安全动作。安全作为运行时不变性得以保障，与策略质量或训练分布无关。 该框架在Grid2Op基准测试集上接受评估，涵盖正常运行条件、强制线路停运压力测试，以及在ICAPS 2021大规模输电网上的零样本部署（无需重新训练）。结果表明：扁平强化学习策略在压力下表现脆弱，纯安全方法则过于保守；相比之下，所提出的分层安全感知方法实现了更长的运行周期、更低的线路峰值负载，并对未知电网具有稳健的零样本泛化能力。 这些结果表明，电网控制中的安全性与泛化能力通过架构设计而非日益复杂的奖励工程更能有效实现，为现实能源系统中可部署的学习型控制器提供了可行路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe and robust reinforcement learning controllers in real-world power grids, which face strict safety constraints and poor generalization to unseen conditions, this paper proposes a hierarchical control framework that decouples high-level decision-making from real-time safety enforcement. The method employs a high-level RL policy to propose abstract actions, which are then filtered by a deterministic runtime safety shield using fast forward simulation to ensure physical feasibility. Experimental results on the Grid2Op benchmark, including stress tests and zero-shot deployment on a large-scale grid, demonstrate that this approach outperforms flat RL and safety-only methods by achieving longer episode survival, lower peak line loading, and robust generalization without retraining, indicating that architectural design is key to deployable learning-based grid control.
本文的动机是解决强化学习在现实电网控制中面临的安全约束严格和泛化能力不足的问题，提出了一种分层控制框架，将高层决策与实时安全执行解耦。该方法采用高层强化学习策略提出抽象控制动作，并通过一个基于快速前向仿真的确定性运行时安全护盾来过滤不安全动作，确保物理可行性。在Grid2Op基准测试中的实验结果表明，包括压力测试和在大规模电网上的零样本部署，该方法优于扁平强化学习和纯安全方法，实现了更长的运行生存时间、更低的线路峰值负载以及无需重新训练的鲁棒泛化能力，表明架构设计是实现可部署学习型电网控制器的关键。
GFT: From Imitation to Reward Fine-Tuning with Unbiased Group Advantages and Dynamic Coefficient Rectification
Authors: Wangjie Gan, Miao Pan, Linbo Xi, Wenqi Zhang, Jintao Chen, Jianwei Yin, Xuhong Zhang
First: 2026-04-15T15:49:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:49:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models are typically post-trained using supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL), yet effectively unifying efficient knowledge injection with robust generalization remains challenging. In this work, we provide a training-dynamics analysis showing that SFT can be interpreted as a special case of policy gradient optimization with an extremely sparse implicit reward and unstable inverse-probability weighting, which together lead to single-path dependency, entropy collapse, and gradient explosion. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose Group Fine-Tuning (GFT), a unified post-training framework that addresses these intrinsic limitations through two mechanisms: Group Advantage Learning, which constructs diverse response groups and derives normalized contrastive supervision to alleviate reward sparsity, and Dynamic Coefficient Rectification, which adaptively bounds inverse-probability weights to stabilize optimization while preserving efficient knowledge injection. Experiments demonstrate that GFT consistently surpasses SFT-based methods and yields policies that integrate more smoothly with subsequent RL training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GFT：从模仿到奖励微调——基于无偏群体优势与动态系数校正
大语言模型通常通过监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）进行后训练，但如何有效统一高效知识注入与鲁棒泛化能力仍具挑战。本研究通过训练动态分析表明，SFT可视为策略梯度优化的特例：其隐含奖励极度稀疏且逆概率加权不稳定，共同导致单一路径依赖、熵崩塌与梯度爆炸。基于此诊断，我们提出群体微调（GFT）这一统一后训练框架，通过双重机制解决固有局限：群体优势学习通过构建多样化响应群体并推导归一化对比监督以缓解奖励稀疏性；动态系数校正通过自适应约束逆概率权重来稳定优化过程，同时保持高效知识注入。实验表明，GFT持续超越基于SFT的方法，并能生成与后续RL训练更平滑集成的策略。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of unifying efficient knowledge injection with robust generalization in post-training large language models, where supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is analyzed as a policy gradient method with sparse implicit rewards and unstable weighting, leading to issues like entropy collapse. To address this, the method introduces Group Fine-Tuning (GFT), which employs Group Advantage Learning to create diverse response groups for normalized contrastive supervision and Dynamic Coefficient Rectification to adaptively bound weights for stable optimization. Experimental results show that GFT consistently outperforms SFT-based approaches and produces policies that integrate more smoothly with subsequent reinforcement learning training.
本文的动机在于解决大型语言模型后训练中高效知识注入与鲁棒泛化统一的挑战，分析指出监督微调（SFT）作为一种策略梯度方法存在隐式奖励稀疏和权重不稳定问题，导致熵崩溃等缺陷。为此，方法提出了分组微调（GFT），通过分组优势学习构建多样化响应组以提供归一化对比监督，并利用动态系数校正自适应约束权重以稳定优化。实验结果表明，GFT持续超越基于SFT的方法，并生成能更平滑地融入后续强化学习训练的策略。
BOAT: Navigating the Sea of In Silico Predictors for Antibody Design via Multi-Objective Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Jackie Rao, Ferran Gonzalez Hernandez, Leon Gerard, Alexandra Gessner
First: 2026-04-15T15:25:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:25:52+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 29th International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Antibody lead optimization is inherently a multi-objective challenge in drug discovery. Achieving a balance between different drug-like properties is crucial for the development of viable candidates, and this search becomes exponentially challenging as desired properties grow. The ever-growing zoo of sophisticated in silico tools for predicting antibody properties calls for an efficient joint optimization procedure to overcome resource-intensive sequential filtering pipelines. We present BOAT, a versatile Bayesian optimization framework for multi-property antibody engineering. Our `plug-and-play' framework couples uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling with a genetic algorithm to jointly optimize various predicted antibody traits while enabling efficient exploration of sequence space. Through systematic benchmarking against genetic algorithms and newer generative learning approaches, we demonstrate competitive performance with state-of-the-art methods for multi-objective protein optimization. We identify clear regimes where surrogate-driven optimization outperforms expensive generative approaches and establish practical limits imposed by sequence dimensionality and oracle costs.

标题：BOAT：通过多目标贝叶斯优化在抗体设计的硅学预测器海洋中导航
抗体先导优化本质上是药物发现中的多目标挑战。在不同类药性质间取得平衡对于开发可行候选药物至关重要，而随着所需性质的增加，这种搜索的难度呈指数级增长。日益复杂的抗体性质硅学预测工具亟需一种高效的联合优化流程，以克服资源密集型的顺序筛选流程。我们提出BOAT——一个用于多性质抗体工程的通用贝叶斯优化框架。该'即插即用'框架将不确定性感知代理模型与遗传算法相结合，在高效探索序列空间的同时联合优化多种预测的抗体特性。通过对遗传算法和新型生成学习方法的系统基准测试，我们证明了其在多目标蛋白质优化任务中与前沿方法具有竞争力的性能。我们明确了代理驱动优化优于昂贵生成方法的适用场景，并确定了序列维度和评估成本带来的实际限制。

The paper introduces BOAT, a Bayesian optimization framework designed to address the multi-objective challenge of antibody lead optimization, where balancing multiple drug-like properties is critical but computationally demanding due to the proliferation of in silico prediction tools. The method employs a plug-and-play approach that combines uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling with a genetic algorithm to jointly optimize predicted antibody traits while efficiently exploring sequence space. Experimental benchmarking against genetic algorithms and generative learning methods shows that BOAT achieves competitive performance, identifying scenarios where surrogate-driven optimization surpasses costlier generative approaches and highlighting practical limits related to sequence dimensionality and computational costs.

Provably Efficient Offline-to-Online Value Adaptation with General Function Approximation
Authors: Shangzhe Li, Weitong Zhang
First: 2026-04-15T15:17:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:17:40+00:00
Comments: 44 pages, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study value adaptation in offline-to-online reinforcement learning under general function approximation. Starting from an imperfect offline pretrained $Q$-function, the learner aims to adapt it to the target environment using only a limited amount of online interaction. We first characterize the difficulty of this setting by establishing a minimax lower bound, showing that even when the pretrained $Q$-function is close to optimal $Q^\star$, online adaptation can be no more efficient than pure online RL on certain hard instances. On the positive side, under a novel structural condition on the offline-pretrained value functions, we propose O2O-LSVI, an adaptation algorithm with problem-dependent sample complexity that provably improves over pure online RL. Finally, we complement our theory with neural-network experiments that demonstrate the practical effectiveness of the proposed method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于通用函数逼近的可证明高效离线到在线价值适应方法
本文研究通用函数逼近框架下离线到在线强化学习中的价值适应问题。学习者从一个不完美的离线预训练$Q$函数出发，仅通过有限的在线交互将其调整至目标环境。我们首先通过建立极小极大下界来刻画该场景的难度，证明即使预训练$Q$函数接近最优$Q^\star$，在某些困难实例上在线适应的效率仍无法超越纯在线强化学习。积极方面，在离线预训练价值函数满足新颖结构条件的前提下，我们提出O2O-LSVI算法——该适应算法具有问题依赖的样本复杂度，可证明优于纯在线强化学习。最后，通过神经网络实验验证了所提方法的实际有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of efficiently adapting an imperfect offline-learned Q-function to a new target environment using limited online interaction in reinforcement learning with general function approximation. The motivation stems from the need to leverage offline pretraining while overcoming its limitations through online fine-tuning. The method introduces a novel structural condition on the pretrained value functions and proposes O2O-LSVI, an algorithm with problem-dependent sample complexity. Experimental results include a minimax lower bound showing that adaptation can be as hard as pure online RL in some cases, but under the proposed condition, O2O-LSVI provably outperforms pure online RL, with neural-network experiments validating its practical effectiveness.
本文研究在一般函数逼近下，强化学习中的离线到在线价值适应问题，旨在利用有限的在线交互将不完美的离线预训练Q函数适应到目标环境。动机在于结合离线预训练的优势并通过在线微调克服其局限。方法提出了一种针对预训练价值函数的新颖结构条件，并设计了O2O-LSVI算法，该算法具有问题依赖的样本复杂度。实验结果包括一个极小极大下界，表明在某些困难实例中适应可能不优于纯在线强化学习，但在所提条件下，O2O-LSVI在理论上优于纯在线方法，神经网络实验也验证了其实际有效性。
Restless Bandits with Individual Penalty Constraints: A New Near-Optimal Index Policy and How to Learn It
Authors: Nida Zamir, I-Hong Hou
First: 2026-04-05T12:53:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:05:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates the Restless Multi-Armed Bandit (RMAB) framework under individual penalty constraints to address resource allocation challenges in dynamic wireless networked environments. Unlike conventional RMAB models, our model allows each user (arm) to have distinct and stringent performance constraints, such as energy limits, activation limits, or age of information minimums, enabling the capture of diverse objectives including fairness and efficiency. To find the optimal resource allocation policy, we propose a new Penalty-Optimal Whittle (POW) index policy. The POW index of an user only depends on the user's transition kernel and penalty constraints, and remains invariable to system-wide features such as the number of users present and the amount of resource available. This makes it computationally tractable to calculate the POW indices offline without any need for online adaptation. Moreover, we theoretically prove that the POW index policy is asymptotically optimal while satisfying all individual penalty constraints. We also introduce a deep reinforcement learning algorithm to efficiently learn the POW index on the fly. Simulation results across various applications and system configurations further demonstrate that the POW index policy not only has near-optimal performance but also significantly outperforms other existing policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：带个体惩罚约束的躁动多臂赌博机：一种新的近优索引策略及其学习方法
本文研究了个体惩罚约束下的躁动多臂赌博机（RMAB）框架，以应对动态无线网络环境中的资源分配挑战。与传统RMAB模型不同，本模型允许每个用户（臂）具有独立且严格的性能约束，如能量限制、激活限制或信息时效性下限，从而能够兼顾公平性与效率等多样化目标。为寻求最优资源分配策略，我们提出了一种新的惩罚最优惠特尔（POW）索引策略。用户的POW索引仅取决于其状态转移核与惩罚约束，且与系统规模（如用户数量、可用资源量）无关。这使得离线计算POW索引具有计算可行性，无需在线调整。理论证明该策略在满足所有个体惩罚约束的同时具有渐近最优性。我们还引入了一种深度强化学习算法以动态高效学习POW索引。多场景仿真结果表明，POW索引策略不仅具备近优性能，且显著优于现有其他策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to address resource allocation in dynamic wireless networks where users have distinct and stringent performance constraints, such as energy limits or age of information minimums, which are not captured by conventional Restless Multi-Armed Bandit (RMAB) models. The method introduces a new Penalty-Optimal Whittle (POW) index policy, where each user's index depends solely on its own transition kernel and penalty constraints, making it computationally tractable to compute offline without online adaptation. Experimental results from simulations across various applications show that the POW index policy is asymptotically optimal, satisfies all individual constraints, and outperforms existing policies in near-optimal performance.
本文的动机是解决动态无线网络中的资源分配问题，其中用户具有独特且严格的性能约束，如能量限制或信息年龄最小值，这是传统多臂赌博机模型所无法捕捉的。方法上提出了一种新的惩罚最优惠特尔指数策略，每个用户的指数仅取决于其自身的转移核和惩罚约束，使得离线计算变得易于处理，无需在线调整。在不同应用和系统配置的模拟实验中，结果表明该指数策略是渐近最优的，满足所有个体约束，并且在接近最优性能方面显著优于现有策略。
Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization
Authors: Yu Li, Sizhe Tang, Tian Lan
First: 2026-04-08T14:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T15:01:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：链中推理，树中学习：多轮智能体策略优化的自校正与嫁接方法
大语言模型智能体的强化学习常受多步推理任务中稀疏奖励的制约。现有方法（如组相对策略优化）将采样轨迹视为独立链，对每条链的所有步骤赋予均匀奖励，忽略了可能对推理结果产生不成比例影响的关键步骤。本文提出T-STAR（树状结构自教导智能体校正）框架，该框架能还原看似独立轨迹间的潜在关联奖励结构。具体而言，我们通过识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点，将轨迹整合为统一的认知树。该结构支持内省评估机制，将轨迹级奖励沿树反向传播，从而获得步骤级方差缩减的相对优势新度量。基于认知树，我们还开发了上下文思维嫁接技术，通过对比关键分歧点/步骤的成功与失败分支来合成校正推理。随后，我们提出的精准策略优化利用布拉德利-特里型精准损失函数，聚焦于这些关键点/步骤的丰富策略梯度信息。在具身交互、推理与规划基准上的大量实验表明，T-STAR在强基线模型上实现了持续改进，在需要长链推理的任务中增益尤为显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sparse rewards in reinforcement learning for multi-turn LLM agents, where existing methods fail to differentiate critical reasoning steps. The proposed T-STAR framework consolidates sampled trajectories into a Cognitive Tree to uncover latent reward structures, enabling introspective valuation for step-level advantage estimation and in-context thought grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning from successful and failed branches. Experimental results across diverse benchmarks show that T-STAR consistently outperforms baselines, particularly in tasks with long reasoning chains.
该论文针对多轮大型语言模型智能体强化学习中奖励稀疏的问题，现有方法未能区分关键推理步骤。提出的T-STAR框架将采样轨迹整合为认知树以揭示潜在奖励结构，通过内省评估实现步骤级优势估计，并利用上下文思维嫁接从成功和失败分支中合成纠正推理。在多个基准测试中的实验结果表明，T-STAR持续优于基线方法，尤其在需要长推理链的任务中提升最为显著。
DiPO: Disentangled Perplexity Policy Optimization for Fine-grained Exploration-Exploitation Trade-Off
Authors: Xiaofan Li, Ming Yang, Zhiyuan Ma, Shichao Ma, Jintao Du, Yu Cheng, Weiqiang Wang, Zhizhong Zhang, Xin Tan, Yanyun Qu, Lizhuang Ma, Yuan Xie
First: 2026-04-15T14:12:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T14:12:10+00:00
Comments: LLM Reinforce Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed significant advances in the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, effectively managing the exploration and exploitation trade-off remains a critical challenge. In this paper, we fully analyze the exploration and exploitation dilemma of extremely hard and easy samples during the training and propose a new fine-grained trade-off mechanism. Concretely, we introduce a perplexity space disentangling strategy that divides the sample space into distinct exploration (high perplexity) and exploitation (low perplexity) subspaces, thereby mining fine-grained samples requiring exploration-exploitation trade-off. Subsequently, we propose a bidirectional reward allocation mechanism with a minimum impact on verification rewards to implement perplexity-guided exploration and exploitation, enabling more stable policy optimization. Finally, we have evaluated our method on two mainstream tasks: mathematical reasoning and function calling, and experimental results demonstrate the superiority of the proposed method, confirming its effectiveness in enhancing LLM performance by fine-grained exploration-exploitation trade-off.

标题：DiPO：面向细粒度探索-利用权衡的解耦困惑度策略优化
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著推动了大型语言模型（LLM）推理能力的发展，但如何有效管理探索与利用的权衡仍是关键挑战。本文深入分析了训练过程中极难与极易样本的探索-利用困境，提出一种新的细粒度权衡机制。具体而言，我们引入一种困惑度空间解耦策略，将样本空间划分为独立的探索（高困惑度）与利用（低困惑度）子空间，从而挖掘需要探索-利用权衡的细粒度样本。随后，我们提出一种对验证奖励影响最小的双向奖励分配机制，实现困惑度引导的探索与利用，使策略优化更稳定。最后，我们在数学推理和函数调用两个主流任务上评估了本方法，实验结果证明了所提方法的优越性，证实了其通过细粒度探索-利用权衡提升LLM性能的有效性。

The paper addresses the challenge of managing the exploration-exploitation trade-off in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models (LLMs), particularly for extremely hard and easy training samples. It proposes DiPO, a method that introduces a perplexity space disentangling strategy to partition the sample space into high-perplexity (exploration) and low-perplexity (exploitation) subspaces, enabling fine-grained identification of samples requiring trade-off. A bidirectional reward allocation mechanism is then applied with minimal impact on verification rewards to guide perplexity-based exploration and exploitation for stable policy optimization. Experimental evaluations on mathematical reasoning and function calling tasks demonstrate the method's superiority in enhancing LLM performance through this fine-grained trade-off approach.

Beyond Conservative Automated Driving in Multi-Agent Scenarios via Coupled Model Predictive Control and Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Saeed Rahmani, Gözde Körpe, Zhenlin, Xu, Bruno Brito, Simeon Craig Calvert, Bart van Arem
First: 2026-04-15T13:58:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T13:58:38+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automated driving at unsignalized intersections is challenging due to complex multi-vehicle interactions and the need to balance safety and efficiency. Model Predictive Control (MPC) offers structured constraint handling through optimization but relies on hand-crafted rules that often produce overly conservative behavior. Deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) learns adaptive behaviors from experience but often struggles with safety assurance and generalization to unseen environments. In this study, we present an integrated MPC-RL framework to improve navigation performance in multi-agent scenarios. Experiments show that MPC-RL outperforms standalone MPC and end-to-end RL across three traffic-density levels. Collectively, MPC-RL reduces the collision rate by 21% and improves the success rate by 6.5% compared to pure MPC. We further evaluate zero-shot transfer to a highway merging scenario without retraining. Both MPC-based methods transfer substantially better than end-to-end PPO, which highlights the role of the MPC backbone in cross-scenario robustness. The framework also shows faster loss stabilization than end-to-end RL during training, which indicates a reduced learning burden. These results suggest that the integrated approach can improve the balance between safety performance and efficiency in multi-agent intersection scenarios, while the MPC component provides a strong foundation for generalization across driving environments. The implementation code is available open-source.
