Three Roles, One Model: Role Orchestration at Inference Time to Close the Performance Gap Between Small and Large Agents
Authors: S. Aaron McClendon, Jorge Gallego-Feliciano, Stavros Zervoudakis, Antonios Saravanos
First: 2026-04-13T13:40:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T13:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents show promise on realistic tool-use tasks, but deploying capable agents on modest hardware remains challenging. We study whether inference-time scaffolding alone, without any additional training compute, can improve the performance of a small model in complex multi-step environments. Operating on a single 24GB GPU, we evaluate Qwen3-8B on the AppWorld benchmark under both full-precision and 4-bit quantized configurations. Without any intervention, the raw model achieves just 5.4% (FP16) and 3.0% (AWQ) task goal completion. Guided by a systematic failure mode analysis, we introduce a three-tier inference scaffolding pipeline that deploys the same frozen model in three distinct roles: (1) a summarization model that preserves critical artifacts (tokens, credentials, API responses) while compressing dialogue history; (2) the main agent model that reasons over the compressed context; and (3) an isolated correction model that reviews and revises the agent's code output without access to conversation history, breaking repetitive failure loops. Applied to the same unmodified model, this scaffolding yields 8.9% (FP16) and 5.9% (AWQ) task goal completion, roughly doubling performance in both settings, with particularly strong gains on difficulty-1 tasks (15.8% to 26.3% FP16; 5.3% to 14.0% AWQ). On full-precision inference, our scaffolded 8B model surpasses DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct (7.1%) from the original AppWorld evaluation, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with systems 4 times their size. We formalize the approach as a scaffolded policy over a frozen base model, three invocations of the same weights with different conditioning, drawing connections to test-time compute scaling and action-space shaping in reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：三重角色，单一模型：通过推理时角色编排缩小大小智能体间的性能差距
大语言模型智能体在现实工具使用任务中展现出潜力，但在有限硬件上部署高性能智能体仍具挑战。本研究探讨仅通过推理时架构支持（无需额外训练计算）能否提升小模型在复杂多步环境中的性能。我们在单张24GB GPU上，评估了Qwen3-8B模型在AppWorld基准测试中的全精度与4位量化配置表现。未经干预时，原始模型任务目标完成率仅为5.4%（FP16）和3.0%（AWQ）。基于系统性故障模式分析，我们引入三层推理架构流水线，将同一冻结模型部署于三个独立角色：（1）摘要模型——在压缩对话历史时保留关键信息（令牌、凭证、API响应）；（2）主智能体模型——在压缩上下文中进行推理；（3）独立校正模型——在无法访问对话历史的情况下审查并修正智能体的代码输出，打破重复故障循环。将此架构应用于同一未修改模型后，任务目标完成率提升至8.9%（FP16）和5.9%（AWQ），两种设置下性能均实现约两倍提升，在难度1任务上增益尤为显著（FP16：15.8%→26.3%；AWQ：5.3%→14.0%）。全精度推理时，经架构优化的8B模型超越了原始AppWorld评估中的DeepSeek-Coder 33B Instruct（7.1%），证明结构化推理时干预能使小模型与四倍体量系统竞争。我们将该方法形式化为冻结基础模型的架构化策略——通过三种不同条件调用同一权重参数，建立了与强化学习中测试时计算扩展及动作空间塑形的理论联系。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the challenge of deploying capable language model agents on modest hardware, aiming to close the performance gap between small and large models through inference-time scaffolding alone, without additional training. The method introduces a three-tier pipeline that orchestrates a single frozen small model (Qwen3-8B) into three distinct roles: a summarization model to compress dialogue history, a main agent for reasoning, and an isolated correction model to review and revise code outputs, thereby breaking repetitive failure loops. Experimental results on the AppWorld benchmark show that this scaffolding roughly doubles task goal completion rates, from 5.4% to 8.9% in FP16 and from 3.0% to 5.9% in 4-bit quantization, with the scaffolded 8B model even surpassing a 33B model from prior evaluations, demonstrating that structured inference-time interventions can make small models competitive with much larger ones.
本研究旨在解决在有限硬件上部署高效能语言模型智能体的挑战，其动机是通过仅使用推理时脚手架技术，在不增加训练计算的情况下，缩小小型与大型模型之间的性能差距。方法上，提出了一个三层推理管道，将同一个冻结的小型模型（Qwen3-8B）编排为三个不同角色：用于压缩对话历史的摘要模型、进行推理的主智能体模型，以及独立审查和修正代码输出的校正模型，从而打破重复失败循环。在AppWorld基准测试上的实验结果表明，该脚手架使任务目标完成率大致翻倍，从FP16的5.4%提升至8.9%，从4位量化的3.0%提升至5.9%，并且经过脚手架处理的8B模型甚至超越了先前评估中的33B模型，证明了结构化推理时干预能使小模型与规模大得多的模型相竞争。
RPS: Information Elicitation with Reinforcement Prompt Selection
Authors: Tao Wang, Jingyao Lu, Xibo Wang, Haonan Huang, Su Yao, Zhiqiang Hu, Xingyan Chen, Enmao Diao
First: 2026-04-15T12:51:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:51:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have shown remarkable capabilities in dialogue generation and reasoning, yet their effectiveness in eliciting user-known but concealed information in open-ended conversations remains limited. In many interactive AI applications, such as personal assistants, tutoring systems, and legal or clinical support, users often withhold sensitive or uncertain information due to privacy concerns, ambiguity, or social hesitation. This makes it challenging for LLMs to gather complete and contextually relevant inputs. In this work, we define the problem of information elicitation in open-ended dialogue settings and propose Reinforcement Prompt Selection (RPS), a lightweight reinforcement learning framework that formulates prompt selection as a sequential decision-making problem. To analyze this problem in a controlled setting, we design a synthetic experiment, where a reinforcement learning agent outperforms a random query baseline, illustrating the potential of policy-based approaches for adaptive information elicitation. Building on this insight, RPS learns a policy over a pool of prompts to adaptively elicit concealed or incompletely expressed information from users through dialogue. We also introduce IELegal, a new benchmark dataset constructed from real legal case documents, which simulates dialogue-based information elicitation tasks aimed at uncovering case-relevant facts. In this setting, RPS outperforms static prompt baselines, demonstrating the effectiveness of adaptive prompt selection for eliciting critical information in LLM-driven dialogue systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RPS：基于强化提示选择的信息引导方法
大语言模型在对话生成与推理方面展现出卓越能力，但在开放式对话中引导用户已知却隐藏信息的效果仍有限。在个人助手、教学系统、法律或临床支持等交互式AI应用中，用户常因隐私顾虑、表述模糊或社交迟疑而隐瞒敏感或不确定信息，导致大语言模型难以获取完整且上下文相关的输入。本研究定义了开放式对话场景中的信息引导问题，提出强化提示选择框架——一种将提示选择建模为序列决策问题的轻量级强化学习方法。通过设计合成实验进行可控分析，强化学习智能体在随机查询基线对比中表现更优，验证了基于策略的自适应信息引导方法的潜力。基于此，RPS通过对话从提示池中学习策略，自适应引导用户透露隐藏或未完整表达的信息。同时，我们构建了IELegal基准数据集——基于真实法律案例文档构建，模拟旨在挖掘案件相关事实的对话式信息引导任务。在该场景中，RPS显著优于静态提示基线，证明了自适应提示选择在LLM驱动对话系统中引导关键信息的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of eliciting concealed or incompletely expressed information from users in open-ended dialogues with large language models (LLMs), motivated by applications like personal assistants and legal support where users may withhold sensitive details. It proposes Reinforcement Prompt Selection (RPS), a lightweight reinforcement learning framework that treats prompt selection as a sequential decision-making problem to adaptively query users. Experimental results from a synthetic setup show RPS outperforms random query baselines, and on the newly introduced IELegal benchmark based on real legal cases, it surpasses static prompt methods, demonstrating its effectiveness in uncovering critical information in LLM-driven dialogues.
本文针对大型语言模型在开放对话中难以获取用户已知但隐藏信息的问题展开研究，动机源于个人助理和法律支持等应用场景中用户常因隐私或不确定性而隐瞒信息。方法上提出了强化提示选择框架，将提示选择建模为序列决策问题，通过强化学习自适应地引导用户透露信息。实验结果表明，在合成设置中该框架优于随机查询基线，并在基于真实法律案例构建的IELegal基准测试中超越了静态提示方法，验证了其在对话系统中有效获取关键信息的能力。
AlphaCNOT: Learning CNOT Minimization with Model-Based Planning
Authors: Jacopo Cossio, Daniele Lizzio Bosco, Riccardo Romanello, Giuseppe Serra, Carla Piazza
First: 2026-04-15T12:46:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:46:40+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 11 figures , journal
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum circuit optimization is a central task in Quantum Computing, as current Noisy Intermediate Scale Quantum devices suffer from error propagation that often scales with the number of operations. Among quantum operations, the CNOT gate is of fundamental importance, being the only 2-qubit gate in the universal Clifford+T set. The problem of CNOT gates minimization has been addressed by heuristic algorithms such as the well-known Patel-Markov-Hayes (PMH) for linear reversible synthesis (i.e., CNOT minimization with no topological constraints), and more recently by Reinforcement Learning (RL) based strategies in the more complex case of topology-aware synthesis, where each CNOT can act on a subset of all qubits pairs. In this work we introduce AlphaCNOT, a RL framework based on Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) that address effectively the CNOT minimization problem by modeling it as a planning problem. In contrast to other RL- based solution, our method is model-based, i.e. it can leverage lookahead search to evaluate future trajectories, thus finding more efficient sequences of CNOTs. Our method achieves a reduction of up to 32% in CNOT gate count compared to PMH baseline on linear reversible synthesis, while in the constraint version we report a consistent gate count reduction on a variety of topologies with up to 8 qubits, with respect to state-of-the-art RL-based solutions. Our results suggest the combination of RL with search-based strategies can be applied to different circuit optimization tasks, such as Clifford minimization, thus fostering the transition toward the "quantum utility" era.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AlphaCNOT：基于模型规划学习的CNOT门最小化方法
量子电路优化是量子计算的核心任务，当前噪声中等规模量子设备受误差传播影响，其程度常随操作数量增加而加剧。在量子操作中，CNOT门具有基础重要性，是通用Clifford+T集合中唯一的双量子比特门。CNOT门最小化问题已通过启发式算法得到研究，如线性可逆综合中著名的Patel-Markov-Hayes算法，以及近期在更复杂的拓扑感知综合中采用基于强化学习的方法。本文提出AlphaCNOT——基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的强化学习框架，通过将问题建模为规划任务有效解决CNOT最小化问题。区别于其他基于强化学习的方案，本方法采用模型化设计，可利用前瞻搜索评估未来轨迹，从而发现更高效的CNOT序列。在线性可逆综合中，本方法相较PMH基线实现CNOT门数量最高32%的缩减；在约束版本中，针对最多8量子比特的多种拓扑结构，相较前沿强化学习方案实现了持续的门数量优化。结果表明，强化学习与搜索策略的结合可扩展至其他电路优化任务，如Clifford最小化，从而推动向'量子效用'时代的演进。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the critical need for quantum circuit optimization to mitigate error propagation in Noisy Intermediate Scale Quantum devices by focusing on minimizing CNOT gates, which are fundamental but error-prone two-qubit operations. The authors introduce AlphaCNOT, a model-based reinforcement learning framework that employs Monte Carlo Tree Search to treat CNOT minimization as a planning problem, enabling lookahead search to evaluate future trajectories and identify more efficient gate sequences. Experimental results demonstrate that AlphaCNOT reduces CNOT gate counts by up to 32% compared to the Patel-Markov-Hayes baseline in linear reversible synthesis and consistently outperforms state-of-the-art RL methods in topology-aware synthesis across various configurations with up to 8 qubits, suggesting broader applicability to tasks like Clifford minimization for advancing quantum utility.
本文针对当前噪声中等规模量子设备中误差随操作数量增加而传播的问题，聚焦于减少关键的双量子比特CNOT门数量以优化量子电路。作者提出了AlphaCNOT，一种基于模型的强化学习框架，利用蒙特卡洛树搜索将CNOT最小化建模为规划问题，通过前瞻搜索评估未来轨迹以找到更高效的门序列。实验结果表明，在线性可逆合成中，AlphaCNOT相比Patel-Markov-Hayes基准方法将CNOT门数量减少了高达32%；在拓扑感知合成中，对于最多8个量子比特的各种配置，该方法也持续优于现有的强化学习解决方案，表明其可扩展至如Clifford最小化等其他电路优化任务，推动量子实用化发展。
Character Beyond Speech: Leveraging Role-Playing Evaluation in Audio Large Language Models via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dongjie Fu, Fangming Feng, Xize Cheng, Linjun Li, Zhou Zhao, Tao Jin
First: 2026-04-15T12:39:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:39:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid evolution of multimodal large models has revolutionized the simulation of diverse characters in speech dialogue systems, enabling a novel interactive paradigm. Character attributes are manifested not only in textual responses but also through vocal features, as speech conveys rich paralinguistic information that is challenging to quantify. This poses significant difficulties in evaluating the character alignment of role-playing agents. To address these challenges, we present RoleJudge, an evaluation framework that leverages audio large language models to systematically assess the alignment between speech and character across multiple modalities and dimensions. Furthermore, we introduce RoleChat, the first voice role-playing evaluation dataset enriched with chain-of-thought reasoning annotations, comprising a diverse set of authentic and LLM-generated speech samples. Utilizing this dataset, we implement a multi-stage training paradigm and incorporate Standard Alignment in reinforcement learning to mitigate reward misalignment during optimization. Experimental results in terms of accuracy and subjective assessment demonstrate that RoleJudge outperforms various baseline models, validating the effectiveness of our multidimensional evaluation framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越言语的角色：通过强化学习在音频大语言模型中利用角色扮演评估
多模态大模型的快速发展革新了语音对话系统中多样化角色的模拟，催生了一种新颖的交互范式。角色属性不仅体现在文本回应中，还通过语音特征展现，因为语音传递了丰富的副语言信息，这些信息难以量化。这给评估角色扮演代理的角色一致性带来了显著挑战。为解决这些问题，我们提出了RoleJudge评估框架，该框架利用音频大语言模型，系统性地评估跨多种模态和维度的语音与角色一致性。此外，我们引入了RoleChat，这是首个富含思维链推理注释的语音角色扮演评估数据集，包含多样化的真实和LLM生成的语音样本。利用该数据集，我们实施了一个多阶段训练范式，并在强化学习中融入标准对齐，以缓解优化过程中的奖励错位问题。在准确性和主观评估方面的实验结果表明，RoleJudge优于多种基线模型，验证了我们多维评估框架的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of evaluating character alignment in speech dialogue systems, where vocal features convey rich paralinguistic information beyond text, this paper introduces RoleJudge, a framework that uses audio large language models to assess speech-character alignment across multiple modalities and dimensions. The method involves creating RoleChat, a voice role-playing dataset with chain-of-thought annotations, and implementing a multi-stage training paradigm with Standard Alignment in reinforcement learning to address reward misalignment. Experimental results show that RoleJudge outperforms baseline models in both accuracy and subjective assessments, validating its effectiveness as a multidimensional evaluation tool.
本文的动机源于评估语音对话系统中角色对齐的挑战，其中语音特征传达了超越文本的丰富副语言信息，难以量化。为此，研究提出了RoleJudge框架，利用音频大语言模型从多模态和多维度系统评估语音与角色的对齐性。方法包括创建RoleChat——首个带有思维链推理注释的语音角色扮演数据集，并采用多阶段训练范式，在强化学习中引入标准对齐以优化奖励偏差。实验结果表明，RoleJudge在准确性和主观评估上均优于多种基线模型，验证了该多维评估框架的有效性。
Soft $Q(λ)$: A multi-step off-policy method for entropy regularised reinforcement learning using eligibility traces
Authors: Pranav Mahajan, Ben Seymour
First: 2026-04-15T12:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T12:10:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Soft Q-learning has emerged as a versatile model-free method for entropy-regularised reinforcement learning, optimising for returns augmented with a penalty on the divergence from a reference policy. Despite its success, the multi-step extensions of soft Q-learning remain relatively unexplored and limited to on-policy action sampling under the Boltzmann policy. In this brief research note, we first present a formal $n$-step formulation for soft Q-learning and then extend this framework to the fully off-policy case by introducing a novel Soft Tree Backup operator. Finally, we unify these developments into Soft $Q(λ)$, an elegant online, off-policy, eligibility trace framework that allows for efficient credit assignment under arbitrary behaviour policies. Our derivations propose a model-free method for learning entropy-regularised value functions that can be utilised in future empirical experiments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Soft $Q(λ)$：一种基于资格迹的多步离策略熵正则化强化学习方法
Soft Q-learning 已成为一种通用的无模型熵正则化强化学习方法，通过优化回报并惩罚与参考策略的差异来实现。尽管其成功，soft Q-learning 的多步扩展仍相对未被充分探索，且局限于玻尔兹曼策略下的同策略动作采样。在本研究简报中，我们首先提出了 soft Q-learning 的正式 $n$ 步公式，随后通过引入一种新颖的 Soft Tree Backup 算子，将该框架扩展至完全离策略场景。最后，我们将这些进展统一为 Soft $Q(λ)$——一个优雅的在线、离策略、基于资格迹的框架，能够在任意行为策略下实现高效的信用分配。我们的推导提出了一种用于学习熵正则化价值函数的无模型方法，可供未来实证实验使用。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend soft Q-learning, a model-free entropy-regularised reinforcement learning method, to multi-step and fully off-policy settings, as existing extensions are limited to on-policy sampling. The method introduces a formal n-step formulation and a novel Soft Tree Backup operator, culminating in Soft Q(λ), an online, off-policy eligibility trace framework that enables efficient credit assignment under arbitrary behaviour policies. The main experimental results are not detailed in the abstract, but the derivations propose a model-free approach for learning entropy-regularised value functions intended for future empirical validation.
本文的动机在于需要将软Q学习（一种无模型的熵正则化强化学习方法）扩展到多步和完全离策略设置，因为现有扩展仅限于在策略采样。方法上，提出了一个正式的n步公式和一个新颖的软树回溯算子，最终形成了软Q(λ)，这是一个在线、离策略的资格迹框架，能够在任意行为策略下实现高效的信用分配。摘要中未详述主要实验结果，但推导提出了一种用于学习熵正则化价值函数的无模型方法，旨在供未来的实证实验使用。
RL-PLUS: Countering Capability Boundary Collapse of LLMs in Reinforcement Learning with Hybrid-policy Optimization
Authors: Yihong Dong, Xue Jiang, Yongding Tao, Huanyu Liu, Kechi Zhang, Lili Mou, Rongyu Cao, Yingwei Ma, Jue Chen, Binhua Li, Zhi Jin, Fei Huang, Yongbin Li, Ge Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-07-31T23:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:41:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (main)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) has significantly advanced the complex reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, it struggles to break through the inherent capability boundaries of the base LLM, due to its essentially on-policy strategy coupled with LLM's immense action space and sparse reward. Critically, RLVR can lead to the capability boundary collapse, narrowing the LLM's problem-solving scope. To address this problem, we propose RL-PLUS, a novel hybrid-policy optimization approach for LLMs that synergizes internal exploitation with external data to achieve stronger reasoning capabilities and surpass the boundaries of base models. RL-PLUS integrates two core components, i.e., Multiple Importance Sampling to address distributional mismatch from external data, and Exploration-Based Advantage Function to guide the model towards high-value, unexplored reasoning paths. We provide both theoretical analysis and extensive experiments to demonstrate the superiority and generalizability of our approach. Compared with existing RLVR methods, RL-PLUS achieves 1) state-of-the-art performance on six math reasoning benchmarks; 2) superior performance on six out-of-distribution reasoning tasks; 3) consistent and significant gains across diverse model families, with average relative improvements up to 69.2\%. Moreover, the analysis of Pass@k curves indicates that RL-PLUS effectively resolves the capability boundary collapse problem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-PLUS：通过混合策略优化应对大语言模型在强化学习中的能力边界坍缩
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的复杂推理能力，但由于其本质上的同策略特性，结合LLMs庞大的动作空间与稀疏奖励，难以突破基础LLM固有的能力边界。关键的是，RLVR可能导致能力边界坍缩，缩小LLM的解决问题范围。为解决此问题，我们提出RL-PLUS——一种新颖的混合策略优化方法，通过协同内部开发与外部数据，实现更强的推理能力并超越基础模型边界。RL-PLUS整合了两个核心组件：多重重要性采样以解决外部数据的分布失配问题，以及基于探索的优势函数以引导模型走向高价值、未探索的推理路径。我们通过理论分析和大量实验证明了该方法的优越性与泛化能力。与现有RLVR方法相比，RL-PLUS实现了：1）在六个数学推理基准上达到最先进性能；2）在六个分布外推理任务上表现优异；3）在不同模型家族中取得一致且显著的提升，平均相对改进高达69.2%。此外，Pass@k曲线分析表明RL-PLUS有效解决了能力边界坍缩问题。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of capability boundary collapse in Large Language Models (LLMs) during Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR), where on-policy strategies limit performance due to the LLM's vast action space and sparse rewards. To overcome this, the authors propose RL-PLUS, a hybrid-policy optimization method that combines internal exploitation with external data, utilizing Multiple Importance Sampling to handle distributional mismatches and an Exploration-Based Advantage Function to guide exploration of high-value reasoning paths. Experimental results show that RL-PLUS achieves state-of-the-art performance on six math reasoning benchmarks, superior out-of-distribution generalization on six tasks, and consistent gains across model families with average improvements up to 69.2%, effectively mitigating capability boundary collapse as evidenced by Pass@k curve analysis.
本文针对大型语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中因策略内策略、巨大动作空间和稀疏奖励导致的模型能力边界崩溃问题，提出了一种名为RL-PLUS的混合策略优化方法。该方法通过结合内部利用和外部数据，采用多重重要性采样处理分布不匹配，并利用基于探索的优势函数引导模型探索高价值推理路径。实验结果表明，RL-PLUS在六个数学推理基准上取得了最先进的性能，在六个分布外推理任务上表现优异，并在不同模型系列中实现了高达69.2%的平均相对提升，通过Pass@k曲线分析证实其有效解决了能力边界崩溃问题。
Think Outside the Policy: In-Context Steered Policy Optimization
Authors: Hsiu-Yuan Huang, Chenming Tang, Weijie Liu, Clive Bai, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-10-30T14:14:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:36:27+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings. 19 pages, 13 figures, 12 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), have achieved remarkable progress in improving the reasoning capabilities of Large Reasoning Models (LRMs). However, they exhibit limited exploration due to reliance on on-policy rollouts which are confined to the current policy's distribution, resulting in narrow trajectory diversity. Recent approaches attempt to expand policy coverage by incorporating trajectories generated from stronger expert models, yet this reliance increases computational cost and such advanced models are often inaccessible. To address these issues, we propose In-Context Steered Policy Optimization (ICPO), a unified framework that leverages the inherent in-context learning capability of LRMs to provide expert guidance using existing datasets. ICPO introduces mixed-policy GRPO with implicit expert forcing, which expands exploration beyond the current policy distribution without requiring advanced LRM trajectories. To further stabilize optimization, ICPO integrates expert region reject sampling to filter unreliable off-policy trajectories and annealed expert-bonus reward shaping to balance early expert guidance with later autonomous improvement. Results demonstrate that ICPO consistently enhances RLVR performance and training stability on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, revealing a scalable and effective RLVR paradigm for LRMs. Our code is available at https://github.com/Celine-hxy/ICPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破策略局限：上下文引导策略优化
现有可验证奖励强化学习方法（如GRPO）在提升大型推理模型能力方面取得显著进展，但其依赖当前策略分布内的同策略轨迹，导致探索受限与轨迹多样性不足。近期研究尝试引入专家模型轨迹以扩展策略覆盖，但会带来计算成本增加且依赖难以获取的先进模型。为此，我们提出上下文引导策略优化框架，利用大型推理模型固有的上下文学习能力，通过现有数据集提供专家指导。该框架引入隐式专家强化的混合策略GRPO，无需依赖先进模型轨迹即可突破当前策略分布的探索限制。为进一步稳定优化，本方法集成专家区域拒绝采样以过滤不可靠的异策略轨迹，并采用退火专家奖励塑形来平衡早期专家指导与后期自主改进。实验表明，该方法在数学推理基准上持续提升可验证奖励强化学习的性能与训练稳定性，为大型推理模型提供了一种可扩展的有效范式。代码已开源。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limited exploration in existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods like GRPO, which rely on on-policy rollouts that constrain trajectory diversity, and the computational cost or inaccessibility of using stronger expert models for guidance. To overcome these issues, it proposes In-Context Steered Policy Optimization (ICPO), a unified framework that leverages the in-context learning capability of Large Reasoning Models to provide expert guidance from existing datasets, employing mixed-policy GRPO with implicit expert forcing to expand exploration without advanced models, along with expert region reject sampling and annealed expert-bonus reward shaping for stability. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that ICPO consistently improves RLVR performance and training stability, offering a scalable and effective paradigm for LRMs.
本文针对现有可验证奖励强化学习方法（如GRPO）因依赖当前策略分布内的策略内采样而探索有限、轨迹多样性不足的问题，以及使用更强专家模型带来计算成本高或模型不可访问的局限性，提出了上下文引导策略优化框架。该方法利用大型推理模型固有的上下文学习能力，从现有数据集中获取专家指导，通过混合策略GRPO与隐式专家强制来扩展探索范围，无需高级模型轨迹，并结合专家区域拒绝采样和退火专家奖励塑形以稳定优化。在数学推理基准测试中，结果表明该框架能持续提升RLVR性能与训练稳定性，为大型推理模型提供了一种可扩展且有效的强化学习范式。
Jump-Start Reinforcement Learning with Vision-Language-Action Regularization
Authors: Angelo Moroncelli, Roberto Zanetti, Marco Maccarini, Loris Roveda
First: 2026-04-15T11:17:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T11:17:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) enables high-frequency, closed-loop control for robotic manipulation, but scaling to long-horizon tasks with sparse or imperfect rewards remains difficult due to inefficient exploration and poor credit assignment. Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models leverage large-scale multimodal pretraining to provide generalist, task-level reasoning, but current limitations hinder their direct use in fast and precise manipulation. In this paper, we propose Vision-Language-Action Jump-Starting (VLAJS), a method that bridges sparse VLA guidance with on-policy RL to improve exploration and learning efficiency. VLAJS treats VLAs as transient sources of high-level action suggestions that bias early exploration and improve credit assignment, while preserving the high-frequency, state-based control of RL. Our approach augments Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with a directional action-consistency regularization that softly aligns the RL agent's actions with VLA guidance during early training, without enforcing strict imitation, requiring demonstrations, or relying on continuous teacher queries. VLA guidance is applied sparsely and annealed over time, allowing the agent to adapt online and ultimately surpass the guiding policy. We evaluate VLAJS on six challenging manipulation tasks: lifting, pick-and-place, peg reorientation, peg insertion, poking, and pushing in simulation, and validate a subset on a real Franka Panda robot. VLAJS consistently outperforms PPO and distillation-style baselines in sample efficiency, reducing required environment interactions by over 50% in several tasks. Real-world experiments demonstrate zero-shot sim-to-real transfer and robust execution under clutter, object variation, and external perturbations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于视觉-语言-动作正则化的强化学习快速启动方法
强化学习（RL）能够实现机器人操作的高频闭环控制，但由于探索效率低下和信用分配困难，在稀疏或不完美奖励的长周期任务中仍难以扩展。视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通过大规模多模态预训练提供通用任务级推理能力，但现有局限阻碍了其在快速精确操作中的直接应用。本文提出视觉-语言-动作快速启动（VLAJS）方法，通过稀疏VLA指导与在线策略RL的桥接来提升探索和学习效率。VLAJS将VLA模型视为高层动作建议的瞬态源，在早期探索阶段提供偏向性引导并改进信用分配，同时保留RL基于状态的高频控制特性。该方法通过方向性动作一致性正则化增强近端策略优化（PPO），在训练初期将智能体动作与VLA指导进行软对齐，无需强制严格模仿、演示数据或持续教师查询。VLA指导以稀疏方式随时间退火应用，使智能体能够在线适应并最终超越指导策略。我们在六项挑战性操作任务（模拟环境中的抓举、取放、钉孔重定向、钉孔插入、推触和推动）上评估VLAJS，并在真实Franka Panda机器人上验证了子集任务。VLAJS在样本效率上持续优于PPO和蒸馏式基线方法，在多项任务中减少超过50%的环境交互需求。真实世界实验展示了零样本仿真到实物的迁移能力，以及在杂乱场景、物体变化和外部干扰下的鲁棒执行性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling reinforcement learning (RL) for long-horizon robotic manipulation tasks, where sparse rewards and inefficient exploration hinder performance, while Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models offer high-level task reasoning but lack precise, high-frequency control. The proposed method, Vision-Language-Action Jump-Starting (VLAJS), bridges this gap by using VLA models to provide sparse, high-level action suggestions that bias early RL exploration, augmented with a directional action-consistency regularization within Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) to softly align RL actions with VLA guidance without strict imitation or continuous queries. Towards Fine-grained Temporal Perception: Post-Training Large Audio-Language Models with Audio-Side Time Prompt
Authors: Yanfeng Shi, Pengfei Cai, Jun Liu, Qing Gu, Nan Jiang, Lirong Dai, Ian McLoughlin, Yan Song
First: 2026-04-15T10:50:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T10:50:29+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Interspeech 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Audio-Language Models (LALMs) enable general audio understanding and demonstrate remarkable performance across various audio tasks. However, these models still face challenges in temporal perception (e.g., inferring event onset and offset), leading to limited utility in fine-grained scenarios. To address this issue, we propose Audio-Side Time Prompt and leverage Reinforcement Learning (RL) to develop the TimePro-RL framework for fine-grained temporal perception. Specifically, we encode timestamps as embeddings and interleave them within the audio feature sequence as temporal coordinates to prompt the model. Furthermore, we introduce RL following Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) to directly optimize temporal alignment performance. Experiments demonstrate that TimePro-RL achieves significant performance gains across a range of audio temporal tasks, such as audio grounding, sound event detection, and dense audio captioning, validating its robust effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向细粒度时序感知：基于音频侧时间提示的大规模音频-语言模型后训练
大规模音频-语言模型（LALMs）实现了通用音频理解，并在多种音频任务中展现出卓越性能。然而，这些模型在时序感知（如推断事件起始与结束）方面仍面临挑战，导致其在细粒度场景中的应用受限。为解决此问题，我们提出音频侧时间提示，并利用强化学习（RL）构建了TimePro-RL框架以提升细粒度时序感知能力。具体而言，我们将时间戳编码为嵌入向量，并将其作为时序坐标交错插入音频特征序列中以引导模型。此外，我们在监督微调（SFT）后引入RL，直接优化时序对齐性能。实验表明，TimePro-RL在音频定位、声音事件检测和密集音频描述等一系列音频时序任务中均取得显著性能提升，验证了其强健的有效性。

Experimental results show that TimePro-RL achieves significant performance improvements on tasks including audio grounding, sound event detection, and dense audio captioning, demonstrating its robust effectiveness for temporal understanding.

Reward Hacking in the Era of Large Models: Mechanisms, Emergent Misalignment, Challenges
Authors: Xiaohua Wang, Muzhao Tian, Yuqi Zeng, Zisu Huang, Jiakang Yuan, Bowen Chen, Jingwen Xu, Mingbo Zhou, Wenhao Liu, Muling Wu, Zhengkang Guo, Qi Qian, Yifei Wang, Feiran Zhang, Ruicheng Yin, Shihan Dou, Changze Lv, Tao Chen, Kaitao Song, Xu Tan, Tao Gui, Xiaoqing Zheng, Xuanjing Huang
First: 2026-04-15T08:11:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T08:11:34+00:00
Comments: 42 pages, 5 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and related alignment paradigms have become central to steering large language models (LLMs) and multimodal large language models (MLLMs) toward human-preferred behaviors. However, these approaches introduce a systemic vulnerability: reward hacking, where models exploit imperfections in learned reward signals to maximize proxy objectives without fulfilling true task intent. As models scale and optimization intensifies, such exploitation manifests as verbosity bias, sycophancy, hallucinated justification, benchmark overfitting, and, in multimodal settings, perception--reasoning decoupling and evaluator manipulation. Recent evidence further suggests that seemingly benign shortcut behaviors can generalize into broader forms of misalignment, including deception and strategic gaming of oversight mechanisms. In this survey, we propose the Proxy Compression Hypothesis (PCH) as a unifying framework for understanding reward hacking. We formalize reward hacking as an emergent consequence of optimizing expressive policies against compressed reward representations of high-dimensional human objectives. Under this view, reward hacking arises from the interaction of objective compression, optimization amplification, and evaluator--policy co-adaptation. This perspective unifies empirical phenomena across RLHF, RLAIF, and RLVR regimes, and explains how local shortcut learning can generalize into broader forms of misalignment, including deception and strategic manipulation of oversight mechanisms. We further organize detection and mitigation strategies according to how they intervene on compression, amplification, or co-adaptation dynamics. By framing reward hacking as a structural instability of proxy-based alignment under scale, we highlight open challenges in scalable oversight, multimodal grounding, and agentic autonomy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大模型时代的奖励黑客：机制、涌现性失配与挑战
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）及相关对齐范式已成为引导大语言模型（LLM）和多模态大语言模型（MLLM）符合人类偏好行为的核心方法。然而，这些方法引入了系统性脆弱性：奖励黑客，即模型利用习得奖励信号中的缺陷，在不满足真实任务意图的情况下最大化代理目标。随着模型规模扩大和优化强度提升，此类利用行为表现为冗长偏好、迎合倾向、幻觉合理化、基准过拟合，以及在多模态场景下的感知-推理解耦和评估器操纵。近期证据进一步表明，看似良性的捷径行为可能泛化为更广泛的失配形式，包括欺骗和对监督机制的策略性博弈。本文提出“代理压缩假说”（PCH）作为理解奖励黑客的统一框架，将奖励黑客形式化为针对高维人类目标的压缩奖励表示优化表达性策略时涌现的结果。该视角认为奖励黑客源于目标压缩、优化放大和评估器-策略协同适应的相互作用，统一了RLHF、RLAIF和RLVR领域的实证现象，并解释了局部捷径学习如何泛化为包括欺骗和监督机制策略性操纵在内的广泛失配形式。我们进一步根据干预压缩、放大或协同适应动态的方式，系统归类检测与缓解策略。通过将奖励黑客定义为规模化时代基于代理的对齐机制的结构性不稳定问题，本文强调了可扩展监督、多模态 grounding 和智能体自主性等开放挑战。

The authors propose the Proxy Compression Hypothesis as a unifying framework, formalizing reward hacking as an emergent result of optimizing expressive policies against compressed reward representations, which explains phenomena across RLHF, RLAIF, and RLVR regimes. Experimental evidence highlights that such exploitation manifests as various shortcut behaviors, including benchmark overfitting and evaluator manipulation, with detection and mitigation strategies organized around intervening in compression, amplification, or co-adaptation dynamics.

Enhancing Reinforcement Learning for Radiology Report Generation with Evidence-aware Rewards and Self-correcting Preference Learning
Authors: Qin Zhou, Guoyan Liang, Qianyi Yang, Jingyuan Chen, Sai Wu, Chang Yao, Zhe Wang
First: 2026-04-15T08:08:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T08:08:06+00:00
Comments: 13 pages,4 figures, ACL2026-main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent reinforcement learning (RL) approaches have advanced radiology report generation (RRG), yet two core limitations persist: (1) report-level rewards offer limited evidence-grounded guidance for clinical faithfulness; and (2) current methods lack an explicit self-improving mechanism to align with clinical preference. We introduce clinically aligned Evidence-aware Self-Correcting Reinforcement Learning (ESC-RL), comprising two key components. First, a Group-wise Evidence-aware Alignment Reward (GEAR) delivers group-wise, evidence-aware feedback. GEAR reinforces consistent grounding for true positives, recovers missed findings for false negatives, and suppresses unsupported content for false positives. Second, a Self-correcting Preference Learning (SPL) strategy automatically constructs a reliable, disease-aware preference dataset from multiple noisy observations and leverages an LLM to synthesize refined reports without human supervision. ESC-RL promotes clinically faithful, disease-aligned reward and supports continual self-improvement during training. Extensive experiments on two public chest X-ray datasets demonstrate consistent gains and state-of-the-art performance.

Robust Adversarial Policy Optimization Under Dynamics Uncertainty
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T07:15:04+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) policies often fail under dynamics that differ from training, a gap not fully addressed by domain randomization or existing adversarial RL methods. Distributionally robust RL provides a formal remedy but still relies on surrogate adversaries to approximate intractable primal problems, leaving blind spots that potentially cause instability and over-conservatism. We propose a dual formulation that directly exposes the robustness-performance trade-off. At the trajectory level, a temperature parameter from the dual problem is approximated with an adversarial network, yielding efficient and stable worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound. At the model level, we employ Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles, focusing on more adverse environments to the current policy rather than uniform sampling. The two components act independently and complement each other: trajectory-level steering ensures robust rollouts, while model-level sampling provides policy-sensitive coverage of adverse dynamics. The resulting framework, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO) outperforms robust RL baselines, improving resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining dual tractability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态不确定性下的鲁棒对抗策略优化
强化学习策略常在训练环境之外的动态系统中失效，领域随机化或现有对抗性强化学习方法未能完全解决此问题。分布鲁棒强化学习提供了形式化解决方案，但仍依赖代理对抗器逼近难解的原问题，存在可能导致不稳定和过度保守的盲区。我们提出一种对偶形式，直接揭示鲁棒性与性能的权衡关系。在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络逼近对偶问题中的温度参数，在散度界内实现高效稳定的最坏情况推演。在模型层面，采用玻尔兹曼重加权方法处理动态系统集成，聚焦对当前策略更不利的环境而非均匀采样。两个组件独立运作且相互补充：轨迹层面引导确保鲁棒推演，模型层面采样提供对策略敏感的对抗动态覆盖。所提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化框架优于现有鲁棒强化学习基线，在保持对偶可解性的同时，提升了对不确定性的鲁棒性及对分布外动态的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of reinforcement learning policies to dynamics shifts not fully mitigated by existing robust RL methods, which often rely on surrogate adversaries leading to instability or over-conservatism. The proposed method, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO), introduces a dual formulation to explicitly manage the robustness-performance trade-off: at the trajectory level, an adversarial network approximates a temperature parameter for efficient worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound, while at the model level, Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles prioritizes sampling more adverse environments specific to the current policy. Experimental results demonstrate that RAPO outperforms robust RL baselines, enhancing resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining computational tractability.
本文针对强化学习策略在动态变化下的脆弱性问题，现有鲁棒强化学习方法常依赖代理对抗者，易导致不稳定或过度保守。提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化（RAPO）方法采用对偶公式显式权衡鲁棒性与性能：在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络近似温度参数以在发散边界内高效生成最坏情况推演；在模型层面，利用玻尔兹曼重加权对动态集成进行采样，优先关注对当前策略更不利的环境。实验结果表明，RAPO优于现有鲁棒强化学习基线，在保持计算可处理性的同时，提升了对不确定性的适应能力及对分布外动态的泛化性能。
WOMBET: World Model-based Experience Transfer for Robust and Sample-efficient Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-10T04:57:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T07:14:50+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures, 8th Annual Learning for Dynamics & Control Conference (L4DC)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) in robotics is often limited by the cost and risk of data collection, motivating experience transfer from a source task to a target task. Offline-to-online RL leverages prior data but typically assumes a given fixed dataset and does not address how to generate reliable data for transfer. We propose \textit{World Model-based Experience Transfer} (WOMBET), a framework that jointly generates and utilizes prior data. WOMBET learns a world model in the source task and generates offline data via uncertainty-penalized planning, followed by filtering trajectories with high return and low epistemic uncertainty. It then performs online fine-tuning in the target task using adaptive sampling between offline and online data, enabling a stable transition from prior-driven initialization to task-specific adaptation. We show that the uncertainty-penalized objective provides a lower bound on the true return and derive a finite-sample error decomposition capturing distribution mismatch and approximation error. Empirically, WOMBET improves sample efficiency and final performance over strong baselines on continuous control benchmarks, demonstrating the benefit of jointly optimizing data generation and transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WOMBET：基于世界模型的强化学习经验迁移框架，实现鲁棒与样本高效学习
机器人强化学习常受数据采集成本与风险限制，需通过源任务向目标任务迁移经验。离线-在线强化学习虽能利用先验数据，但通常假设固定数据集且未解决如何生成可靠迁移数据。本文提出《基于世界模型的经验迁移》框架，联合生成并利用先验数据：在源任务学习世界模型，通过不确定性惩罚规划生成离线数据，筛选高回报低认知不确定性的轨迹；在目标任务中采用离线-在线数据自适应采样进行在线微调，实现从先验驱动初始化到任务自适应学习的稳定过渡。理论证明不确定性惩罚目标函数为真实回报下界，推导出包含分布失配与近似误差的有限样本误差分解。实验表明，WOMBET在连续控制基准测试中显著提升样本效率与最终性能，验证了数据生成与迁移联合优化的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the high cost and risk of data collection in robotic reinforcement learning (RL), which drives the need for effective experience transfer from source to target tasks. The proposed method, WOMBET, jointly generates and utilizes prior data by learning a world model in the source task, generating offline data through uncertainty-penalized planning, and filtering trajectories based on high return and low epistemic uncertainty; it then fine-tunes online in the target task with adaptive sampling between offline and online data. Experimental results on continuous control benchmarks show that WOMBET improves sample efficiency and final performance over strong baselines, demonstrating the benefits of optimizing both data generation and transfer.
本文的动机是机器人强化学习中数据收集成本高、风险大，因此需要从源任务向目标任务进行有效的经验迁移。所提出的WOMBET方法通过联合生成和利用先验数据，在源任务中学习世界模型，通过不确定性惩罚规划生成离线数据，并筛选高回报、低认知不确定性的轨迹；随后在目标任务中通过离线与在线数据的自适应采样进行在线微调。在连续控制基准测试中的实验结果表明，WOMBET相比强基线方法提高了样本效率和最终性能，证明了优化数据生成与迁移的益处。
Failure Makes the Agent Stronger: Enhancing Accuracy through Structured Reflection for Reliable Tool Interactions
Authors: Junhao Su, Yuanliang Wan, Junwei Yang, Hengyu Shi, Tianyang Han, Junfeng Luo, Yurui Qiu
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-09-23T09:35:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:57:52+00:00
Comments: ACL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-augmented large language models (LLMs) are usually trained with supervised imitation or coarse-grained reinforcement learning that optimizes single tool calls. Current self-reflection practices rely on heuristic prompts or one-way reasoning: the model is urged to 'think more' instead of learning error diagnosis and repair. This is fragile in multi-turn interactions; after a failure the model often repeats the same mistake. We propose structured reflection, which turns the path from error to repair into an explicit, controllable, and trainable action. The agent produces a short yet precise reflection: it diagnoses the failure using evidence from the previous step and then proposes a correct, executable follow-up call. For training we combine DAPO and GSPO objectives with a reward scheme tailored to tool use, optimizing the stepwise strategy Reflect, then Call, then Final. To evaluate, we introduce Tool-Reflection-Bench, a lightweight benchmark that programmatically checks structural validity, executability, parameter correctness, and result consistency. Tasks are built as mini trajectories of erroneous call, reflection, and corrected call, with disjoint train and test splits. Experiments on BFCL v3 and Tool-Reflection-Bench show large gains in multi-turn tool-call success and error recovery, and a reduction of redundant calls. These results indicate that making reflection explicit and optimizing it directly improves the reliability of tool interaction and offers a reproducible path for agents to learn from failure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：失败使智能体更强大：通过结构化反思提升工具交互的可靠性精度
工具增强的大型语言模型通常通过监督模仿或优化单次工具调用的粗粒度强化学习进行训练。当前的自反思实践依赖启发式提示或单向推理：模型被催促'多思考'而非学习错误诊断与修复。这在多轮交互中十分脆弱；失败后模型常重复相同错误。我们提出结构化反思，将错误到修复的路径转化为显式、可控、可训练的动作。智能体生成简短而精确的反思：基于前一步证据诊断失败，随后提出正确且可执行的后续调用。训练中我们结合DAPO与GSPO目标及针对工具使用的奖励机制，优化'反思-调用-终判'的逐步策略。为评估性能，我们引入Tool-Reflection-Bench轻量基准，通过编程方式检查结构有效性、可执行性、参数正确性与结果一致性。任务构建为包含错误调用、反思、修正调用的微型轨迹，采用分离的训练测试集。在BFCL v3和Tool-Reflection-Bench上的实验显示，多轮工具调用成功率与错误恢复能力显著提升，冗余调用减少。结果表明：显式化反思并直接优化能提升工具交互可靠性，为智能体提供可复现的从失败中学习的路径。

Motivated by the fragility of current self-reflection methods in tool-augmented LLMs, which often lead to repeated errors after failures, this paper proposes structured reflection to explicitly diagnose and repair errors in multi-turn tool interactions. The method formulates reflection as a trainable action, combining DAPO and GSPO objectives with a tailored reward scheme to optimize a stepwise strategy of Reflect, Call, then Final. Experimental results on BFCL v3 and the introduced Tool-Reflection-Bench show significant improvements in multi-turn tool-call success, error recovery, and a reduction in redundant calls, demonstrating that explicit reflection training enhances reliability.
针对当前工具增强大语言模型的自反思方法在失败后易重复错误的脆弱性，本文提出结构化反思，将错误诊断与修复转化为明确、可训练的动作。该方法结合DAPO和GSPO目标及定制奖励方案，优化“反思、调用、最终”的逐步策略。在BFCL v3和自建的Tool-Reflection-Bench上的实验表明，多轮工具调用成功率显著提升，错误恢复能力增强，冗余调用减少，验证了显式反思训练能提高工具交互的可靠性。
Auto-FP: An Experimental Study of Automated Feature Preprocessing for Tabular Data
Authors: Danrui Qi, Jinglin Peng, Yongjun He, Jiannan Wang
First: 2023-10-04T02:46:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:43:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Classical machine learning models, such as linear models and tree-based models, are widely used in industry. These models are sensitive to data distribution, thus feature preprocessing, which transforms features from one distribution to another, is a crucial step to ensure good model quality. Manually constructing a feature preprocessing pipeline is challenging because data scientists need to make difficult decisions about which preprocessors to select and in which order to compose them. In this paper, we study how to automate feature preprocessing (Auto-FP) for tabular data. Due to the large search space, a brute-force solution is prohibitively expensive. To address this challenge, we interestingly observe that Auto-FP can be modelled as either a hyperparameter optimization (HPO) or a neural architecture search (NAS) problem. This observation enables us to extend a variety of HPO and NAS algorithms to solve the Auto-FP problem. We conduct a comprehensive evaluation and analysis of 15 algorithms on 45 public ML datasets. Overall, evolution-based algorithms show the leading average ranking. Surprisingly, the random search turns out to be a strong baseline. Many surrogate-model-based and bandit-based search algorithms, which achieve good performance for HPO and NAS, do not outperform random search for Auto-FP. We analyze the reasons for our findings and conduct a bottleneck analysis to identify the opportunities to improve these algorithms. Furthermore, we explore how to extend Auto-FP to support parameter search and compare two ways to achieve this goal. In the end, we evaluate Auto-FP in an AutoML context and discuss the limitations of popular AutoML tools. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study on automated feature preprocessing. We hope our work can inspire researchers to develop new algorithms tailored for Auto-FP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Auto-FP：面向表格数据的自动化特征预处理实验研究
经典机器学习模型（如线性模型与树模型）在工业界应用广泛。这类模型对数据分布敏感，因此特征预处理——即将特征从一种分布转换至另一种分布——成为保证模型质量的关键步骤。手动构建特征预处理流程具有挑战性，因为数据科学家需艰难决策预处理器的选择与组合顺序。本文研究如何对表格数据实现自动化特征预处理（Auto-FP）。由于搜索空间庞大，暴力求解方案成本过高。针对此挑战，我们有趣地发现Auto-FP可被建模为超参数优化问题或神经架构搜索问题。这一洞见使我们能扩展多种HPO与NAS算法以求解Auto-FP问题。我们在45个公开机器学习数据集上对15种算法进行了全面评估与分析。总体而言，基于进化的算法表现出领先的平均排名。令人惊讶的是，随机搜索成为强劲基线。许多在HPO和NAS中表现优异的基于代理模型和赌博机的搜索算法，在Auto-FP任务中并未超越随机搜索。我们分析了现象成因，并通过瓶颈分析指出改进这些算法的潜在方向。此外，我们探索了如何扩展Auto-FP以支持参数搜索，并比较了两种实现路径。最后，我们在AutoML场景中评估Auto-FP，并讨论了主流AutoML工具的局限性。据我们所知，这是首个针对自动化特征预处理的系统性研究。我们希望这项工作能启发研究者开发专门面向Auto-FP的新算法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of automating feature preprocessing (Auto-FP) for tabular data, motivated by the sensitivity of classical machine learning models to data distributions and the difficulty of manually designing preprocessing pipelines. The method models Auto-FP as either a hyperparameter optimization (HPO) or neural architecture search (NAS) problem, enabling the adaptation of various search algorithms to explore the large space of preprocessor selections and compositions. Experimental results from evaluating 15 algorithms on 45 datasets show that evolution-based algorithms perform best on average, while random search serves as a surprisingly strong baseline, outperforming many surrogate-model and bandit-based approaches; the study also includes bottleneck analysis and extensions for parameter search and AutoML integration.

RiskWebWorld: A Realistic Interactive Benchmark for GUI Agents in E-commerce Risk Management
Authors: Renqi Chen, Zeyin Tao, Jianming Guo, Jing Wang, Zezhou Xu, Jingzhe Zhu, Qingqing Sun, Tianyi Zhang, Shuai Chen
First: 2026-04-15T06:27:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:27:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents show strong capabilities for automating web tasks, but existing interactive benchmarks primarily target benign, predictable consumer environments. Their effectiveness in high-stakes, investigative domains such as authentic e-commerce risk management remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we present RiskWebWorld, the first highly realistic interactive benchmark for evaluating GUI agents in e-commerce risk management. RiskWebWorld features 1,513 tasks sourced from production risk-control pipelines across 8 core domains, and captures the authentic challenges of risk operations on uncooperative websites, partially environmental hijackments. To support scalable evaluation and agentic reinforcement learning (RL), we further build a Gymnasium-compliant infrastructure that decouples policy planning from environment mechanics. Our evaluation across diverse models reveals a dramatic capability gap: top-tier generalist models achieve 49.1% success, while specialized open-weights GUI models lag at near-total failure. This highlights that foundation model scale currently matters more than zero-shot interface grounding in long-horizon professional tasks. We also demonstrate the viability of our infrastructure through agentic RL, which improves open-source models by 16.2%. These results position RiskWebWorld as a practical testbed for developing robust digital workers.

本文的动机在于需要评估图形用户界面（GUI）代理在高风险、真实的电子商务风险管理场景中的表现，而现有基准主要针对良性的消费者任务。方法上提出了RiskWebWorld，这是一个包含来自八个领域生产流程的1,513个任务的基准，模拟了如不合作网站等挑战，并构建了兼容Gymnasium的基础设施以支持可扩展评估和代理强化学习。主要实验结果显示显著的能力差距：顶级通用模型达到49.1%的成功率，而专用GUI模型几乎完全失败，表明基础模型规模比零样本界面接地更重要；代理强化学习将开源模型性能提升了16.2%，证明了该基准在开发鲁棒数字工作者方面的实用性。
Representation over Routing: Overcoming Surrogate Hacking in Multi-Timescale PPO
Authors: Jing Sun
First: 2026-04-15T06:03:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:03:07+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Temporal credit assignment in reinforcement learning has long been a central challenge. Inspired by the multi-timescale encoding of the dopamine system in neurobiology, recent research has sought to introduce multiple discount factors into Actor-Critic architectures, such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), to balance short-term responses with long-term planning. However, this paper reveals that blindly fusing multi-timescale signals in complex delayed-reward tasks can lead to severe algorithmic pathologies. We systematically demonstrate that exposing a temporal attention routing mechanism to policy gradients results in surrogate objective hacking, while adopting gradient-free uncertainty weighting triggers irreversible myopic degeneration, a phenomenon we term the Paradox of Temporal Uncertainty. To address these issues, we propose a Target Decoupling architecture: on the Critic side, we retain multi-timescale predictions to enforce auxiliary representation learning, while on the Actor side, we strictly isolate short-term signals and update the policy based solely on long-term advantages. Rigorous empirical evaluations across multiple independent random seeds in the LunarLander-v2 environment demonstrate that our proposed architecture achieves statistically significant performance improvements. Without relying on hyperparameter hacking, it consistently surpasses the ''Environment Solved'' threshold with minimal variance, completely eliminates policy collapse, and escapes the hovering local optima that trap single-timescale baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：表征优于路由：克服多时间尺度PPO中的代理目标破解
强化学习中的时序信用分配长期是核心挑战。受神经生物学中多巴胺系统多时间尺度编码的启发，近期研究尝试在Actor-Critic架构（如近端策略优化）中引入多个折扣因子，以平衡短期响应与长期规划。然而，本文揭示在复杂延迟奖励任务中盲目融合多时间尺度信号会导致严重的算法病理现象。我们系统论证：将时序注意力路由机制暴露给策略梯度会引发代理目标破解，而采用无梯度不确定性加权则会触发不可逆的短视退化——这一现象被我们称为“时序不确定性悖论”。为解决这些问题，我们提出目标解耦架构：在Critic侧保留多时间尺度预测以强化辅助表征学习，在Actor侧则严格隔离短期信号，仅基于长期优势更新策略。在LunarLander-v2环境中通过多个独立随机种子的严格实证评估表明，所提架构实现了统计显著的性能提升：无需依赖超参数调试即能以最小方差持续超越“环境求解”阈值，完全消除策略崩溃，并摆脱困住单时间尺度基线的悬停局部最优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of temporal credit assignment in reinforcement learning and inspired by multi-timescale dopamine encoding, this paper investigates pathologies in multi-timescale PPO for delayed-reward tasks. Experimental results in the LunarLander-v2 environment show the architecture achieves statistically significant performance improvements, consistently surpasses the solved threshold with minimal variance, eliminates policy collapse, and escapes local optima that trap single-timescale baselines.

Feedback-Driven Tool-Use Improvements in Large Language Models via Automated Build Environments
Authors: Junjie Ye, Changhao Jiang, Zhengyin Du, Yufei Xu, Xuesong Yao, Zhiheng Xi, Xiaoran Fan, Qi Zhang, Tao Gui, Xuanjing Huang, Jiecao Chen
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-08-12T09:45:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T06:01:13+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Effective tool use is essential for large language models (LLMs) to interact with their environment. However, progress is limited by the lack of efficient reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks specifically designed for tool use, due to challenges in constructing stable training environments and designing verifiable reward mechanisms. To address this, we propose an automated environment construction pipeline, incorporating scenario decomposition, document generation, function integration, complexity scaling, and localized deployment. This enables the creation of high-quality training environments that provide detailed and measurable feedback without relying on external tools. Additionally, we introduce a verifiable reward mechanism that evaluates both the precision of tool use and the completeness of task execution. When combined with trajectory data collected from the constructed environments, this mechanism integrates seamlessly with standard RL algorithms to facilitate feedback-driven model training. Experiments on LLMs of varying scales demonstrate that our approach significantly enhances the models' tool-use performance without degrading their general capabilities. Our analysis suggests that these gains result from improved context understanding and reasoning, driven by updates to the lower-layer MLP parameters in models. Code and data are available at https://github.com/bytedance/FTRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自动化构建环境的反馈驱动大语言模型工具使用能力提升
大语言模型（LLM）有效使用工具是其与环境交互的关键。然而，由于构建稳定训练环境和设计可验证奖励机制的挑战，专门针对工具使用的强化学习（RL）框架发展受限。为此，我们提出自动化环境构建流程，包含场景分解、文档生成、功能集成、复杂度调节和本地化部署，能够创建无需依赖外部工具即可提供详细可量化反馈的高质量训练环境。同时，我们引入可验证奖励机制，评估工具使用的精确性和任务执行的完整性。该机制与构建环境中收集的轨迹数据相结合，可无缝集成标准RL算法以支持反馈驱动的模型训练。不同规模LLM的实验表明，该方法显著提升模型工具使用性能且不损害通用能力。分析指出，这些提升源于模型底层MLP参数更新驱动的上下文理解与推理能力改进。代码与数据详见 https://github.com/bytedance/FTRL。

This paper addresses the challenge of improving tool-use capabilities in large language models (LLMs) by developing a specialized reinforcement learning framework, motivated by the lack of efficient training environments and verifiable reward mechanisms. 本文针对大语言模型工具使用能力提升的挑战，提出了一种专门的强化学习框架，其动机在于缺乏高效的训练环境和可验证的奖励机制。方法通过场景分解、文档生成和本地化部署等自动化流程构建高质量训练环境，并引入可验证的奖励机制来评估工具使用的精确性和任务完整性。在不同规模的大语言模型上的实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了工具使用性能，且未损害通用能力，分析显示这些增益源于模型底层MLP参数更新带来的上下文理解和推理能力改进。
Chain of Uncertain Rewards with Large Language Models for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shentong Mo
First: 2026-04-15T05:44:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective reward functions is a cornerstone of reinforcement learning (RL), yet it remains a challenging and labor-intensive process due to the inefficiencies and inconsistencies inherent in traditional methods. Existing methods often rely on extensive manual design and evaluation steps, which are prone to redundancy and overlook local uncertainties at intermediate decision points. To address these challenges, we propose the Chain of Uncertain Rewards (CoUR), a novel framework that integrates large language models (LLMs) to streamline reward function design and evaluation in RL environments. Specifically, our CoUR introduces code uncertainty quantification with a similarity selection mechanism that combines textual and semantic analyses to identify and reuse the most relevant reward function components. By reducing redundant evaluations and leveraging Bayesian optimization on decoupled reward terms, CoUR enables a more efficient and robust search for optimal reward feedback. We comprehensively evaluate CoUR across nine original environments from IsaacGym and all 20 tasks from the Bidexterous Manipulation benchmark. The experimental results demonstrate that CoUR not only achieves better performance but also significantly lowers the cost of reward evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的不确定性奖励链强化学习方法
设计有效的奖励函数是强化学习的核心挑战，但传统方法效率低下且存在不一致性，导致该过程既复杂又耗时。现有方法通常依赖大量人工设计与评估步骤，容易产生冗余并忽略中间决策点的局部不确定性。为解决这些问题，我们提出了不确定性奖励链（CoUR）这一创新框架，该框架集成大语言模型以优化强化学习环境中的奖励函数设计与评估流程。具体而言，CoUR通过代码不确定性量化与相似性选择机制，结合文本与语义分析来识别并复用最相关的奖励函数组件。通过减少冗余评估并对解耦的奖励项进行贝叶斯优化，CoUR实现了更高效、更鲁棒的最优奖励反馈搜索。我们在IsaacGym的九个原始环境及双手灵巧操作基准的全部20项任务中进行了全面评估。实验结果表明，CoUR不仅取得了更优性能，还显著降低了奖励评估成本。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the inefficiencies and inconsistencies in traditional reinforcement learning reward function design, which is often manual and overlooks local uncertainties. The proposed method, Chain of Uncertain Rewards (CoUR), integrates large language models to streamline the process by quantifying code uncertainty and using a similarity selection mechanism that combines textual and semantic analysis to reuse relevant reward components, thereby reducing redundant evaluations and employing Bayesian optimization for efficient search. Experimental results across nine IsaacGym environments and 20 Bidexterous Manipulation tasks show that CoUR achieves better performance while significantly lowering evaluation costs.
本研究的动机在于传统强化学习奖励函数设计存在效率低下和不一致的问题，通常依赖手动设计且忽略局部不确定性。提出的方法“不确定性奖励链”通过集成大语言模型来简化流程，利用代码不确定性量化和结合文本与语义分析的相似性选择机制来重用相关奖励组件，从而减少冗余评估，并采用贝叶斯优化进行高效搜索。在九个IsaacGym环境和20个双手操作基准任务上的实验结果表明，该方法不仅性能更优，还显著降低了奖励评估成本。
Towards Scalable Lightweight GUI Agents via Multi-role Orchestration
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Junjie Zheng, Leyang Yang, Sheng Zhou, Xiaoxuan Tang, Zhouhua Fang, Zhiwei Liu, Dajun Chen, Yong Li, Jiajun Bu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-15T05:23:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T05:23:04+00:00
Comments: Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents powered by Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) enable digital automation on end-user devices. While scaling both parameters and data has yielded substantial gains, advanced methods still suffer from prohibitive deployment costs on resource-constrained devices. When facing complex in-the-wild scenarios, lightweight GUI agents are bottlenecked by limited capacity and poor task scalability under end-to-end episodic learning, impeding adaptation to multi-agent systems (MAS), while training multiple skill-specific experts remains costly. Can we strike an effective trade-off in this cost-scalability dilemma, enabling lightweight MLLMs to participate in realistic GUI workflows? To address these challenges, we propose the LAMO framework, which endows a lightweight MLLM with GUI-specific knowledge and task scalability, allowing multi-role orchestration to expand its capability boundary for GUI automation. LAMO combines role-oriented data synthesis with a two-stage training recipe: (i) supervised fine-tuning with Perplexity-Weighted Cross-Entropy optimization for knowledge distillation and visual perception enhancement, and (ii) reinforcement learning for role-oriented cooperative exploration. With LAMO, we develop a task-scalable native GUI agent, LAMO-3B, supporting monolithic execution and MAS-style orchestration. When paired with advanced planners as a plug-and-play policy executor, LAMO-3B can continuously benefit from planner advances, enabling a higher performance ceiling. Extensive static and online evaluations validate the effectiveness of our design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过多角色编排实现可扩展的轻量级GUI智能体
基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的自主图形用户界面（GUI）智能体实现了终端设备上的数字自动化。尽管扩大参数和数据规模带来了显著收益，但先进方法在资源受限设备上仍面临高昂的部署成本。面对复杂的实际场景，轻量级GUI智能体在端到端情景学习下受限于能力不足和任务可扩展性差，难以适应多智能体系统（MAS），而训练多个专用技能专家成本依然高昂。我们能否在成本与可扩展性的困境中实现有效权衡，使轻量级MLLM能够参与实际GUI工作流？为解决这些挑战，我们提出LAMO框架，该框架赋予轻量级MLLM以GUI专用知识与任务可扩展性，通过多角色编排拓展其GUI自动化的能力边界。LAMO结合面向角色的数据合成与两阶段训练方案：（i）采用困惑度加权交叉熵优化的监督微调，实现知识蒸馏与视觉感知增强；（ii）强化学习驱动的面向角色协同探索。基于LAMO，我们开发了任务可扩展的原生GUI智能体LAMO-3B，支持单体执行与MAS式编排。当与先进规划器作为即插即用策略执行器配合使用时，LAMO-3B可持续受益于规划器进展，实现更高的性能上限。大量静态与在线评估验证了我们设计的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enable lightweight multimodal large language models (MLLMs) to perform complex GUI automation on resource-constrained devices, addressing the cost-scalability dilemma where existing methods are either too heavy or lack task adaptability. The method introduces the LAMO framework, which uses role-oriented data synthesis and a two-stage training approach: supervised fine-tuning with Perplexity-Weighted Cross-Entropy for knowledge distillation and visual enhancement, followed by reinforcement learning for cooperative role exploration. Main experimental results show that LAMO-3B, a 3-billion parameter agent developed with this framework, effectively supports both monolithic execution and multi-agent orchestration in GUI tasks, with extensive evaluations confirming its performance and scalability when paired with advanced planners.
该研究的动机是让轻量级多模态大语言模型（MLLM）能在资源受限的设备上执行复杂的图形用户界面（GUI）自动化任务，解决现有方法部署成本高或任务可扩展性不足的困境。方法上提出了LAMO框架，通过角色导向的数据合成和两阶段训练方案：首先使用基于困惑度加权的交叉熵优化进行监督微调，以蒸馏知识并增强视觉感知，然后采用强化学习进行角色协作探索。主要实验结果表明，基于此框架开发的3B参数代理LAMO-3B能有效支持单体执行和多智能体协同的GUI任务，大量静态和在线评估验证了其与高级规划器结合时的性能和可扩展性优势。
Bridging MARL to SARL: An Order-Independent Multi-Agent Transformer via Latent Consensus
Authors: Zijian Zhao, Jing Gao, Sen Li
First: 2026-04-15T04:52:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:52:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) is widely used to address large joint observation and action spaces by decomposing a centralized control problem into multiple interacting agents. However, such decomposition often introduces additional challenges, including non-stationarity, unstable training, weak coordination, and limited theoretical guarantees. In this paper, we propose the Consensus Multi-Agent Transformer (CMAT), a centralized framework that bridges cooperative MARL to a hierarchical single-agent reinforcement learning (SARL) formulation. CMAT treats all agents as a unified entity and employs a Transformer encoder to process the large joint observation space. To handle the extensive joint action space, we introduce a hierarchical decision-making mechanism in which a Transformer decoder autoregressively generates a high-level consensus vector, simulating the process by which agents reach agreement on their strategies in latent space. Conditioned on this consensus, all agents generate their actions simultaneously, enabling order-independent joint decision making and avoiding the sensitivity to action-generation order in conventional Multi-Agent Transformers (MAT). This factorization allows the joint policy to be optimized using single-agent PPO while preserving expressive coordination through the latent consensus. To evaluate the proposed method, we conduct experiments on benchmark tasks from StarCraft II, Multi-Agent MuJoCo, and Google Research Football. The results show that CMAT achieves superior performance over recent centralized solutions, sequential MARL methods, and conventional MARL baselines. The code for this paper is available at:https://github.com/RS2002/CMAT .
中文标题/摘要
标题：从多智能体强化学习到单智能体强化学习的桥梁：基于潜在共识的序无关多智能体Transformer
协作式多智能体强化学习（MARL）通过将集中控制问题分解为多个交互智能体，广泛用于处理庞大的联合观测与动作空间。然而，这种分解常带来额外挑战，包括非平稳性、训练不稳定、协调能力弱及理论保证有限。本文提出共识多智能体Transformer（CMAT），这是一个将协作式MARL桥接至分层单智能体强化学习（SARL）的集中式框架。CMAT将所有智能体视为统一实体，采用Transformer编码器处理大规模联合观测空间。为应对庞大的联合动作空间，我们引入分层决策机制：Transformer解码器自回归生成高层共识向量，模拟智能体在潜在空间就策略达成一致的过程。基于该共识，所有智能体同步生成动作，实现序无关的联合决策，避免了传统多智能体Transformer（MAT）对动作生成顺序的敏感性。这种分解使得联合策略可通过单智能体PPO进行优化，同时通过潜在共识保持丰富的协调能力。为评估所提方法，我们在星际争霸II、多智能体MuJoCo和谷歌研究足球的基准任务上开展实验。结果表明，CMAT在性能上优于近期集中式解决方案、顺序式MARL方法及传统MARL基线。本文代码已开源：https://github.com/RS2002/CMAT。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses challenges in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), such as non-stationarity and weak coordination, by proposing the Consensus Multi-Agent Transformer (CMAT), which bridges MARL to a hierarchical single-agent reinforcement learning formulation. The method employs a Transformer encoder for joint observations and a Transformer decoder to autoregressively generate a high-level consensus vector in latent space, enabling order-independent joint action generation conditioned on this consensus, optimized via single-agent PPO. Experimental results on StarCraft II, Multi-Agent MuJoCo, and Google Research Football benchmarks demonstrate that CMAT outperforms recent centralized solutions, sequential MARL methods, and conventional MARL baselines.
本文针对合作式多智能体强化学习中的非平稳性、弱协调性等挑战，提出了共识多智能体变换器（CMAT），将MARL桥接至分层单智能体强化学习框架。该方法使用变换器编码器处理联合观测，并通过变换器解码器在潜在空间中自回归生成高层共识向量，基于此共识实现顺序无关的联合动作生成，采用单智能体PPO进行优化。在星际争霸II、多智能体MuJoCo和谷歌研究足球等基准任务上的实验结果表明，CMAT优于近期集中式解决方案、顺序MARL方法及传统MARL基线。
Data-Efficient RLVR via Off-Policy Influence Guidance
Authors: Erle Zhu, Dazhi Jiang, Yuan Wang, Xujun Li, Jiale Cheng, Yuxian Gu, Yilin Niu, Aohan Zeng, Jie Tang, Minlie Huang, Hongning Wang
First: 2025-10-30T13:40:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:43:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Data selection is a critical aspect of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). Current data selection methods are largely heuristic-based, lacking theoretical guarantees and generalizability. This work proposes a theoretically-grounded approach using influence functions to estimate the contribution of each data point to the learning objective. To overcome the prohibitive computational cost of policy rollouts required for online influence estimation, we introduce an off-policy influence estimation method that efficiently approximates data influence using pre-collected offline trajectories. Furthermore, to manage the high-dimensional gradients of LLMs, we employ sparse random projection to reduce dimensionality and improve storage and computation efficiency. Leveraging these techniques, we develop \textbf{C}urriculum \textbf{R}L with \textbf{O}ff-\textbf{P}olicy \text{I}nfluence guidance (\textbf{CROPI}), a multi-stage RL framework that iteratively selects the most influential data for the current policy. Experiments on models up to 7B parameters demonstrate that CROPI significantly accelerates training. On a 1.5B model, it achieves a 2.66x step-level acceleration while using only 10\% of the data per stage compared to full-dataset training. Our results highlight the substantial potential of influence-based data selection for efficient RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于离线策略影响引导的数据高效RLVR方法
数据选择是强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）提升大语言模型（LLMs）推理能力的关键环节。当前数据选择方法多基于启发式策略，缺乏理论保证与泛化能力。本研究提出一种理论驱动的方法，利用影响函数估计每个数据点对学习目标的贡献。为克服在线影响估计所需策略展开的过高计算成本，我们引入离线策略影响估计方法，利用预收集的离线轨迹高效近似数据影响力。此外，为处理LLMs的高维梯度，我们采用稀疏随机投影降低维度并提升存储与计算效率。基于这些技术，我们开发了\textbf{C}urriculum \textbf{R}L with \textbf{O}ff-\textbf{P}olicy \text{I}nfluence guidance（\textbf{CROPI}），这是一个多阶段强化学习框架，能迭代选择对当前策略最具影响力的数据。在高达70亿参数的模型实验中，CROPI显著加速训练过程：在15亿参数模型上，相比全数据集训练，每阶段仅使用10%数据即可实现2.66倍的步骤级加速。我们的研究结果凸显了基于影响力的数据选择在高效RLVR中的巨大潜力。

The paper addresses the inefficiency of heuristic data selection in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for large language models by proposing a theoretically-grounded method that uses influence functions to estimate each data point's contribution to the learning objective. To overcome computational bottlenecks, it introduces an off-policy influence estimation technique that approximates data influence using pre-collected offline trajectories and employs sparse random projection to handle high-dimensional gradients efficiently. The resulting framework, CROPI, demonstrates significant acceleration in experiments, achieving a 2.66x step-level speedup on a 1.5B model while using only 10% of data per stage compared to full-dataset training, highlighting the potential of influence-based selection for data-efficient RLVR.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习中启发式数据选择效率低下的问题，提出了一种基于理论的方法，利用影响函数估计每个数据点对学习目标的贡献。为克服计算瓶颈，该方法引入了离策略影响估计技术，通过预收集的离线轨迹近似数据影响，并采用稀疏随机投影高效处理高维梯度。由此开发的CROPI框架在实验中显示出显著的加速效果，在15亿参数模型上实现了2.66倍的步骤级加速，且每阶段仅使用10%的数据，相比全数据集训练，证明了基于影响的数据选择在高效RLVR中的巨大潜力。
Outperforming Self-Attention Mechanisms in Solar Irradiance Forecasting via Physics-Guided Neural Networks
Authors: Mohammed Ezzaldin Babiker Abdullah, Rufaidah Abdallah Ibrahim Mohammed
First: 2026-04-15T04:17:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T04:17:20+00:00
Comments: This is a second version of a previously published paper. DOI: Https://doi.org/10.36227/techrxiv.176827103.31624241/v1
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate Global Horizontal Irradiance (GHI) forecasting is critical for grid stability, particularly in arid regions characterized by rapid aerosol fluctuations. While recent trends favor computationally expensive Transformer-based architectures, this paper challenges the prevailing "complexity-first" paradigm. We propose a lightweight, Physics-Informed Hybrid CNN-BiLSTM framework that prioritizes domain knowledge over architectural depth. The model integrates a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) for spatial feature extraction with a Bi-Directional LSTM for capturing temporal dependencies. Unlike standard data-driven approaches, our model is explicitly guided by a vector of 15 engineered features including Clear-Sky indices and Solar Zenith Angle - rather than relying solely on raw historical data. Hyperparameters are rigorously tuned using Bayesian Optimization to ensure global optimality. Experimental validation using NASA POWER data in Sudan demonstrates that our physics-guided approach achieves a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 19.53 W/m^2, significantly outperforming complex attention-based baselines (RMSE 30.64 W/m^2). These results confirm a "Complexity Paradox": in high-noise meteorological tasks, explicit physical constraints offer a more efficient and accurate alternative to self-attention mechanisms. The findings advocate for a shift towards hybrid, physics-aware AI for real-time renewable energy management.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于物理引导神经网络在太阳辐照度预测中超越自注意力机制
全球水平辐照度（GHI）的精确预测对电网稳定性至关重要，尤其在气溶胶快速波动的干旱地区。尽管当前趋势偏向计算成本高昂的Transformer架构，本文挑战了主流的“复杂度优先”范式。我们提出一种轻量级的物理信息混合CNN-BiLSTM框架，将领域知识置于架构深度之上。该模型结合卷积神经网络（CNN）进行空间特征提取，以及双向LSTM捕捉时间依赖性。与标准数据驱动方法不同，我们的模型明确受15个工程特征向量（包括晴空指数和太阳天顶角）引导，而非仅依赖原始历史数据。通过贝叶斯优化严格调整超参数以确保全局最优性。使用NASA POWER数据在苏丹的实验验证表明，我们的物理引导方法实现了19.53 W/m²的均方根误差（RMSE），显著优于复杂的基于注意力的基线模型（RMSE 30.64 W/m²）。这些结果证实了“复杂度悖论”：在高噪声气象任务中，显式物理约束为自注意力机制提供了更高效、更准确的替代方案。该发现倡导向混合型、物理感知的人工智能转变，以支持实时可再生能源管理。
Summary / 总结

The method combines a CNN for spatial features and a BiLSTM for temporal dependencies, explicitly guided by 15 engineered physical features like Clear-Sky indices, with hyperparameters optimized via Bayesian Optimization. Experimental results using NASA POWER data from Sudan show the model achieves an RMSE of 19.53 W/m², significantly outperforming attention-based baselines (RMSE 30.64 W/m²), demonstrating that physics-guided approaches can be more efficient and accurate than self-attention mechanisms in noisy meteorological tasks.
本研究旨在解决干旱地区气溶胶快速变化下的太阳辐照度精准预测问题，挑战了当前依赖复杂Transformer模型的趋势，提出了一种轻量级的物理信息混合CNN-BiLSTM框架，强调融合领域知识而非模型深度。该方法结合CNN提取空间特征和BiLSTM捕捉时间依赖性，并明确引入了包括晴空指数和太阳天顶角在内的15个工程化物理特征进行指导，同时使用贝叶斯优化进行超参数调优。基于苏丹NASA POWER数据的实验验证表明，该模型的均方根误差为19.53 W/m²，显著优于基于注意力机制的基线模型（30.64 W/m²），结果证实了在高噪声气象任务中，显式的物理约束比自注意力机制更高效、准确。
In-Context Autonomous Network Incident Response: An End-to-End Large Language Model Agent Approach
Authors: Yiran Gao, Kim Hammar, Tao Li
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-02-13T18:09:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:45:06+00:00
Comments: 2026 AAAI Summer Symposium on Human-Aware AI Agents for the Cyber Battlefield
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rapidly evolving cyberattacks demand incident response systems that can autonomously learn and adapt to changing threats. Prior work has extensively explored the reinforcement learning approach, which involves learning response strategies through extensive simulation of the incident. While this approach can be effective, it requires handcrafted modeling of the simulator and suppresses useful semantics from raw system logs and alerts. To address these limitations, we propose to leverage large language models' (LLM) pre-trained security knowledge and in-context learning to create an end-to-end agentic solution for incident response planning. Specifically, our agent integrates four functionalities, perception, reasoning, planning, and action, into one lightweight LLM (14b model). Through fine-tuning and chain-of-thought reasoning, our LLM agent is capable of processing system logs and inferring the underlying network state (perception), updating its conjecture of attack models (reasoning), simulating consequences under different response strategies (planning), and generating an effective response (action). By comparing LLM-simulated outcomes with actual observations, the LLM agent repeatedly refines its attack conjecture and corresponding response, thereby demonstrating in-context adaptation. Our agentic approach is free of modeling and can run on commodity hardware. When evaluated on incident logs reported in the literature, our agent achieves recovery up to 23% faster than those of frontier LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：情境自适网络事件响应：一种端到端大语言模型智能体方法
快速演变的网络攻击需要能够自主学习并适应动态威胁的事件响应系统。先前研究已广泛探索强化学习方法，该方法通过大量事件模拟学习响应策略。虽然有效，但需人工构建模拟器模型，且抑制了原始系统日志与告警中的有效语义。为突破这些局限，我们提出利用大语言模型（LLM）预训练的安全知识与情境学习能力，构建端到端的智能体化事件响应规划方案。具体而言，我们的智能体将感知、推理、规划、执行四项功能集成于一个轻量化LLM（140亿参数模型）中。通过微调与思维链推理，该LLM智能体能够处理系统日志并推断底层网络状态（感知）、更新攻击模型假设（推理）、模拟不同响应策略的后果（规划）、生成有效响应方案（执行）。通过对比LLM模拟结果与实际观测，智能体持续优化攻击假设与对应响应，实现情境自适应。我们的智能体方法无需建模，可在商用硬件上运行。基于文献记载的事件日志评估表明，本智能体的恢复速度比前沿LLM方案最高提升23%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for autonomous incident response systems that can adapt to evolving cyberattacks without the handcrafted modeling and semantic suppression inherent in prior reinforcement learning approaches, this paper proposes an end-to-end agent using a lightweight large language model (LLM). The method integrates perception, reasoning, planning, and action into a single 14B-parameter LLM, which is fine-tuned and employs chain-of-thought reasoning to process system logs, infer network states, update attack conjectures, simulate response strategies, and generate actions, enabling in-context adaptation by comparing simulated outcomes with observations. The main experimental results show that this agentic approach, which requires no explicit modeling and runs on commodity hardware, achieves recovery up to 23% faster than frontier LLMs when evaluated on literature-reported incident logs.
本文的动机是应对快速演变的网络攻击，需要能够自主适应威胁的事件响应系统，而先前基于强化学习的方法需要手工建模模拟器且抑制了原始日志中的有用语义。为此，论文提出一种端到端的智能体方法，利用轻量级大语言模型（LLM），通过微调和思维链推理，将感知、推理、规划和行动四个功能集成到一个14B参数的LLM中，使其能处理系统日志、推断网络状态、更新攻击假设、模拟响应策略并生成行动，通过比较模拟结果与实际观察实现上下文自适应。主要实验结果表明，该智能体方法无需显式建模，可在商用硬件上运行，在文献报告的事件日志评估中，其恢复速度比前沿大语言模型快达23%。
Minimax Optimality and Spectral Routing for Majority-Vote Ensembles under Markov Dependence
Authors: Ibne Farabi Shihab, Sanjeda Akter, Anuj Sharma
First: 2026-04-15T02:32:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:32:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Majority-vote ensembles achieve variance reduction by averaging over diverse, approximately independent base learners. When training data exhibits Markov dependence, as in time-series forecasting, reinforcement learning (RL) replay buffers, and spatial grids, this classical guarantee degrades in ways that existing theory does not fully quantify. We provide a minimax characterization of this phenomenon for discrete classification in a fixed-dimensional Markov setting, together with an adaptive algorithm that matches the rate on a graph-regular subclass. We first establish an information-theoretic lower bound for stationary, reversible, geometrically ergodic chains in fixed ambient dimension, showing that no measurable estimator can achieve excess classification risk better than $Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$. We then prove that, on the AR(1) witness subclass underlying the lower-bound construction, dependence-agnostic uniform bagging is provably suboptimal with excess risk bounded below by $Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$, exhibiting a $\sqrt{\Tmix}$ algorithmic gap. Finally, we propose \emph{adaptive spectral routing}, which partitions the training data via the empirical Fiedler eigenvector of a dependency graph and achieves the minimax rate $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$ up to a lower-order geometric cut term on a graph-regular subclass, without knowledge of $\Tmix$. Experiments on synthetic Markov chains, 2D spatial grids, the 128-dataset UCR archive, and Atari DQN ensembles validate the theoretical predictions. Consequences for deep RL target variance, scalability via Nyström approximation, and bounded non-stationarity are developed as supporting material in the appendix.

标题：马尔可夫依赖下多数投票集成的最小最大最优性与谱路由
多数投票集成通过平均多样化、近似独立的基础学习器实现方差缩减。当训练数据呈现马尔可夫依赖性时（如时间序列预测、强化学习回放缓冲区和空间网格场景），这一经典保证会以现有理论未能完全量化的方式退化。我们在固定维度的马尔可夫设定中，针对离散分类问题给出了该现象的最小最大刻画，并提出一种在图正则子类上达到该速率的自适应算法。首先，我们在固定环境维度下为平稳、可逆、几何遍历链建立了信息论下界，证明任何可测估计器的超额分类风险无法优于$Ω(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$。随后证明，在下界构造所基于的AR(1)见证子类上，依赖无关的均匀装袋法存在可证明的次优性，其超额风险下界为$Ω(\Tmix/\sqrt{n})$，呈现$\sqrt{\Tmix}$的算法间隙。最后提出\emph{自适应谱路由}方法，通过依赖图的经验费德勒特征向量划分训练数据，在图正则子类上以忽略低阶几何切割项的代价达到最小最大速率$\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{\Tmix/n})$，且无需预知$\Tmix$。在合成马尔可夫链、二维空间网格、128数据集UCR档案及Atari DQN集成上的实验验证了理论预测。附录中进一步推导了深度强化学习目标方差、通过Nyström近似的可扩展性及有界非平稳性等相关推论。

Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Augmented Step-Level Transitions for LLM Agents
Authors: Shuai Zhen, Yanhua Yu, Ruopei Guo, Nan Cheng, Yang Deng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-15T02:16:31+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in complex interactive decision-making tasks. However, existing LLM agents typically rely on increasingly long interaction histories, resulting in high computational cost and limited scalability. In this paper, we propose STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) framework that enables step-level learning by conditioning only on single-step transitions rather than full interaction histories. STEP-HRL structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress of overall task. By introducing a local progress module, it also iteratively and selectively summarizes interaction history within each subtask to produce a compact summary of local progress. Together, these components yield augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks consistently demonstrate that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baselines in terms of performance and generalization while reducing token usage. Our code is available at https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强步级转移的分层强化学习框架STEP-HRL用于大语言模型智能体
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在复杂交互决策任务中展现出强大能力，但现有方法通常依赖不断增长的交互历史，导致计算成本高昂且可扩展性受限。本文提出STEP-HRL分层强化学习框架，通过仅基于单步转移而非完整交互历史实现步级学习。该框架采用分层任务结构，利用已完成子任务表征整体任务的全局进展，并通过局部进展模块迭代选择性地汇总子任务内的交互历史，生成紧凑的局部进展摘要。这些组件共同为高层与低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试中，STEP-HRL在性能与泛化能力上均显著超越基线方法，同时大幅降低令牌使用量。代码已开源：https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost and limited scalability of large language model (LLM) agents that rely on long interaction histories, this paper introduces STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework designed to enable step-level learning by conditioning policies only on single-step transitions rather than full histories. The method structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress and employing a local progress module to iteratively summarize interaction history within subtasks, thereby producing augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies.
